"""
Arbore и®ёеҸҜиҜҒжЁЎеқ?- е®ҝдё»жңәзЎ¬д»¶жҢҮзә№дёҺж ЎйӘҢз ҒйӘҢиҜ?
Arbore License Utilities вҖ?host hardware fingerprint & validation code.

зЎ¬д»¶жҢҮзә№е§Ӣз»ҲдҪҝз”Ёе®ҝдё»жңәж ҮиҜҶпјҢдёҚдҪҝз”Ёе®№еҷ?IDгҖ?
еңЁе®№еҷЁеҢ–йғЁзҪІзҺҜеўғдёӯпјҢд»»дҪ•дҫқиө–е®№еҷЁиҮӘиә« ID дҪңдёәжҺҲжқғдҫқжҚ®зҡ„еҒҡжі•йғҪдёҚеӨҹзЁіе®ҡпј?
еӣ жӯӨжң¬жЁЎеқ—з»ҹдёҖйҖҡиҝҮе®ҝдё»жң?machine-id и®Ўз®—еҮәзЁіе®ҡзҡ„жҢҮзә№пјҢз”ЁдәҺз”ҹжҲҗе’Ңж ЎйӘҢи®ёеҸҜиҜҒгҖ?

Docker йғЁзҪІж—¶йңҖе°Ҷе®ҝдё»жңә /etc/machine-id жҢӮиҪҪеҲ°е®№еҷЁеҶ…пјҢдҫӢеҰӮпјҡ
  -v /etc/machine-id:/host/etc/machine-id:ro
жҲ–и®ҫзҪ®зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮ?HOST_MACHINE_ID_FILE жҢҮеҗ‘е®ҝдё»жң?machine-id ж–Үд»¶и·Ҝеҫ„гҖ?

HighвҖ‘level description (English):
- The license system always binds to the physical host identity instead of
  ephemeral container identifiers.
- A stable fingerprint is derived from the host `machine-id` using SHAвҖ?56,
  and then combined with company information and version prefix to generate
  an HMAC based validation code.
- This module is intentionally selfвҖ‘contained so that it can be reused by
  both the backend API and offline tooling used to issue licenses.
"""
import os
import json
import hmac
import hashlib
from typing import Optional, Tuple, Dict

# е®ҝдё»жң?machine-id еҖҷйҖүи·Ҝеҫ„пјҲдјҳе…ҲдҪҝз”ЁжҳҫејҸжҢӮиҪҪзҡ„е®ҝдё»жңәи·Ҝеҫ„пј?
HOST_MACHINE_ID_PATHS = [
    os.environ.get("HOST_MACHINE_ID_FILE"),  # жҳҫејҸжҢҮе®ҡе®ҝдё»жң?machine-id ж–Үд»¶и·Ҝеҫ„
    "/host/etc/machine-id",   # еёёи§Ғпјҡе®ҝдё»жңәжҢӮиҪҪеҲ°е®№еҷЁеҶ…
    "/etc/machine-id",        # зӣҙжҺҘи·‘еңЁе®ҝдё»жңәдёҠпјҢжҲ–е®ҝдё»жңәжҢӮиҪҪеҲ°жӯ?
]
LICENSE_FILENAME = "license.json"
# зүҲжң¬еҸ·еҸӘеҸ–дё»ж®өпјҢеҰ?1.1.0 -> 001
VERSION_MAJOR_PREFIX = "001"


def _get_project_root() -> str:
    env_root = os.environ.get('ARBORE_PROJECT_ROOT')
    if env_root:
        return env_root
    current_file = os.path.abspath(__file__)
    return os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(current_file)))


def get_host_hardware_fingerprint() -> Tuple[Optional[str], str]:
    """
    иҺ·еҸ–е®ҝдё»жңәзЎ¬д»¶жҢҮзә№пјҲеҸӘиҜ»е®ҝдё»жңәпјҢдёҚдҪҝз”Ёе®№еҷ?IDпјүгҖ?
    дҫқж¬Ўе°қиҜ•: HOST_MACHINE_ID_FILE -> /host/etc/machine-id -> /etc/machine-id
    иҝ”еӣһ (fingerprint_id, display_id)пјҢдҫӢеҰ?("abc123", "host-abc123")гҖ?
    иӢҘж— жі•иҺ·еҸ–еҲҷ fingerprint_id дё?NoneпјҢdisplay_id дёәй”ҷиҜҜжҸҸиҝ°гҖ?
    """
    for path in HOST_MACHINE_ID_PATHS:
        if not path or not os.path.isfile(path):
            continue
        try:
            with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                raw = f.read().strip()
            if not raw:
                continue
            # дҪҝз”Ё SHA256 еҫ—еҲ°еӣәе®ҡй•ҝеәҰжҢҮзә№пјҲдёҺж–ҮжЎЈдёҖиҮҙпјү
            fingerprint = hashlib.sha256(raw.encode()).hexdigest()
            display_id = f"host-{fingerprint[:16]}"
            return (fingerprint, display_id)
        except Exception:
            continue
    return (None, "host-unavailable (mount host /etc/machine-id)")


# дё?validation-code-generator.js дёӯзЎ¬зј–з ҒеҜҶй’ҘдёҖиҮҙпјҢжңӘй…ҚзҪ®зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸж—¶дҪҝз”Ё
DEFAULT_LICENSE_SECRET = "Arbore-License-Secret-Key-2024"

def get_license_secret() -> Optional[str]:
    """д»ҺзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸиҜ»еҸ?HMAC еҜҶй’ҘпјҲдёҺ validation-code-generator.js дёҖиҮҙпјүпјҢжңӘй…ҚзҪ®ж—¶дҪҝз”Ёй»ҳи®ӨеҜҶй’?""
    return os.environ.get("ARBORE_LICENSE_SECRET") or os.environ.get("LICENSE_HMAC_SECRET") or DEFAULT_LICENSE_SECRET


def _version_major(version: str) -> str:
    """зүҲжң¬еҸ·еҸ–дё»ж®өпјҢеҰӮ 1.1.0 / 001.0064 -> 001"""
    if not version:
        return VERSION_MAJOR_PREFIX
    part = version.split(".")[0].strip()
    if not part.isdigit():
        return VERSION_MAJOR_PREFIX
    return part.zfill(3)


def _version_major_for_hmac(version: str) -> str:
    """дё?validation-code-generator.js дёҖиҮҙпјҡдё»ж®өеҸ?3 дҪҚпјҲеҰ?001.0001->001пј?.1.0->001пјүпјҢдё?JS fallback еҜ№йҪҗ"""
    part = (version or "").split(".")[0].strip()
    if not part or not part.isdigit():
        return "001"
    return part.zfill(3)

def compute_validation_code(company_id: str, host_id: str, version: str, secret: str) -> str:
    """дё?validation-code-generator.js е®Ңе…ЁдёҖиҮҙпјҡHMAC-SHA256(companyId-hostId-versionMajor)пјҢеҸ–еү?6дҪҚеӨ§еҶҷгҖ?
    host_id дҪҝз”Ёз•Ңйқўеұ•зӨәзҡ„дё»жңәж ҮиҜҶпјҢеҰ?host-a5b50f0617a557b8пјҲдёҺ JS зҡ?hostId дёҖиҮҙпјүгҖ?""
    version_major = _version_major_for_hmac(version)
    message = f"{company_id}-{host_id}-{version_major}"
    digest = hmac.new(secret.encode(), message.encode(), hashlib.sha256).hexdigest().upper()
    return digest[:16]


def get_license_path() -> str:
    """license.json еӯҳж”ҫи·Ҝеҫ„пјҡйЎ№зӣ?config зӣ®еҪ•"""
    root = _get_project_root()
    config_dir = os.path.join(root, "config")
    os.makedirs(config_dir, exist_ok=True)
    return os.path.join(config_dir, LICENSE_FILENAME)


def load_license() -> Optional[Dict]:
    """иҜ»еҸ–еҪ“еүҚ license.jsonпјҢдёҚеӯҳеңЁжҲ–ж јејҸй”ҷиҜҜиҝ”еӣ?None"""
    path = get_license_path()
    if not os.path.isfile(path):
        return None
    try:
        with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            return json.load(f)
    except Exception:
        return None


def save_license(data: Dict) -> None:
    """еҶҷе…Ҙ license.json"""
    path = get_license_path()
    root = _get_project_root()
    config_dir = os.path.join(root, "config")
    os.makedirs(config_dir, exist_ok=True)
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(data, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)


def validate_license(version: str) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[str], Optional[Dict]]:
    """
    йӘҢиҜҒеҪ“еүҚи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжҳҜеҗҰжңүж•ҲгҖ?
    иҝ”еӣһ (is_valid, error_code, license_data)гҖ?
    error_code: LICENSE_NOT_FOUND, LICENSE_INVALID, HARDWARE_MISMATCH, VERSION_MISMATCH, SECRET_NOT_CONFIGURED
    """
    secret = get_license_secret()
    if not secret:
        return (False, "SECRET_NOT_CONFIGURED", None)

    license_data = load_license()
    if not license_data:
        return (False, "LICENSE_NOT_FOUND", None)

    company_id = license_data.get("companyId") or license_data.get("company_id")
    validation_code = license_data.get("validationCode") or license_data.get("validation_code")
    company_name = license_data.get("companyName") or license_data.get("company_name")
    if not company_id or not validation_code:
        return (False, "LICENSE_INVALID", None)

    host_fingerprint, display_id = get_host_hardware_fingerprint()
    if not host_fingerprint:
        return (False, "HARDWARE_MISMATCH", None)

    # дҪҝз”Ё display_idпјҲhost-xxxпјүдёҺ validation-code-generator.js зҡ?hostId дёҖиҮ?
    expected_code = compute_validation_code(company_id, display_id, version, secret)
    if not hmac.compare_digest(expected_code.upper(), str(validation_code).upper()):
        return (False, "LICENSE_INVALID", None)

    version_major = _version_major(version)
    # еҸҜйҖүпјҡж ЎйӘҢзүҲжң¬дё»ж®өдёҺзӯҫеҸ‘ж—¶дёҖиҮҙпјҲиӢ?license дёӯеӯҳдә?versionпј?
    stored_version = license_data.get("version") or license_data.get("versionInfo")
    if stored_version and _version_major(str(stored_version)) != version_major:
        return (False, "VERSION_MISMATCH", None)

    return (True, None, {
        "companyId": company_id,
        "companyName": company_name or "",
        "validationCode": validation_code,
        "versionInfo": version_major,
    })
"""
Arbore Webз®ЎзҗҶз•Ңйқў - еҗҺз«Ҝ API
Arbore Web Admin Backend API

жң¬жЁЎеқ—жҳҜ Arbore AI Host з®ЎзҗҶжҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°еңЁжңҚеҠЎз«Ҝзҡ„е”ҜдёҖе…ҘеҸЈпјҢиҙҹиҙЈеҜ№еӨ–жҡҙйңІдёҖз»?
з»ҹдёҖдё”е®үе…Ёзҡ„ HTTP APIпјҢз”ЁдәҺй©ұеҠЁеүҚз«Ҝз•Ңйқўеұ•зӨәе®№еҷЁзҠ¶жҖҒгҖҒзі»з»ҹиө„жәҗдҝЎжҒҜгҖ?
и®ёеҸҜиҜҒж ЎйӘҢз»“жһңд»ҘеҸҠиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎзј–жҺ’зӯүеҠҹиғҪгҖ?

This module serves as the central backend entrypoint for the Arbore AI Host
management console.  It exposes a wellвҖ‘structured and securityвҖ‘oriented HTTP
API that powers the frontend dashboard, including container status querying,
system resource inspection, license verification and customвҖ‘service orchestration.

и®ҫи®ЎиҰҒзӮ№пјҲдёӯж–Үпјү:
1. з»ҹдёҖе…ҘеҸЈпјҡжүҖжңүеүҚз«Ҝи°ғз”ЁеқҮйҖҡиҝҮжң?FastAPI еә”з”ЁиҝӣиЎҢпјҢдҫҝдәҺжқғйҷҗжҺ§еҲ¶е’Ңе®Ўи®ЎгҖ?
2. е®үе…Ёи®ҝй—® DockerпјҡйҖҡиҝҮжң¬ең° /var/run/docker.sock жҲ?HTTP API и®ҝй—® Dockerпј?
   е№¶еңЁеҲқе§ӢеҢ–ж—¶еҒҡеӨҡз§ҚеӨұиҙҘе…ңеә•пјҢйҒҝе…ҚејӮеёёеҜјиҮҙж•ҙдёӘжҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°дёҚеҸҜз”ЁгҖ?
3. иҪҜи‘—еҸӢеҘҪпјҡд»Јз Ғдёӯдҝқз•ҷдәҶзӣёеҜ№е®Ңж•ҙзҡ„дёҡеҠЎиҜӯд№үжіЁйҮҠпјҢдҫҝдәҺйҳ…иҜ»е’ҢеҗҺз»ӯз»ҙжҠӨпј?
   еҗҢж—¶еҸҜдҪңдёәиҪҜд»¶и‘—дҪңжқғзҷ»и®°ж—¶зҡ„жҠҖжңҜиҜҙжҳҺдҫқжҚ®гҖ?
4. еҸҜиҝҗз»ҙжҖ§пјҡAPI иҮӘиә«зҡ„иҝҗиЎҢж—Ҙеҝ—дјҡеҶҷе…ҘзӢ¬з«Ӣж–Үд»¶пјҢй…ҚеҗҲеүҚз«ҜгҖҢж—Ҙеҝ—жҹҘзңӢгҖҚйЎөйқўпјҢ
   иҝҗз»ҙдәәе‘ҳеҸҜд»ҘеңЁжөҸи§ҲеҷЁдёӯзӣҙжҺҘжҹҘзңӢеҗҺеҸ°иЎҢдёәгҖ?

Key design points (English):
1. Single entrypoint: every frontend interaction goes through this FastAPI
   application, which makes authorization, logging and future extensions easier.
2. Docker access hardening: the code tries multiple strategies to talk to the
   local Docker daemon, and degrades gracefully when the socket or permissions
   are not available, instead of failing the whole API.
3. Readability and IP support: extensive comments keep the intent of each
   subsystem clear (licensing, monitoring, service control), which is useful
   both for future maintainers and for software copyright registration.
4. Operability: the backend writes its own logs into an API specific log file;
   the frontend log viewer page can stream these logs to the browser so that
   operators can debug the platform without logging into the server.

жіЁж„Ҹпјҡжң¬ж–Үд»¶дёӯзҡ„жіЁйҮҠдёәи®ҫи®Ўе’Ңиҝҗз»ҙи§ЈйҮҠжҖ§еҶ…е®№пјҢдёҚдјҡеҸӮдёҺд»»дҪ•иҝҗиЎҢж—¶йҖ»иҫ‘пј?
д»…з”ЁдәҺеё®еҠ©зҗҶи§Јзі»з»ҹжһ¶жһ„гҖҒж»Ўи¶іж–ҮжЎЈдёҺд»Јз ҒиЎҢж•°иҰҒжұӮгҖ?
Note: all the comments in this file are descriptive only, they never change
the runtime behavior of the API and are safe to keep even in production.
"""
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, UploadFile, File, Form
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
import docker
import psutil
import os
import subprocess
import logging
import re
import shutil
import json
import hmac
from typing import List, Dict, Optional
from datetime import datetime
from pydantic import BaseModel
import threading
import time

from license_utils import (
    get_host_hardware_fingerprint,
    load_license,
    save_license,
    validate_license,
    get_license_secret,
    compute_validation_code,
)

# зүҲжң¬дҝЎжҒҜ
API_VERSION = "1.1.0"
BUILD_TIME = "2026-01-21T09:00:00Z"  # жһ„е»әж—¶жӣҙж–°жӯӨж—¶й—ҙжҲ?

app = FastAPI(title="Arbore Web Admin API", version=API_VERSION)

# й…ҚзҪ®CORS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],  # з”ҹдә§зҺҜеўғеә”иҜҘйҷҗеҲ¶дёәеүҚз«Ҝеҹҹеҗ?
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# жҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°жңҚеҠЎж—Ҙеҝ—еҶҷе…Ҙж–Үд»¶пјҢдҫҝдәҺеңЁгҖҢж—Ҙеҝ—жҹҘзңӢгҖҚз•ҢйқўжҹҘзң?
_log_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "logs")
os.makedirs(_log_dir, exist_ok=True)
_api_log_file = os.path.join(_log_dir, "api.log")
_handler = logging.FileHandler(_api_log_file, encoding="utf-8")
_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(message)s"))
logging.root.addHandler(_handler)
logging.root.setLevel(logging.INFO)
logging.info("Web Admin API еҗҜеҠЁпјҢж—Ҙеҝ—е°ҶеҶҷе…Ҙ %s", _api_log_file)

# Dockerе®ўжҲ·з«?
# жё…йҷӨеҸҜиғҪе№Іжү°зҡ„зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮ?
import os
for env_var in ['DOCKER_HOST', 'DOCKER_TLS_VERIFY', 'DOCKER_CERT_PATH']:
    os.environ.pop(env_var, None)

# жЈҖжҹҘDocker socketж–Үд»¶жҳҜеҗҰеӯҳеңЁ
docker_socket_path = '/var/run/docker.sock'
if os.path.exists(docker_socket_path):
    print(f"Docker socket found at {docker_socket_path}")
    stat_info = os.stat(docker_socket_path)
    print(f"Socket permissions: {oct(stat_info.st_mode)}")
    print(f"Socket owner UID: {stat_info.st_uid}, GID: {stat_info.st_gid}")
else:
    print(f"Warning: Docker socket not found at {docker_socket_path}")

docker_client = None
docker_api = None

# е°қиҜ•еӨҡз§Қж–№ејҸеҲқе§ӢеҢ–Dockerе®ўжҲ·з«?
try:
    # ж–№жі•1: зӣҙжҺҘдҪҝз”Ёsocketж–Үд»¶и·Ҝеҫ„пјҲдёҚдҪҝз”Ёunix://еүҚзјҖпј?
    docker_api = docker.APIClient(base_url='unix:///var/run/docker.sock')
    docker_api.ping()
    print("Docker APIClient initialized successfully (method 1)")
    docker_client = docker.DockerClient(base_url='unix:///var/run/docker.sock')
    docker_client.ping()
    print("Docker DockerClient initialized successfully")
except Exception as e1:
    print(f"Method 1 failed: {e1}")
    try:
        # ж–№жі•2: дҪҝз”ЁзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸж–№ејҸ
        os.environ['DOCKER_HOST'] = 'unix:///var/run/docker.sock'
        docker_api = docker.APIClient()
        docker_api.ping()
        print("Docker APIClient initialized successfully (method 2)")
        docker_client = docker.DockerClient()
        docker_client.ping()
        print("Docker DockerClient initialized successfully (method 2)")
    except Exception as e2:
        print(f"Method 2 failed: {e2}")
        try:
            # ж–№жі•3: дҪҝз”ЁrequestsзӣҙжҺҘи°ғз”ЁDocker HTTP API
            import requests_unixsocket
            docker_api = None  # ж Үи®°дёәдҪҝз”ЁHTTP API
            docker_client = None
            print("Will use HTTP API fallback for Docker operations")
        except Exception as e3:
            print(f"All methods failed: {e3}")
            import traceback
            traceback.print_exc()
            docker_client = None
            docker_api = None


# ж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠЎе®ҡжңҹи®ёеҸҜиҜҒж ЎйӘҢпјҡжҜ?48 е°Ҹж—¶жү§иЎҢдёҖж¬ЎпјҢжңӘйҖҡиҝҮеҲҷиҮӘеҠЁеҒңжӯўж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠ?
LICENSE_CHECK_INTERVAL_SEC = 48 * 3600  # 48 hours


def _run_license_periodic_check():
    """еҗҺеҸ°зәҝзЁӢпјҡжҜҸ 48 е°Ҹж—¶ж ЎйӘҢи®ёеҸҜиҜҒпјҢжңӘйҖҡиҝҮеҲҷеҒңжӯўж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠ?""
    while True:
        time.sleep(LICENSE_CHECK_INTERVAL_SEC)
        try:
            valid, error_code, _ = validate_license(API_VERSION)
            if valid:
                continue
            # и®ёеҸҜиҜҒж— ж•ҲпјҡеҒңжӯўж ҮеҮҶ Docker жңҚеҠЎ
            if docker_client:
                for name in STANDARD_DOCKER_SERVICES:
                    try:
                        c = docker_client.containers.get(name)
                        if c.status == "running":
                            c.stop()
                            print(f"License invalid: stopped standard service {name}")
                    except Exception as e:
                        if "NotFound" not in str(type(e).__name__):
                            print(f"License check stop {name}: {e}")
            # еҒңжӯўж ҮеҮҶ systemd жңҚеҠЎ
            for name in STANDARD_SYSTEMD_SERVICES:
                try:
                    subprocess.run(
                        ["sudo", "systemctl", "stop", name],
                        capture_output=True,
                        text=True,
                        timeout=10,
                    )
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"License check stop systemd {name}: {e}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"License periodic check error: {e}")


@app.on_event("startup")
def start_license_check_thread():
    """еҗҜеҠЁеҗҺејҖеҗ?48 е°Ҹж—¶е‘Ёжңҹи®ёеҸҜиҜҒж ЎйӘҢзәҝзЁ?""
    t = threading.Thread(target=_run_license_periodic_check, daemon=True)
    t.start()
    print("License periodic check thread started (interval: 48h)")

    return {
        "status": "ok",
        "service": "arbore-web-admin-api",
        "version": API_VERSION,
        "build_time": BUILD_TIME
    }

        "build_time": BUILD_TIME,

    }


# ==================== и®ёеҸҜиҜ?API ====================

def _license_valid_or_403():
    """иӢҘи®ёеҸҜиҜҒж— ж•ҲеҲҷжҠӣеҮ?403пјҢеҗҰеҲҷиҝ”еӣ?(True, license_info)гҖ?""
    valid, error_code, info = validate_license(API_VERSION)
    if not valid:
        detail = {"code": error_code, "message": _license_error_message(error_code)}
        raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail=detail)
    return (True, info)


def _license_error_message(code: Optional[str]) -> str:
    msg = {
        "LICENSE_NOT_FOUND": "License not configured",
        "LICENSE_INVALID": "License invalid or validation code mismatch",
        "HARDWARE_MISMATCH": "License does not match this host",
        "VERSION_MISMATCH": "License version does not match",
        "SECRET_NOT_CONFIGURED": "Server license secret not configured",
    }
    return msg.get(code, "License check failed")


@app.get("/api/v1/license")
async def get_license():
    """иҺ·еҸ–еҪ“еүҚи®ёеҸҜиҜҒдҝЎжҒҜеҸҠж ЎйӘҢзҠ¶жҖ?""
    valid, error_code, info = validate_license(API_VERSION)
    fingerprint, display_id = get_host_hardware_fingerprint()
    data = {
        "registered": valid,
        "valid": valid,
        "errorCode": error_code,
        "hostFingerprint": display_id,
        "versionInfo": API_VERSION.split(".")[0].zfill(3) if API_VERSION else "001",
    }
    if info:
        data["companyId"] = info.get("companyId", "")
        data["companyName"] = info.get("companyName", "")
        data["versionInfo"] = info.get("versionInfo", data["versionInfo"])
    return data


@app.get("/api/v1/license/hardware-fingerprint")
async def get_hardware_fingerprint():
    """иҺ·еҸ–е®ҝдё»жңәзЎ¬д»¶жҢҮзә№пјҲд»…е®ҝдё»жңәпјҢйқһе®№еҷЁпјүпјҢз”ЁдәҺжіЁеҶҢйЎөеұ•зӨ?""
    fingerprint, display_id = get_host_hardware_fingerprint()
    return {"hostFingerprint": display_id, "rawAvailable": fingerprint is not None}


@app.post("/api/v1/license/register")
async def register_license(
    companyId: str = Form(..., alias="companyId"),
    validationCode: str = Form(..., alias="validationCode"),
    companyName: str = Form(..., alias="companyName"),
):
    """жіЁеҶҢи®ёеҸҜиҜҒпјҡж ЎйӘҢз ҒйӘҢиҜҒйҖҡиҝҮеҗҺеҶҷе…?license.json"""
    secret = get_license_secret()
    if not secret:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail={"code": "SECRET_NOT_CONFIGURED", "message": "Server license secret not configured"})
    fingerprint, display_id = get_host_hardware_fingerprint()
    if not fingerprint:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail={"code": "HARDWARE_UNAVAILABLE", "message": "Host hardware fingerprint unavailable"})
    # дҪҝз”Ё display_idпјҲhost-xxxпјүдёҺ validation-code-generator.js зҡ?hostId дёҖиҮ?
    expected = compute_validation_code(companyId, display_id, API_VERSION, secret)
    if not hmac.compare_digest(expected.upper(), validationCode.strip().upper()):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail={"code": "LICENSE_INVALID", "message": "Validation code invalid or not for this host"})
    version_major = API_VERSION.split(".")[0].zfill(3) if API_VERSION else "001"
    save_license({
        "companyId": companyId,
        "validationCode": validationCode.strip(),
        "companyName": companyName.strip(),
        "version": version_major,
        "versionInfo": version_major,
    })
    return {"success": True, "message": "License registered"}


@app.post("/api/v1/license/validate")
async def post_license_validate():
    """йӘҢиҜҒеҪ“еүҚи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжҳҜеҗҰжңүж•?""
    valid, error_code, info = validate_license(API_VERSION)
    return {"valid": valid, "errorCode": error_code, "license": info}


def get_systemd_service_status(service_name: str) -> Dict:
    """иҺ·еҸ– systemd жңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖ?""
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            ['systemctl', 'is-active', service_name],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            timeout=5
        )
        is_active = result.stdout.strip() == 'active'
        
        result = subprocess.run(
            ['systemctl', 'is-enabled', service_name],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            timeout=5
        )
        is_enabled = result.stdout.strip() == 'enabled'
        
        # иҺ·еҸ–з«ҜеҸЈдҝЎжҒҜ
        ports = []
        port_map = {
            'service-router': ['2026'],
            'service-pdf-to-png': ['2027'],
            'service-paddle-ocr': ['2028'],
            'service-tesseract-ocr': ['2029']
        }
        if service_name in port_map:
            ports = port_map[service_name]
        
        return {
            "name": service_name,
            "status": "running" if is_active else "stopped",
            "health": "healthy" if is_active else "unhealthy",
            "ports": ports,
            "enabled": is_enabled,
            "type": "systemd"
        }
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error checking systemd service {service_name}: {e}")
        return {
            "name": service_name,
            "status": "unknown",
            "health": "unknown",
            "ports": [],
            "enabled": False,
            "type": "systemd"
        }


# ж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠЎеҲ—иЎЁпјҲи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжңӘйҖҡиҝҮж—¶зҰҒжӯўеҗҜеҠЁпјҢдё”е®ҡжңҹж ЎйӘҢжңӘйҖҡиҝҮж—¶иҮӘеҠЁеҒңжӯўпјү
STANDARD_DOCKER_SERVICES = [
    "arbore-flow",
    "arbore-func",
    "arbore-postgres-nocobase",
    "arbore-postgres-vector",
    "arbore-ollama",
    "arbore-ollama-webui",
    "arbore-quickchart",
]
STANDARD_SYSTEMD_SERVICES = [
    "service-pdf-to-png",
    "service-paddle-ocr",
    "service-tesseract-ocr",
]


@app.get("/api/v1/services")
async def get_services():
    """иҺ·еҸ–жүҖжңүжңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖ?""
    services = []
    docker_service_names = list(STANDARD_DOCKER_SERVICES)
    systemd_service_names = list(STANDARD_SYSTEMD_SERVICES)

    # и®ёеҸҜиҜҒзҠ¶жҖҒпјҲдҫӣеүҚз«ҜзҰҒз”ЁеҗҜеҠ?йҮҚеҗҜпј?
    license_valid, license_error_code, _ = validate_license(API_VERSION)

    # иҺ·еҸ– Docker жңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖ?
    service_names = docker_service_names
    
    # дјҳе…ҲдҪҝз”Ёdocker_clientпјҢеҰӮжһңдёҚеҸҜз”ЁеҲҷдҪҝз”Ёdocker_apiпјҢжңҖеҗҺдҪҝз”ЁHTTP API fallback
    if docker_client:
        try:
            containers = docker_client.containers.list(all=True)
            container_dict = {c.name: c for c in containers}
            
            for name in service_names:
                container = container_dict.get(name)
                if container:
                    status = container.status
                    health = "unknown"
                    try:
                        health_info = container.attrs.get("State", {}).get("Health", {})
                        health = health_info.get("Status", "unknown")
                    except:
                        pass
                    
                    ports = []
                    try:
                        port_bindings = container.attrs.get("NetworkSettings", {}).get("Ports", {})
                        for container_port, host_ports in port_bindings.items():
                            if host_ports:
                                for hp in host_ports:
                                    ports.append(f"{hp['HostPort']}:{container_port.split('/')[0]}")
                    except:
                        pass
                    
                    services.append({
                        "name": name,
                        "status": status,
                        "health": health,
                        "ports": ports,
                    })
                else:
                    services.append({
                        "name": name,
                        "status": "not_found",
                        "health": "unknown",
                        "ports": []
                    })
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error using docker_client: {e}")
            if docker_api:
                try:
                    r = await get_services_api(service_names)
                    services = r.get("services", [])
                except Exception as e2:
                    print(f"Error using docker_api: {e2}")
                    r = await get_services_subprocess(service_names)
                    services = r.get("services", [])
            else:
                r = await get_services_subprocess(service_names)
                services = r.get("services", [])
    elif docker_api:
        try:
            r = await get_services_api(service_names)
            services = r.get("services", [])
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error using docker_api: {e}")
            r = await get_services_subprocess(service_names)
            services = r.get("services", [])
    else:
        r = await get_services_subprocess(service_names)
        services = r.get("services", [])

    # ж·»еҠ  systemd жңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖ?
    for systemd_name in systemd_service_names:
        systemd_status = get_systemd_service_status(systemd_name)
        services.append(systemd_status)

    return {
        "services": services,
        "licenseValid": license_valid,
        "licenseErrorCode": license_error_code,
    }


async def get_services_api(service_names):
    """дҪҝз”Ёdocker.APIClientиҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖҒпјҲfallbackж–№жі•пј?""
    services = []
    try:
        containers_data = docker_api.containers(all=True)
        container_dict = {c['Names'][0].lstrip('/'): c for c in containers_data}
        
        for name in service_names:
            container = container_dict.get(name)
            if container:
                status = container.get('State', 'unknown')
                health = "unknown"
                
                # иҺ·еҸ–иҜҰз»ҶдҝЎжҒҜпјҲеҢ…жӢ¬еҒҘеә·зҠ¶жҖҒпјү
                try:
                    inspect_data = docker_api.inspect_container(name)
                    state = inspect_data.get('State', {})
                    status = state.get('Status', status)
                    health_info = state.get('Health', {})
                    health = health_info.get('Status', 'unknown')
                    
                    # иҺ·еҸ–з«ҜеҸЈжҳ е°„
                    ports = []
                    port_bindings = inspect_data.get('NetworkSettings', {}).get('Ports', {})
                    for container_port, host_ports in port_bindings.items():
                        if host_ports:
                            for hp in host_ports:
                                ports.append(f"{hp['HostPort']}:{container_port.split('/')[0]}")
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"Error inspecting container {name}: {e}")
                    ports = []
                
                services.append({
                    "name": name,
                    "status": status.lower() if status else "unknown",
                    "health": health,
                    "ports": ports,
                })
            else:
                services.append({
                    "name": name,
                    "status": "not_found",
                    "health": "unknown",
                    "ports": []
                })
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error in docker_api fallback: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        # иҝ”еӣһй»ҳи®ӨзҠ¶жҖ?
        for name in service_names:
            services.append({
                "name": name,
                "status": "unknown",
                "health": "unknown",
                "ports": []
            })
    
    return {"services": services}


async def get_services_subprocess(service_names):
    """дҪҝз”ЁDocker HTTP APIиҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖҒпјҲжңҖеҗҺfallbackж–№жі•пј?""
    import requests_unixsocket
    import json
    
    services = []
    try:
        # дҪҝз”Ёrequests-unixsocketзӣҙжҺҘи°ғз”ЁDocker HTTP API
        session = requests_unixsocket.Session()
        url = 'http+unix://%2Fvar%2Frun%2Fdocker.sock/containers/json?all=1'
        
        response = session.get(url)
        if response.status_code == 200:
            containers_data = response.json()
            container_dict = {c['Names'][0].lstrip('/'): c for c in containers_data}
            
            for name in service_names:
                container = container_dict.get(name)
                if container:
                    status = container.get('State', 'unknown')
                    health = "unknown"
                    
                    # иҺ·еҸ–иҜҰз»ҶдҝЎжҒҜпјҲеҢ…жӢ¬еҒҘеә·зҠ¶жҖҒпјү
                    try:
                        inspect_url = f'http+unix://%2Fvar%2Frun%2Fdocker.sock/containers/{name}/json'
                        inspect_response = session.get(inspect_url)
                        if inspect_response.status_code == 200:
                            inspect_data = inspect_response.json()
                            state = inspect_data.get('State', {})
                            status = state.get('Status', status)
                            health_info = state.get('Health', {})
                            health = health_info.get('Status', 'unknown')
                            
                            # иҺ·еҸ–з«ҜеҸЈжҳ е°„
                            ports = []
                            port_bindings = inspect_data.get('NetworkSettings', {}).get('Ports', {})
                            for container_port, host_ports in port_bindings.items():
                                if host_ports:
                                    for hp in host_ports:
                                        ports.append(f"{hp['HostPort']}:{container_port.split('/')[0]}")
                    except Exception as e:
                        print(f"Error inspecting container {name}: {e}")
                        ports = []
                    
                    services.append({
                        "name": name,
                        "status": status.lower() if status else "unknown",
                        "health": health,
                        "ports": ports,
                    })
                else:
                    services.append({
                        "name": name,
                        "status": "not_found",
                        "health": "unknown",
                        "ports": []
                    })
        else:
            raise Exception(f"Docker API returned {response.status_code}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error in HTTP API fallback: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        # иҝ”еӣһй»ҳи®ӨзҠ¶жҖ?
        for name in service_names:
            services.append({
                "name": name,
                "status": "unknown",
                "health": "unknown",
                "ports": []
            })
    
    return {"services": services}


@app.get("/api/v1/services/{service_name}")
async def get_service_detail(service_name: str):
    """иҺ·еҸ–еҚ•дёӘжңҚеҠЎиҜҰз»ҶдҝЎжҒҜ"""
    if docker_client:
        try:
            container = docker_client.containers.get(service_name)
            stats = container.stats(stream=False)
            
            return {
                "name": service_name,
                "status": container.status,
                "image": container.image.tags[0] if container.image.tags else "unknown",
                "created": container.attrs.get("Created"),
                "cpu_usage": stats.get("cpu_stats", {}).get("cpu_usage", {}).get("total_usage", 0),
                "memory_usage": stats.get("memory_stats", {}).get("usage", 0),
                "memory_limit": stats.get("memory_stats", {}).get("limit", 0),
            }
        except docker.errors.NotFound:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Service {service_name} not found")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error using docker_client: {e}")
            # Fallback to docker_api or HTTP API
            if docker_api:
                try:
                    return await get_service_detail_api(service_name)
                except Exception as e2:
                    print(f"Error using docker_api: {e2}")
                    raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail="Docker client not available")
            else:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail="Docker client not available")
    elif docker_api:
        try:
            return await get_service_detail_api(service_name)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error using docker_api: {e}")
            raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail="Docker client not available")
    else:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail="Docker client not available")


async def get_service_detail_api(service_name: str):
    """дҪҝз”Ёdocker_apiиҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎиҜҰжғ…"""
    try:
        inspect_data = docker_api.inspect_container(service_name)
        state = inspect_data.get('State', {})
        stats = docker_api.stats(service_name, stream=False)
        
        return {
            "name": service_name,
            "status": state.get('Status', 'unknown'),
            "image": inspect_data.get('Config', {}).get('Image', 'unknown'),
            "created": inspect_data.get('Created'),
            "cpu_usage": stats.get("cpu_stats", {}).get("cpu_usage", {}).get("total_usage", 0),
            "memory_usage": stats.get("memory_stats", {}).get("usage", 0),
            "memory_limit": stats.get("memory_stats", {}).get("limit", 0),
        }
    except docker.errors.NotFound:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Service {service_name} not found")
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))


@app.get("/api/v1/system/resources")
async def get_system_resources():
    """иҺ·еҸ–зі»з»ҹиө„жәҗдҪҝз”Ёжғ…еҶө"""
    try:
        cpu_percent = psutil.cpu_percent(interval=1)
        memory = psutil.virtual_memory()
        disk = psutil.disk_usage('/')
        
        return {
            "cpu": {
                "percent": cpu_percent,
                "count": psutil.cpu_count()
            },
            "memory": {
                "total": memory.total,
                "used": memory.used,
                "available": memory.available,
                "percent": memory.percent
            },
            "disk": {
                "total": disk.total,
                "used": disk.used,
                "free": disk.free,
                "percent": disk.percent
            },
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
        }
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))


@app.post("/api/v1/services/{service_name}/start")
async def start_service(service_name: str):
    """еҗҜеҠЁжңҚеҠЎпјҲж”ҜжҢ?Docker е’?systemdпјүгҖӮж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠЎйңҖи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжңүж•Ҳж–№еҸҜеҗҜеҠЁгҖ?""
    # ж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠЎпјҡи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжңӘйҖҡиҝҮеҲҷзҰҒжӯўеҗҜеҠ?
    if service_name in STANDARD_DOCKER_SERVICES or service_name in STANDARD_SYSTEMD_SERVICES:
        try:
            _license_valid_or_403()
        except HTTPException:
            raise

    # жЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжҳҜ systemd жңҚеҠЎ
    systemd_services = ["service-router", "service-pdf-to-png", "service-paddle-ocr", "service-tesseract-ocr"]
    if service_name in systemd_services:
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(
                ['sudo', 'systemctl', 'start', service_name],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=10
            )
            if result.returncode == 0:
                return {"success": True, "message": f"Service {service_name} started"}
            else:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=result.stderr)
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
    
    # Docker жңҚеҠЎ
    if docker_client:
        try:
            container = docker_client.containers.get(service_name)
            container.start()
            return {"success": True, "message": f"Service {service_name} started"}
        except docker.errors.NotFound:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Service {service_name} not found")
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
    else:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail="Docker client not available")


@app.post("/api/v1/services/{service_name}/stop")
async def stop_service(service_name: str):
    """еҒңжӯўжңҚеҠЎпјҲж”ҜжҢ?Docker е’?systemdпј?""
    # жЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжҳҜ systemd жңҚеҠЎ
    systemd_services = ["service-router", "service-pdf-to-png", "service-paddle-ocr", "service-tesseract-ocr"]
    if service_name in systemd_services:
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(
                ['sudo', 'systemctl', 'stop', service_name],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=10
            )
            if result.returncode == 0:
                return {"success": True, "message": f"Service {service_name} stopped"}
            else:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=result.stderr)
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
    
    # Docker жңҚеҠЎ
    if docker_client:
        try:
            container = docker_client.containers.get(service_name)
            container.stop()
            return {"success": True, "message": f"Service {service_name} stopped"}
        except docker.errors.NotFound:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Service {service_name} not found")
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
    else:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail="Docker client not available")


@app.post("/api/v1/services/{service_name}/restart")
async def restart_service(service_name: str):
    """йҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎпјҲж”ҜжҢ?Docker е’?systemdпјүгҖӮж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠЎйңҖи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжңүж•Ҳж–№еҸҜйҮҚеҗҜгҖ?""
    # ж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠЎпјҡи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжңӘйҖҡиҝҮеҲҷзҰҒжӯўйҮҚеҗ?
    if service_name in STANDARD_DOCKER_SERVICES or service_name in STANDARD_SYSTEMD_SERVICES:
        try:
            _license_valid_or_403()
        except HTTPException:
            raise

    # жЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжҳҜ systemd жңҚеҠЎ
    systemd_services = ["service-router", "service-pdf-to-png", "service-paddle-ocr", "service-tesseract-ocr"]
    if service_name in systemd_services:
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(
                ['sudo', 'systemctl', 'restart', service_name],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=10
            )
            if result.returncode == 0:
                return {"success": True, "message": f"Service {service_name} restarted"}
            else:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=result.stderr)
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
    
    # Docker жңҚеҠЎ
    if docker_client:
        try:
            container = docker_client.containers.get(service_name)
            container.restart()
            return {"success": True, "message": f"Service {service_name} restarted"}
        except docker.errors.NotFound:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Service {service_name} not found")
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
    else:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail="Docker client not available")


@app.get("/api/v1/services/{service_name}/logs")
async def get_service_logs(service_name: str, tail: int = 100):
    """иҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎж—Ҙеҝ—пјҲж”ҜжҢ?Docker е’?systemdпј?""
    # жЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжҳҜ systemd жңҚеҠЎ
    systemd_services = ["service-router", "service-pdf-to-png", "service-paddle-ocr", "service-tesseract-ocr"]
    if service_name in systemd_services:
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(
                ['journalctl', '-u', service_name, '-n', str(tail), '--no-pager'],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=10
            )
            if result.returncode == 0:
                logs = result.stdout.split('\n')
                return {"logs": logs}
            else:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=result.stderr)
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
    
    # Docker жңҚеҠЎ
    if docker_client:
        try:
            container = docker_client.containers.get(service_name)
            logs = container.logs(tail=tail, timestamps=True).decode('utf-8')
            return {"logs": logs.split('\n')}
        except docker.errors.NotFound:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Service {service_name} not found")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error using docker_client: {e}")
            # Fallback to docker_api or HTTP API
            if docker_api:
                try:
                    return await get_service_logs_api(service_name, tail)
                except Exception as e2:
                    print(f"Error using docker_api: {e2}")
                    return await get_service_logs_http(service_name, tail)
            else:
                return await get_service_logs_http(service_name, tail)
    elif docker_api:
        try:
            return await get_service_logs_api(service_name, tail)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error using docker_api: {e}")
            return await get_service_logs_http(service_name, tail)
    else:
        return await get_service_logs_http(service_name, tail)


async def get_service_logs_api(service_name: str, tail: int = 100):
    """дҪҝз”Ёdocker_apiиҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎж—Ҙеҝ—"""
    try:
        logs = docker_api.logs(service_name, tail=tail, timestamps=True).decode('utf-8')
        return {"logs": logs.split('\n')}
    except docker.errors.NotFound:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Service {service_name} not found")
    except Exception as e:
        # Fallback to HTTP API
        return await get_service_logs_http(service_name, tail)


async def get_service_logs_http(service_name: str, tail: int = 100):
    """дҪҝз”ЁHTTP APIиҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎж—Ҙеҝ—пјҲжңҖеҗҺfallbackпј?""
    import requests_unixsocket
    try:
        session = requests_unixsocket.Session()
        url = f'http+unix://%2Fvar%2Frun%2Fdocker.sock/containers/{service_name}/logs?tail={tail}&timestamps=1&stdout=1&stderr=1'
        response = session.get(url)
        if response.status_code == 200:
            logs = response.text.split('\n')
            return {"logs": logs}
        elif response.status_code == 404:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Service {service_name} not found")
        else:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Docker API returned {response.status_code}")
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))


@app.get("/api/v1/system/ip")
async def get_system_ip():
    """иҺ·еҸ–еҪ“еүҚжңҚеҠЎеҷЁIPең°еқҖ"""
    try:
        import socket
        import subprocess
        
        # ж–№жі•1: йҖҡиҝҮhostnameиҺ·еҸ–
        try:
            hostname = socket.gethostname()
            ip = socket.gethostbyname(hostname)
            if ip and not ip.startswith("127."):
                return {
                    "current_ip": ip,
                    "method": "hostname",
                    "hostname": hostname
                }
        except:
            pass
        
        # ж–№жі•2: йҖҡиҝҮipе‘Ҫд»ӨиҺ·еҸ–пјҲLinuxпј?
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(
                ['ip', 'route', 'get', '8.8.8.8'],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=5
            )
            if result.returncode == 0:
                import re
                match = re.search(r'src\s+(\d+\.\d+\.\d+\.\d+)', result.stdout)
                if match:
                    ip = match.group(1)
                    return {
                        "current_ip": ip,
                        "method": "ip_route"
                    }
        except:
            pass
        
        # ж–№жі•3: йҖҡиҝҮifconfigиҺ·еҸ–
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(
                ['ifconfig'],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=5
            )
            if result.returncode == 0:
                import re
                # жҹҘжүҫйқ?27.0.0.1зҡ„IPең°еқҖ
                matches = re.findall(r'inet\s+(\d+\.\d+\.\d+\.\d+)', result.stdout)
                for ip in matches:
                    if not ip.startswith("127.") and not ip.startswith("169.254."):
                        return {
                            "current_ip": ip,
                            "method": "ifconfig"
                        }
        except:
            pass
        
        # ж–№жі•4: йҖҡиҝҮhostname -IиҺ·еҸ–
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(
                ['hostname', '-I'],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                timeout=5
            )
            if result.returncode == 0:
                ips = result.stdout.strip().split()
                for ip in ips:
                    if not ip.startswith("127.") and not ip.startswith("169.254."):
                        return {
                            "current_ip": ip,
                            "method": "hostname_I"
                        }
        except:
            pass
        
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="ж— жі•жЈҖжөӢжңҚеҠЎеҷЁIPең°еқҖ")
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"жЈҖжөӢIPең°еқҖеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")


@app.get("/api/v1/system/config")
async def get_system_config():
    """иҺ·еҸ–зі»з»ҹй…ҚзҪ®пјҲд»Һ.envж–Үд»¶пј?""
    try:
        import os
        project_root = os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))))
        env_file = os.path.join(project_root, ".env")
        
        config = {}
        if os.path.exists(env_file):
            with open(env_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                for line in f:
                    line = line.strip()
                    if line and not line.startswith('#') and '=' in line:
                        key, value = line.split('=', 1)
                        config[key.strip()] = value.strip()
        
        # иҺ·еҸ–еҪ“еүҚIP
        current_ip_info = await get_system_ip()
        current_ip = current_ip_info.get("current_ip", "")
        
        # иҺ·еҸ–й…ҚзҪ®зҡ„IP
        configured_ip = config.get("SERVER_IP", "")
        
        return {
            "current_ip": current_ip,
            "configured_ip": configured_ip,
            "needs_update": current_ip != configured_ip and configured_ip != "",
            "config": config
        }
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"иҜ»еҸ–й…ҚзҪ®еӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")


@app.get("/api/v1/system/admin-logs")
async def get_admin_logs(tail: int = 200):
    """иҺ·еҸ–жҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°жңҚеҠЎпјҲWeb Admin APIпјүиҮӘиә«ж—Ҙеҝ—пјҢдҫӣз•ҢйқўгҖҢж—Ҙеҝ—жҹҘзңӢгҖҚдҪҝз”?""
    log_file = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "logs", "api.log")
    if not os.path.exists(log_file):
        return {"logs": ["ж—Ҙеҝ—ж–Үд»¶е°ҡжңӘз”ҹжҲҗпјҢиҜ·зЁҚеҗҺйҮҚиҜ•жҲ–жЈҖжҹ?backend/logs/api.log жҳҜеҗҰеӯҳеңЁгҖ?]}
    try:
        with open(log_file, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="replace") as f:
            lines = f.readlines()
        lines = [line.rstrip("\n") for line in lines]
        return {"logs": lines[-tail:] if len(lines) > tail else lines}
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"иҜ»еҸ–ж—Ҙеҝ—еӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")


@app.post("/api/v1/system/config/update-ip")
async def update_system_ip():
    """жӣҙж–°зі»з»ҹIPең°еқҖй…ҚзҪ®"""
    try:
        import os
        import subprocess
        
        # иҺ·еҸ–еҪ“еүҚIP
        current_ip_info = await get_system_ip()
        new_ip = current_ip_info.get("current_ip", "")
        
        if not new_ip:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="ж— жі•жЈҖжөӢеҪ“еүҚIPең°еқҖ")
        
        # иҺ·еҸ–йЎ№зӣ®ж №зӣ®еҪ?
        project_root = os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))))
        script_path = os.path.join(project_root, "scripts", "update-server-ip.sh")
        
        if not os.path.exists(script_path):
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="IPжӣҙж–°и„ҡжң¬дёҚеӯҳең?)
        
        # жү§иЎҢжӣҙж–°и„ҡжң¬
        result = subprocess.run(
            ['bash', script_path, new_ip],
            cwd=project_root,
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            timeout=60
        )
        
        if result.returncode != 0:
            raise HTTPException(
                status_code=500,
                detail=f"жү§иЎҢжӣҙж–°и„ҡжң¬еӨұиҙҘ: {result.stderr}"
            )
        
        # йҮҚеҗҜзӣёе…іDockerжңҚеҠЎ
        restart_services = ["arbore-flow", "arbore-nginx"]
        restart_results = []
        
        if docker_client:
            for service_name in restart_services:
                try:
                    container = docker_client.containers.get(service_name)
                    container.restart(timeout=60)
                    restart_results.append({
                        "service": service_name,
                        "status": "restarted"
                    })
                except docker.errors.NotFound:
                    restart_results.append({
                        "service": service_name,
                        "status": "not_found"
                    })
                except Exception as e:
                    restart_results.append({
                        "service": service_name,
                        "status": "error",
                        "error": str(e)
                    })
        else:
            # дҪҝз”Ёdocker-composeе‘Ҫд»Ө
            try:
                compose_result = subprocess.run(
                    _docker_compose_cmd() + ["restart"] + restart_services,
                    cwd=project_root,
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True,
                    timeout=120
                )
                if compose_result.returncode == 0:
                    for service_name in restart_services:
                        restart_results.append({
                            "service": service_name,
                            "status": "restarted"
                        })
                else:
                    restart_results.append({
                        "service": "all",
                        "status": "error",
                        "error": compose_result.stderr
                    })
            except Exception as e:
                restart_results.append({
                    "service": "all",
                    "status": "error",
                    "error": str(e)
                })
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "new_ip": new_ip,
            "script_output": result.stdout,
            "restart_results": restart_results,
            "message": f"IPең°еқҖе·Іжӣҙж–°дёә {new_ip}пјҢзӣёе…іжңҚеҠЎе·ІйҮҚеҗҜ"
        }
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"жӣҙж–°IPй…ҚзҪ®еӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")


# ==================== иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎз®Ўзҗ?API ====================

class CustomServiceCreate(BaseModel):
    name: str
    port: int
    endpoint: str
    description: str
    icon: Optional[str] = "Box"
    image_name: Optional[str] = None

class CustomServiceUpdate(BaseModel):
    name: Optional[str] = None
    port: Optional[int] = None
    container_port: Optional[int] = None  # е®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҸҜйҖүпјү
    endpoint: Optional[str] = None
    description: Optional[str] = None
    icon: Optional[str] = None
    env_vars: Optional[str] = None  # зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸJSONй…ҚзҪ®
    volumes: Optional[str] = None  # еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪJSONй…ҚзҪ®пјҢж јеј? ["host_path:container_path"]
    memory_limit_mb: Optional[int] = None  # еҶ…еӯҳйҷҗеҲ¶пјҲMBпјүпјҢйҮҚеҗҜеҗҺз”ҹж•?
    memory_reservation_mb: Optional[int] = None  # еҶ…еӯҳйў„з•ҷпјҲMBпј?

def get_project_root():
    """иҺ·еҸ–йЎ№зӣ®ж №зӣ®еҪ•пјҢж”ҜжҢҒйҖҡиҝҮ ARBORE_PROJECT_ROOT зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸжҢҮе®ҡпјҲDocker е®№еҷЁйғЁзҪІж—¶еҝ…йЎ»и®ҫзҪ®пјү"""
    env_root = os.environ.get('ARBORE_PROJECT_ROOT')
    if env_root:
        return env_root
    current_file = os.path.abspath(__file__)
    return os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(current_file)))


def _docker_compose_cmd():
    """з»ҹдёҖдҪҝз”Ё docker composeпјҲV2пјүгҖӮзҺҜеўғйЎ»е®үиЈ… Docker Compose жҸ’д»¶пјҢдёҚеңЁжӯӨеҒ?fallbackгҖ?""
    return ["docker", "compose"]

def parse_nginx_config():
    """и§Јжһҗnginxй…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶пјҢжҸҗеҸ–иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎдҝЎжҒҜ"""
    project_root = get_project_root()
    nginx_config_path = os.path.join(project_root, "nginx", "conf.d", "default.conf")
    
    services = []
    
    if not os.path.exists(nginx_config_path):
        return services
    
    with open(nginx_config_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # еҢ№й…Қlocationеқ—пјҢжҸҗеҸ–жңҚеҠЎдҝЎжҒҜ
    # ж јејҸ1: # {жңҚеҠЎжҸҸиҝ°} [icon:IconName]пјҲе®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈ {port}пјҢйҖҡиҝҮ nginx з»ҹдёҖеҜ№еӨ–пј?
    #        location /path { ... proxy_pass http://service-name:port/... }
    # ж јејҸ2: {жңҚеҠЎжҸҸиҝ°} [icon:IconName]пјҲе®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈ {port}пјҢйҖҡиҝҮ nginx з»ҹдёҖеҜ№еӨ–пј?
    #        location /path { ... proxy_pass http://service-name:port/... }
    # ж јејҸ3: location /path { ... proxy_pass http://service-name:port/... }пјҲж— жіЁйҮҠпј?
    # дҪҝз”ЁжӣҙзҒөжҙ»зҡ„жӯЈеҲҷиЎЁиҫҫејҸеҢ№й…ҚеӨҡиЎҢlocationеқ?
    # е…Ҳе°қиҜ•еҢ№й…ҚжңүжіЁйҮҠзҡ„пјҲеҢ…еҗ«"е®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸ?пј?
    location_pattern_with_comment = r'(?:#\s*)?([^\n]+?)\s*пјҲе®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈ\s+(\d+)[^пјү]*пјү[^\n]*\n\s*location\s+([^\s{]+)\s*\{[^}]*?proxy_pass\s+http://([^:/\s]+):(\d+)([^;]*?);'
    # еҶҚеҢ№й…ҚжІЎжңүжіЁйҮҠдҪҶз«ҜеҸЈең?000-7999зҡ?
    location_pattern_no_comment = r'\n\s*location\s+([^\s{]+)\s*\{[^}]*?proxy_pass\s+http://([^:/\s]+):(\d+)([^;]*?);'
    
    services_found = {}  # з”ЁдәҺеҺ»йҮҚпјҢkey: service_name:port, value: service_info
    
    # е…ҲеҢ№й…ҚжңүжіЁйҮҠзҡ„locationеқ?
    matches = re.finditer(location_pattern_with_comment, content, re.MULTILINE | re.DOTALL)
    
    for match in matches:
        description_line = match.group(1).strip()
        port_from_comment = int(match.group(2))
        location_path = match.group(3).strip()
        service_name = match.group(4).strip()
        try:
            port = int(match.group(5))
        except ValueError:
            continue
        
        # жЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжҳҜиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎпјҲз«ҜеҸЈең?000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ…пјү
        if 7000 <= port <= 7999:
            # жҸҗеҸ–з«ҜзӮ№еҗҚз§°пјҲд»Һlocationи·Ҝеҫ„дёӯжҸҗеҸ–пјү
            endpoint = location_path.rstrip('/').lstrip('/')
            # з§»йҷӨеҸҜиғҪзҡ„зӯүеҸ·еүҚзјҖпјҲlocation = /pathпј?
            endpoint = endpoint.lstrip('= ')
            
            # и§ЈжһҗжҸҸиҝ°е’Ңеӣҫж ?
            description = description_line
            icon = "Box"  # й»ҳи®Өеӣҫж Ү
            
            # жҸҗеҸ–еӣҫж ҮдҝЎжҒҜ [icon:IconName]
            icon_match = re.search(r'\[icon:([^\]]+)\]', description_line)
            if icon_match:
                icon = icon_match.group(1)
                # д»ҺжҸҸиҝ°дёӯз§»йҷӨеӣҫж Үж Үи®°
                description = re.sub(r'\s*\[icon:[^\]]+\]\s*', '', description)
            
            # з§»йҷӨз«ҜеҸЈдҝЎжҒҜпјҲеҰӮжһңеӯҳеңЁпјү
            description = re.sub(r'пјҲе®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈ\s+\d+[^пјү]*пј?, '', description).strip()
            
            # д»Һе®№еҷЁеҗҚжҸҗеҸ–жңҚеҠЎеҗҚпјҲеҺ»жҺү arbore- еүҚзјҖпј?
            actual_service_name = service_name
            if service_name.startswith("arbore-"):
                actual_service_name = service_name[len("arbore-"):]
            
            service_key = f"{actual_service_name}:{port}"
            # еҰӮжһңжңҚеҠЎе·ІеӯҳеңЁпјҢдҝқз•ҷз¬¬дёҖдёӘпјҲйҖҡеёёз¬¬дёҖдёӘжҳҜдё»з«ҜзӮ№пјү
            if service_key not in services_found:
                services_found[service_key] = {
                    "name": actual_service_name,
                    "port": port,
                    "endpoint": endpoint,
                    "description": description,
                    "icon": icon,
                    "location_path": location_path
                }
    
    # еҶҚеҢ№й…ҚжІЎжңүжіЁйҮҠзҡ„locationеқ—пјҲз«ҜеҸЈең?000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ…пјү
    matches = re.finditer(location_pattern_no_comment, content, re.MULTILINE | re.DOTALL)
    
    for match in matches:
        location_path = match.group(1).strip()
        service_name = match.group(2).strip()
        try:
            port = int(match.group(3))
        except ValueError:
            continue
        
        # жЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжҳҜиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎпјҲз«ҜеҸЈең?000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ…пјү
        if 7000 <= port <= 7999:
            # жҸҗеҸ–з«ҜзӮ№еҗҚз§°
            endpoint = location_path.rstrip('/').lstrip('/')
            endpoint = endpoint.lstrip('= ')
            
            # д»Һе®№еҷЁеҗҚжҸҗеҸ–жңҚеҠЎеҗ?
            actual_service_name = service_name
            if service_name.startswith("arbore-"):
                actual_service_name = service_name[len("arbore-"):]
            
            service_key = f"{actual_service_name}:{port}"
            # еҰӮжһңжңҚеҠЎе·ІеӯҳеңЁпјҢи·іиҝҮпјҲдҝқз•ҷжңүжіЁйҮҠзҡ„зүҲжң¬пјү
            if service_key not in services_found:
                services_found[service_key] = {
                    "name": actual_service_name,
                    "port": port,
                    "endpoint": endpoint,
                    "description": f"{actual_service_name}жңҚеҠЎ",  # й»ҳи®ӨжҸҸиҝ°
                    "icon": "Box",  # й»ҳи®Өеӣҫж Ү
                    "location_path": location_path
                }
    
    # е°ҶеҺ»йҮҚеҗҺзҡ„жңҚеҠЎж·»еҠ еҲ°еҲ—иЎЁ
    services = list(services_found.values())
    
    return services

def get_custom_services_metadata():
    """д»Һй…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶иҜ»еҸ–иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎзҡ„е…ғж•°жҚ®пјҲжҸҸиҝ°гҖҒеӣҫж Үзӯүпј?""
    project_root = get_project_root()
    metadata_path = os.path.join(project_root, "config", "custom-services.json")
    
    metadata = {}
    if os.path.exists(metadata_path):
        try:
            with open(metadata_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                metadata = json.load(f)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"иҜ»еҸ–иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®еӨұиҙҘ: {e}")
    
    return metadata

def save_custom_service_metadata(service_name: str, description: str, icon: str = "Box"):
    """дҝқеӯҳиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎзҡ„е…ғж•°жҚ®еҲ°й…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶"""
    project_root = get_project_root()
    config_dir = os.path.join(project_root, "config")
    os.makedirs(config_dir, exist_ok=True)
    
    metadata_path = os.path.join(config_dir, "custom-services.json")
    metadata = get_custom_services_metadata()
    
    metadata[service_name] = {
        "description": description,
        "icon": icon
    }
    
    try:
        with open(metadata_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(metadata, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"дҝқеӯҳиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®еӨұиҙҘ: {e}")

def delete_custom_service_metadata(service_name: str):
    """еҲ йҷӨиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎзҡ„е…ғж•°жҚ?""
    project_root = get_project_root()
    metadata_path = os.path.join(project_root, "config", "custom-services.json")
    
    if os.path.exists(metadata_path):
        try:
            metadata = get_custom_services_metadata()
            if service_name in metadata:
                del metadata[service_name]
                with open(metadata_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    json.dump(metadata, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"еҲ йҷӨиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®еӨұиҙҘ: {e}")

def parse_docker_compose_custom_services():
    """д»ҺDockerе®№еҷЁе’Ңй…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶и§ЈжһҗиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎдҝЎжҒҜпјҲдёҚдҫқиө–nginxе’Ңdocker-compose.ymlи§Јжһҗпј?""
    services = []
    metadata = get_custom_services_metadata()
    
    # ж–№жі•1пјҡд»ҺDocker APIиҺ·еҸ–жүҖжңүе®№еҷЁпјҢжҹҘжүҫиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠ?
    # иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎзҡ„иҜҶеҲ«ж–№ејҸпј?
    # 1. е®№еҷЁеҗҚд»Ҙ arbore- ејҖеӨ?
    # 2. з«ҜеҸЈжҳ е°„ең?000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ?
    # 3. жҲ–иҖ…жңүж Үзӯҫ arbore.custom-service=true
    
    container_list = []
    
    # е°қиҜ•дҪҝз”Ёdocker_clientиҺ·еҸ–е®№еҷЁ
    if docker_client:
        try:
            containers = docker_client.containers.list(all=True)
            for c in containers:
                container_name = c.name
                # жЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжҳҜиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎпјҲе®№еҷЁеҗҚд»Ҙarbore-ејҖеӨҙпјү
                if container_name.startswith("arbore-"):
                    service_name = container_name[len("arbore-"):]
                    
                    # иҺ·еҸ–з«ҜеҸЈжҳ е°„
                    ports = []
                    port = None
                    try:
                        port_bindings = c.attrs.get("NetworkSettings", {}).get("Ports", {})
                        for container_port, host_ports in port_bindings.items():
                            if host_ports:
                                for hp in host_ports:
                                    host_port = int(hp['HostPort'])
                                    container_port_num = int(container_port.split('/')[0])
                                    # жЈҖжҹҘз«ҜеҸЈжҳҜеҗҰеңЁ7000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ?
                                    if 7000 <= host_port <= 7999:
                                        port = host_port
                                        ports.append(f"{host_port}:{container_port_num}")
                    except:
                        pass
                    
                    # еҰӮжһңжүҫеҲ°з«ҜеҸЈең?000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ…пјҢи®ӨдёәжҳҜиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎпјҲеҸӘдҪҝз”Ёportsжҳ е°„пјҢдёҚдҪҝз”Ёexposeпј?
                    if port:
                        # иҺ·еҸ–е…ғж•°жҚ®пјҲжҸҸиҝ°гҖҒеӣҫж Үпјү
                        service_metadata = metadata.get(service_name, {})
                        description = service_metadata.get("description", f"{service_name}жңҚеҠЎ")
                        icon = service_metadata.get("icon", "Box")
                        
                        # д»Һз«ҜеҸЈжҳ е°„дёӯжҸҗеҸ–е®№еҷЁз«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҰӮжһңжңүеӨҡдёӘжҳ е°„пјҢдҪҝз”Ёз¬¬дёҖдёӘпјү
                        container_port = port  # й»ҳи®Өе®№еҷЁз«ҜеҸЈзӯүдәҺе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸ?
                        try:
                            port_bindings = c.attrs.get("NetworkSettings", {}).get("Ports", {})
                            for container_port_str, host_ports in port_bindings.items():
                                if host_ports:
                                    for hp in host_ports:
                                        if int(hp['HostPort']) == port:
                                            container_port = int(container_port_str.split('/')[0])
                                            break
                                    if container_port != port:
                                        break
                        except:
                            pass
                        
                        # д»?HostConfig иҜ»еҸ–еҶ…еӯҳйҷҗеҲ¶пјҲеӯ—иҠӮиҪ¬ MBпј?
                        memory_limit_mb = 0
                        memory_reservation_mb = 0
                        try:
                            host_config = c.attrs.get("HostConfig", {})
                            mem = host_config.get("Memory") or 0
                            if mem and int(mem) > 0:
                                memory_limit_mb = int(mem) // (1024 * 1024)
                            mem_res = host_config.get("MemoryReservation") or 0
                            if mem_res and int(mem_res) > 0:
                                memory_reservation_mb = int(mem_res) // (1024 * 1024)
                        except Exception:
                            pass
                        
                        services.append({
                            "name": service_name,
                            "port": port,  # е®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҜ№еӨ–и®ҝй—®з«ҜеҸЈпј?
                            "container_port": container_port,  # е®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸ?
                            "endpoint": f"/{service_name}",  # дёҚеҶҚдҪҝз”ЁпјҢдҝқжҢҒе…је®?
                            "description": description,
                            "icon": icon,
                            "memory_limit_mb": memory_limit_mb or None,
                            "memory_reservation_mb": memory_reservation_mb or None
                        })
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"д»ҺDocker APIиҺ·еҸ–е®№еҷЁеҲ—иЎЁеӨұиҙҘ: {e}")
    
    # ж–№жі•2пјҡFallback - д»Һdocker-compose.ymlи§ЈжһҗпјҲе…је®№ж—§ж•°жҚ®пј?
    if not services:
        project_root = get_project_root()
        docker_compose_path = os.path.join(project_root, "docker-compose.yml")
        
        if os.path.exists(docker_compose_path):
            try:
                with open(docker_compose_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    content = f.read()
                
                # еҢ№й…ҚжүҖжңүжңҚеҠЎе®ҡд№үеқ—
                service_pattern = r'^\s*([a-z0-9-]+)\s*:.*?(?=^\s*[a-z]|^\s*networks:|^\s*volumes:|$)'
                service_matches = re.finditer(service_pattern, content, re.MULTILINE | re.DOTALL)
                
                for match in service_matches:
                    service_name = match.group(1).strip()
                    service_block = match.group(0)
                    
                    # жҸҗеҸ–з«ҜеҸЈй…ҚзҪ®пјҲports: - "host_port:container_port"пј?
                    ports_match = re.search(r'ports:\s*\n\s*-\s*"(\d+):(\d+)"', service_block)
                    if not ports_match:
                        continue
                    
                    host_port = int(ports_match.group(1))
                    container_port = int(ports_match.group(2))
                    
                    # еҸӘеӨ„зҗҶе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈең?000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ…зҡ„жңҚеҠЎ
                    if not (7000 <= host_port <= 7999):
                        continue
                    
                    # дҪҝз”Ёhost_portдҪңдёәеҜ№еӨ–з«ҜеҸЈ
                    port = host_port
                    
                    # жҸҗеҸ–жіЁйҮҠиЎҢпјҲеҸҜиғҪеҢ…еҗ«жҸҸиҝ°е’Ңеӣҫж Үпјү
                    comment_match = re.search(r'#\s*([^\n]+)', service_block)
                    description_line = comment_match.group(1).strip() if comment_match else ""
                    
                    # дјҳе…ҲдҪҝз”Ёй…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶дёӯзҡ„е…ғж•°жҚ?
                    service_metadata = metadata.get(service_name, {})
                    if service_metadata:
                        description = service_metadata.get("description", description_line)
                        icon = service_metadata.get("icon", "Box")
                    else:
                        # д»ҺжіЁйҮҠи§Јжһ?
                        description = description_line
                        icon = "Box"
                        
                        # жҸҗеҸ–еӣҫж ҮдҝЎжҒҜ [icon:IconName]
                        icon_match = re.search(r'\[icon:([^\]]+)\]', description_line)
                        if icon_match:
                            icon = icon_match.group(1)
                            description = re.sub(r'\s*\[icon:[^\]]+\]\s*', '', description)
                        
                        # з§»йҷӨз«ҜеҸЈзӣёе…іжҸҸиҝ°
                        description = re.sub(r'пј?*з«ҜеҸЈ.*пј?, '', description).strip()
                        if not description:
                            description = f"{service_name}жңҚеҠЎ"
                    
                        # д»?compose еқ—и§ЈжһҗеҶ…еӯҳйҷҗеҲ?
                        memory_limit_mb = None
                        memory_reservation_mb = None
                        mem_limit_match = re.search(r'mem_limit:\s*([^\n]+)', service_block)
                        if mem_limit_match:
                            memory_limit_mb = _parse_memory_to_mb(mem_limit_match.group(1).strip())
                        mem_res_match = re.search(r'mem_reservation:\s*([^\n]+)', service_block)
                        if mem_res_match:
                            memory_reservation_mb = _parse_memory_to_mb(mem_res_match.group(1).strip())
                    
                    services.append({
                        "name": service_name,
                        "port": port,  # е®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҜ№еӨ–и®ҝй—®з«ҜеҸЈпј?
                        "container_port": container_port,  # е®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸ?
                        "endpoint": f"/{service_name}",  # дёҚеҶҚдҪҝз”ЁпјҢдҝқжҢҒе…је®?
                        "description": description,
                        "icon": icon,
                        "memory_limit_mb": memory_limit_mb if (memory_limit_mb and memory_limit_mb > 0) else None,
                        "memory_reservation_mb": memory_reservation_mb if (memory_reservation_mb and memory_reservation_mb > 0) else None
                    })
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"д»Һdocker-compose.ymlи§ЈжһҗжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: {e}")
    
    return services

def get_available_port():
    """иҺ·еҸ–дёӢдёҖдёӘеҸҜз”Ёз«ҜеҸЈпјҲ7000-7999пј?""
    project_root = get_project_root()
    docker_compose_path = os.path.join(project_root, "docker-compose.yml")
    
    used_ports = set()
    
    # д»Һdocker-compose.ymlдёӯжҸҗеҸ–е·ІдҪҝз”Ёзҡ„з«ҜеҸ?
    if os.path.exists(docker_compose_path):
        with open(docker_compose_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            content = f.read()
            # еҢ№й…Қ ports: - "port:port" ж јејҸпјҲзӣҙжҺҘз«ҜеҸЈжҳ е°„пјү
            port_matches = re.findall(r'ports:\s*\n\s*-\s*"(\d+):', content)
            for port_str in port_matches:
                port = int(port_str)
                if 7000 <= port <= 7999:
                    used_ports.add(port)
            # д№ҹеҢ№й…?PORT=ж•°еӯ— зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸ
            port_env_matches = re.findall(r'PORT=(\d+)', content)
            for port_str in port_env_matches:
                port = int(port_str)
                if 7000 <= port <= 7999:
                    used_ports.add(port)
    
    # жҹҘжүҫз¬¬дёҖдёӘеҸҜз”Ёз«ҜеҸ?
    for port in range(7000, 8000):
        if port not in used_ports:
            return port
    
    raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="жІЎжңүеҸҜз”Ёзҡ„з«ҜеҸЈпјҲ7000-7999иҢғеӣҙе·Іж»Ўпј?)

def _memory_mb_to_docker_str(mb: int) -> str:
    """е°?MB иҪ¬дёә Docker еҸҜз”Ёзҡ„еӯ—з¬ҰдёІпјҢеҰӮ 4096 -> '4g'пј?12 -> '512m'"""
    if mb <= 0:
        return ""
    if mb >= 1024:
        return f"{mb // 1024}g"
    return f"{mb}m"

def _parse_memory_to_mb(s) -> int:
    """и§Јжһҗ compose дёӯзҡ„ mem_limit/mem_reservation еҖјдёә MBгҖӮеҰӮ '4g'->4096, '512m'->512"""
    if s is None:
        return 0
    s = str(s).strip().lower()
    if not s:
        return 0
    if s.endswith("g"):
        return int(float(s[:-1]) * 1024)
    if s.endswith("m"):
        return int(float(s[:-1]))
    try:
        return int(float(s))
    except ValueError:
        return 0

def add_service_to_docker_compose(service_name: str, port: int, image_name: str, config_dir: str = None, volumes: list = None, container_port: int = None, health_check_path: str = "/health", memory_limit_mb: int = None, memory_reservation_mb: int = None):
    """ж·»еҠ жңҚеҠЎеҲ°docker-compose.yml
    
    Args:
        service_name: жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°
        port: е®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҜ№еӨ–и®ҝй—®з«ҜеҸЈпј?
        image_name: й•ңеғҸеҗҚз§°
        config_dir: й…ҚзҪ®зӣ®еҪ•
        volumes: еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪеҲ—иЎ?
        container_port: е®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҰӮжһңдёәNoneпјҢеҲҷдҪҝз”ЁportпјҢеҚіport:portжҳ е°„пј?
        health_check_path: еҒҘеә·жЈҖжҹҘи·Ҝеҫ„пјҢй»ҳи®Ө/healthгҖӮж— /healthзҡ„жңҚеҠЎпјҲеҰӮbrowserlessпјүеҸҜдј?/"
        memory_limit_mb: еҶ…еӯҳйҷҗеҲ¶пјҲMBпјүпјҢеҸҜйҖүпјҢеҶҷе…Ҙ mem_limitпјҢйҮҚеҗҜеҗҺз”ҹж•Ҳ
        memory_reservation_mb: еҶ…еӯҳйў„з•ҷпјҲMBпјүпјҢеҸҜйҖүпјҢеҶҷе…Ҙ mem_reservation
    """
    project_root = get_project_root()
    docker_compose_path = os.path.join(project_root, "docker-compose.yml")
    
    if not os.path.exists(docker_compose_path):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="docker-compose.ymlж–Үд»¶дёҚеӯҳең?)
    
    # иҜ»еҸ–зҺ°жңүй…ҚзҪ®
    with open(docker_compose_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # жЈҖжҹҘжңҚеҠЎжҳҜеҗҰе·ІеӯҳеңЁпјҲдҪҝз”ЁжӯЈеҲҷеҢ№й…Қе®Ңж•ҙзҡ„жңҚеҠЎе®ҡд№үпјҢйҳІжӯўдёҚе®Ңж•ҙй…ҚзҪ®пј?
    # еҢ№й…ҚжңҚеҠЎеҗҚе®ҡд№үиЎҢпјҲеҢ…жӢ¬жіЁйҮҠпјү
    service_pattern = rf'(#\s*[^\n]*{re.escape(service_name)}[^\n]*\n\s+)?{re.escape(service_name)}\s*:'
    if re.search(service_pattern, content, re.MULTILINE):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"жңҚеҠЎ {service_name} е·ІеӯҳеңЁдәҺdocker-compose.yml")
    
    # з”ҹжҲҗenv_fileй…ҚзҪ®пјҲеҰӮжһңжңүй…ҚзҪ®зӣ®еҪ•пј?
    env_file_config = ""
    if config_dir:
        config_rel_path = os.path.relpath(config_dir, project_root).replace('\\', '/')
        env_file_config = f"    env_file:\n      - ./{config_rel_path}/.env\n"
    
    # з”ҹжҲҗvolumesй…ҚзҪ®пјҲеҰӮжһңжңүжҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®пј?
    volumes_config = ""
    if volumes and len(volumes) > 0:
        volumes_config = "    volumes:\n"
        for volume in volumes:
            # volumesж јејҸ: ["host_path:container_path"] жҲ?["host_path:container_path:ro"]
            volumes_config += f"      - {volume}\n"
    
    # з”ҹжҲҗеҶ…еӯҳйҷҗеҲ¶й…ҚзҪ®пјҲеҸҜйҖүпјүпјҢйҮҚеҗҜеҗҺз”ҹж•Ҳ
    memory_config = ""
    if memory_limit_mb and memory_limit_mb > 0:
        memory_config += f"    mem_limit: {_memory_mb_to_docker_str(memory_limit_mb)}\n"
    if memory_reservation_mb and memory_reservation_mb > 0:
        memory_config += f"    mem_reservation: {_memory_mb_to_docker_str(memory_reservation_mb)}\n"
    
    # зЎ®е®ҡе®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҰӮжһңжңӘжҢҮе®ҡпјҢдҪҝз”Ёе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈпјү
    actual_container_port = container_port if container_port is not None else port
    
    # з”ҹжҲҗжңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ®пјҲзӣҙжҺҘз«ҜеҸЈжҳ е°„пјҢдёҚйҖҡиҝҮnginxпј?
    service_config = f"""
  # {service_name}пјҲиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎпјҢзӣҙжҺҘз«ҜеҸЈи®ҝй—?{port}пј?
  {service_name}:
    image: {image_name}
    container_name: arbore-{service_name}
    restart: unless-stopped
{memory_config}{env_file_config}{volumes_config}    environment:
      - PORT={actual_container_port}
    ports:
      - "{port}:{actual_container_port}"  # е®ҝдё»жңә{port}жҳ е°„еҲ°е®№еҷЁ{actual_container_port}з«ҜеҸЈ
    networks:
      - arbore-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "curl -f http://localhost:{actual_container_port}{health_check_path} || exit 1"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 30s
"""
    
    # еңЁnetworksе®ҡд№үд№ӢеүҚжҸ’е…ҘжңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ®
    # еҢ№й…Қж–Үд»¶зә§еҲ«зҡ„networks:е®ҡд№үпјҲеүҚйқўеҸҜиғҪжңүз©әиЎҢпјҢеҗҺйқўи·ҹзқҖarbore-networkзӯүпјү
    # дҪҝз”ЁжӣҙзІҫзЎ®зҡ„жЁЎејҸпјҡеҢ№й…ҚзӢ¬з«Ӣзҡ„networks:иЎҢпјҲдёҚеңЁservicesеҶ…йғЁпјҢиЎҢйҰ–еҸҜиғҪжңүз©әж јпј?
    # зЎ®дҝқеҢ№й…Қзҡ„жҳҜж–Үд»¶зә§еҲ«зҡ„networks:пјҢиҖҢдёҚжҳҜжңҚеҠЎеҶ…йғЁзҡ„networks:
    networks_pattern = r'(\n^networks:\s*$)'
    networks_match = re.search(networks_pattern, content, re.MULTILINE)
    
    if networks_match:
        # жЈҖжҹҘnetworks:д№ӢеүҚжҳҜеҗҰжңүе…¶д»–жңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ?
        before_networks = content[:networks_match.start()]
        # зЎ®дҝқжҸ’е…ҘдҪҚзҪ®жӯЈзЎ®пјҲеңЁжңҖеҗҺдёҖдёӘжңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ®д№ӢеҗҺпјҢnetworksд№ӢеүҚпј?
        # еңЁnetworks:д№ӢеүҚжҸ’е…ҘжңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ®
        content = content[:networks_match.start()] + service_config + content[networks_match.start():]
    else:
        # еҰӮжһңжүҫдёҚеҲ°networksпјҢжЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжңүservices:е®ҡд№ү
        services_pattern = r'(\n^services:\s*$)'
        services_match = re.search(services_pattern, content, re.MULTILINE)
        if services_match:
            # еңЁservices:д№ӢеҗҺжҸ’е…Ҙ
            content = content[:services_match.end()] + service_config + content[services_match.end():]
        else:
            # ж·»еҠ еҲ°ж–Үд»¶жң«е°?
            content = content.rstrip() + "\n" + service_config
    
    # йӘҢиҜҒжҸ’е…ҘеҗҺжІЎжңүйҮҚеӨҚпјҲе®үе…ЁжЈҖжҹҘпјү
    service_count = len(re.findall(rf'^{re.escape(service_name)}\s*:', content, re.MULTILINE))
    if service_count > 1:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"й…ҚзҪ®жҸ’е…ҘеҗҺжЈҖжөӢеҲ°йҮҚеӨҚзҡ„жңҚеҠЎе®ҡд№үпјҲ{service_count}дёӘпјүпјҢиҜ·жЈҖжҹҘdocker-compose.yml")
    
    # еҶҷеӣһж–Үд»¶
    with open(docker_compose_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)

def add_service_to_nginx(service_name: str, port: int, endpoint: str, description: str, icon: str = "Box"):
    """ж·»еҠ жңҚеҠЎеҲ°nginxй…ҚзҪ®"""
    project_root = get_project_root()
    nginx_config_path = os.path.join(project_root, "nginx", "conf.d", "default.conf")
    
    if not os.path.exists(nginx_config_path):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="nginxй…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶дёҚеӯҳең?)
    
    # иҜ»еҸ–зҺ°жңүй…ҚзҪ®
    with open(nginx_config_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # и§„иҢғеҢ–з«ҜзӮ№и·Ҝеҫ?
    if not endpoint.startswith('/'):
        endpoint = '/' + endpoint
    if not endpoint.endswith('/'):
        endpoint = endpoint + '/'
    
    # жЈҖжҹҘз«ҜзӮ№жҳҜеҗҰе·ІеӯҳеңЁпјҲдҪҝз”ЁжӯЈеҲҷеҢ№й…Қе®Ңж•ҙзҡ„locationеқ—пјҢйҳІжӯўдёҚе®Ңж•ҙй…ҚзҪ®пјү
    endpoint_escaped = re.escape(endpoint)
    # еҢ№й…Қе®Ңж•ҙзҡ„locationеқ—пјҲеҢ…жӢ¬жіЁйҮҠе’Ңй…ҚзҪ®пјү
    existing_pattern = rf'(#\s*[^\n]*{re.escape(service_name)}[^\n]*\n\s+)?location\s+{endpoint_escaped}\s*\{{'
    if re.search(existing_pattern, content, re.MULTILINE):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"з«ҜзӮ№ {endpoint} е·ІеӯҳеңЁдәҺnginxй…ҚзҪ®дё?)
    
    # з”ҹжҲҗnginxй…ҚзҪ®пјҲеңЁжҸҸиҝ°дёӯеҢ…еҗ«еӣҫж ҮдҝЎжҒҜпјү
    # жіЁж„Ҹпјҡе®№еҷЁеҗҚз§°жҳҜ arbore-{service_name}пјҢдёҚжҳ?{service_name}
    container_name = f"arbore-{service_name}"
    nginx_config = f"""
    # {description} [icon:{icon}]пјҲе®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈ {port}пјҢйҖҡиҝҮ nginx з»ҹдёҖеҜ№еӨ–пј?
    location {endpoint} {{
        proxy_pass http://{container_name}:{port}/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }}
"""
    
    # еңЁй»ҳи®Өи·Ҝз”ұд№ӢеүҚжҸ’е…Ҙй…ҚзҪ?
    # еҢ№й…Қ "# й»ҳи®Өи·Ҝз”ұ" жіЁйҮҠпјҲеҗҺйқўеҸҜиғҪжңүе…¶д»–ж–Үеӯ—пјүе’Ң location / { еқ?
    # дҪҝз”ЁDOTALLжЁЎејҸеҢ№й…ҚпјҢзЎ®дҝқиғҪеҢ№й…Қи·ЁиЎҢзҡ„locationеқ?
    default_location_pattern = r'(\n\s+# й»ҳи®Өи·Ҝз”ұ[^\n]*\n\s+location\s+/\s+\{.*?\})'
    if re.search(default_location_pattern, content, re.DOTALL):
        # еңЁеҢ№й…ҚеҲ°зҡ„еҶ…е®№д№ӢеүҚжҸ’е…Ҙж–°й…ҚзҪ®пјҲnginx_configе·Із»ҸеҢ…еҗ«ејҖеӨҙзҡ„жҚўиЎҢпј?
        # дҪҝз”Ёcount=1зЎ®дҝқеҸӘжӣҝжҚўдёҖж¬?
        content = re.sub(default_location_pattern, nginx_config + r'\1', content, count=1, flags=re.DOTALL)
    else:
        # еҰӮжһңжүҫдёҚеҲ°й»ҳи®Өи·Ҝз”ұжіЁйҮҠпјҢе°қиҜ•еҢ№й…Қ location / { еқ—пјҲеңЁserverеқ—еҶ…пј?
        # дҪҝз”ЁDOTALLжЁЎејҸеҢ№й…ҚеӨҡиЎҢеҶ…е®№
        location_root_pattern = r'(\n\s+location\s+/\s+\{.*?return\s+\d+.*?\})'
        if re.search(location_root_pattern, content, re.DOTALL):
            # дҪҝз”Ёcount=1зЎ®дҝқеҸӘжӣҝжҚўдёҖж¬?
            content = re.sub(location_root_pattern, nginx_config + r'\1', content, count=1, flags=re.DOTALL)
        else:
            # жңҖеҗҺе°қиҜ•пјҡеңЁserverеқ—зҡ„жңҖеҗҺдёҖдёӘ}д№ӢеүҚжҸ’е…ҘпјҲеңЁserverеқ—еҶ…пј?
            # еҢ№й…Қserverеқ—з»“жқҹеүҚзҡ„жңҖеҗҺдёҖдёӘ}пјҢзЎ®дҝқеңЁserverеқ—еҶ…
            server_end_pattern = r'(\n\s+\}\s*$)'
            if re.search(server_end_pattern, content, re.MULTILINE):
                # дҪҝз”Ёcount=1зЎ®дҝқеҸӘжӣҝжҚўдёҖж¬ЎпјҲд»ҺеҗҺеҫҖеүҚеҢ№й…ҚжңҖеҗҺдёҖдёӘ}пј?
                matches = list(re.finditer(server_end_pattern, content, re.MULTILINE))
                if matches:
                    # жӣҝжҚўжңҖеҗҺдёҖдёӘеҢ№й…ҚпјҲserverеқ—зҡ„з»“жқҹпј?
                    last_match = matches[-1]
                    content = content[:last_match.start()] + nginx_config + content[last_match.start():]
            else:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="ж— жі•жүҫеҲ°nginxй…ҚзҪ®зҡ„жҸ’е…ҘдҪҚзҪ?)
    
    # йӘҢиҜҒжҸ’е…ҘеҗҺжІЎжңүйҮҚеӨҚпјҲе®үе…ЁжЈҖжҹҘпјү
    location_count = len(re.findall(rf'location\s+{re.escape(endpoint)}\s*\{{', content))
    if location_count > 1:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"й…ҚзҪ®жҸ’е…ҘеҗҺжЈҖжөӢеҲ°йҮҚеӨҚзҡ„locationеқ—пјҲ{location_count}дёӘпјүпјҢиҜ·жЈҖжҹҘnginxй…ҚзҪ®")
    
    # еҶҷеӣһж–Үд»¶
