    with open(nginx_config_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)

def remove_service_from_docker_compose(service_name: str):
    """д»Һdocker-compose.ymlдёӯеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎпјҢдҪҝз”ЁйҖҗиЎҢи§ЈжһҗзЎ®дҝқеҮҶзЎ®жҖ?""
    project_root = get_project_root()
    docker_compose_path = os.path.join(project_root, "docker-compose.yml")
    
    if not os.path.exists(docker_compose_path):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="docker-compose.ymlж–Үд»¶дёҚеӯҳең?)
    
    with open(docker_compose_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        lines = f.readlines()
    
    new_lines = []
    in_service_block = False
    service_indent = -1
    service_found = False
    
    i = 0
    while i < len(lines):
        line = lines[i]
        stripped_line = line.lstrip()
        current_indent = len(line) - len(stripped_line)
        
        # жЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжҳҜзӣ®ж ҮжңҚеҠЎе®ҡд№үиЎҢпјҲдҫӢеҰӮ: service-name:пј?
        if stripped_line.startswith(f"{service_name}:"):
            # жүҫеҲ°зӣ®ж ҮжңҚеҠЎпјҢж Үи®°ејҖе§ӢеҲ йҷ?
            service_found = True
            in_service_block = True
            service_indent = current_indent
            print(f"жүҫеҲ°жңҚеҠЎ '{service_name}' зҡ„иө·е§ӢиЎҢ: {i+1}, зј©иҝӣ: {service_indent}")
            
            # жЈҖжҹҘеүҚдёҖиЎҢжҳҜеҗҰжҳҜжіЁйҮҠпјҢеҰӮжһңжҳҜпјҢд№ҹиҰҒеҲ йҷ?
            if len(new_lines) > 0 and new_lines[-1].strip().startswith('#'):
                # еҲ йҷӨжіЁйҮҠиЎ?
                new_lines.pop()
                # еҰӮжһңжіЁйҮҠеүҚиҝҳжңүз©әиЎҢпјҢд№ҹеҲ йҷ?
                if len(new_lines) > 0 and new_lines[-1].strip() == '':
                    new_lines.pop()
            
            # и·іиҝҮжңҚеҠЎе®ҡд№үиЎ?
            i += 1
            continue
        
        # еҰӮжһңеңЁжңҚеҠЎеқ—еҶ?
        if in_service_block:
            # еҰӮжһңеҪ“еүҚиЎҢзј©иҝӣе°ҸдәҺжҲ–зӯүдәҺжңҚеҠЎеқ—зҡ„зј©иҝӣпјҢдё”дёҚжҳҜз©әиЎҢпјҢиҜҙжҳҺжңҚеҠЎеқ—з»“жқҹ
            if current_indent <= service_indent and stripped_line and not stripped_line.startswith('#'):
                # жңҚеҠЎеқ—з»“жқ?
                in_service_block = False
                service_indent = -1
                # еҰӮжһңеҪ“еүҚиЎҢжҳҜеҸҰдёҖдёӘжңҚеҠЎе®ҡд№үжҲ–йЎ¶зә§й”®пјҢеҲҷж·»еҠ?
                if stripped_line.rstrip().endswith(':') or stripped_line.startswith('networks:') or stripped_line.startswith('volumes:'):
                    new_lines.append(line)
                i += 1
                continue
            else:
                # д»ҚеңЁжңҚеҠЎеқ—еҶ…пјҢи·іиҝҮжӯӨиЎ?
                i += 1
                continue
        
        # дёҚеңЁжңҚеҠЎеқ—еҶ…пјҢж·»еҠ жӯӨиЎ?
        new_lines.append(line)
        i += 1
    
    # жЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰжүҫеҲ°жңҚеҠ?
    if not service_found:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"еңЁdocker-compose.ymlдёӯжңӘжүҫеҲ°жңҚеҠЎ '{service_name}' зҡ„й…ҚзҪ?)
    
    # еҶҷеӣһж–Үд»¶
    with open(docker_compose_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.writelines(new_lines)
    
    print(f"е·Ід»Һdocker-compose.ymlеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎ '{service_name}' зҡ„й…ҚзҪ?)

def remove_service_from_nginx(service_name: str, endpoint: str):
    """д»Һnginxй…ҚзҪ®дёӯеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠ?""
    project_root = get_project_root()
    nginx_config_path = os.path.join(project_root, "nginx", "conf.d", "default.conf")
    
    if not os.path.exists(nginx_config_path):
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="nginxй…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶дёҚеӯҳең?)
    
    with open(nginx_config_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    original_content = content
    
    # е®№еҷЁеҗҚжҳҜ arbore-{service_name}
    container_name = f"arbore-{service_name}"
    
    # и§„иҢғеҢ–endpointи·Ҝеҫ„пјҲеҢ№й…Қж—¶йңҖиҰҒиҖғиҷ‘еҗ„з§Қж јејҸпј?
    endpoint_normalized = endpoint.rstrip('/')
    if not endpoint_normalized.startswith('/'):
        endpoint_normalized = '/' + endpoint_normalized
    
    # ж–№жі•1: йҖҡиҝҮе®№еҷЁеҗҚеҢ№й…ҚпјҲproxy_passдёӯзҡ„е®№еҷЁеҗҚпјү
    # еҢ№й…Қе®Ңж•ҙзҡ„locationеқ—пјҢеҢ…жӢ¬жіЁйҮҠе’Ңй…ҚзҪ?
    # ж јејҸ: # жіЁйҮҠ\n    location /path { ... proxy_pass http://arbore-service-name:port/ ... }
    pattern1 = rf'(\n\s+#[^\n]*\n\s+location\s+[^{{]*\{{[^}}]*proxy_pass\s+http://{re.escape(container_name)}:[^/\s]+[^}}]*\}})'
    content = re.sub(pattern1, '', content, flags=re.MULTILINE | re.DOTALL)
    
    # ж–№жі•2: йҖҡиҝҮendpointи·Ҝеҫ„еҢ№й…ҚпјҲеҰӮжһңж–№жі?жІЎеҢ№й…ҚеҲ°пј?
    if content == original_content:
        # еҢ№й…Қlocationеқ—пјҢеҢ…жӢ¬жіЁйҮҠ
        endpoint_escaped = re.escape(endpoint_normalized)
        pattern2 = rf'(\n\s+#[^\n]*\n\s+location\s+{endpoint_escaped}[^{{]*\{{[^}}]*\}})'
        content = re.sub(pattern2, '', content, flags=re.MULTILINE | re.DOTALL)
    
    # ж–№жі•3: д№ҹеҲ йҷӨеҸҜиғҪзҡ„ж №и·Ҝеҫ„йҮҚе®ҡеҗ‘пјҲlocation = /pathпј?
    redirect_pattern = rf'(\n\s+location\s+=\s+{re.escape(endpoint_normalized)}\s+\{{[^}}]*\}})'
    content = re.sub(redirect_pattern, '', content, flags=re.MULTILINE | re.DOTALL)
    
    # йӘҢиҜҒжҳҜеҗҰзңҹзҡ„еҲ йҷӨдәҶеҶ…е®?
    if content == original_content:
        print(f"иӯҰе‘Ҡ: жңӘиғҪд»Һnginxй…ҚзҪ®дёӯеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠ?{service_name} (е®№еҷЁеҗ? {container_name}, endpoint: {endpoint_normalized})")
        print(f"е°қиҜ•еҢ№й…Қзҡ„е®№еҷЁеҗҚ: {container_name}")
        print(f"е°қиҜ•еҢ№й…Қзҡ„endpoint: {endpoint_normalized}")
        # жү“еҚ°й…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶еҶ…е®№д»Ҙдҫҝи°ғиҜ•
        print("еҪ“еүҚnginxй…ҚзҪ®зүҮж®ө:")
        lines = original_content.split('\n')
        for i, line in enumerate(lines):
            if container_name in line or endpoint_normalized in line or service_name in line:
                print(f"Line {i+1}: {line}")
    else:
        print(f"жҲҗеҠҹд»Һnginxй…ҚзҪ®дёӯеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠ?{service_name}")
    
    with open(nginx_config_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)

@app.get("/api/v1/custom-services")
async def get_custom_services():
    """иҺ·еҸ–жүҖжңүиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎпјҲеҢ…еҗ«е®№еҷЁзҠ¶жҖҒпјү"""
    try:
        services = parse_docker_compose_custom_services()
        
        # жҹҘиҜўжҜҸдёӘжңҚеҠЎзҡ„е®№еҷЁзҠ¶жҖ?
        container_dict = {}
        container_status_dict = {}  # еӯҳеӮЁе®№еҷЁзҠ¶жҖҒдҝЎжҒ?
        
        if docker_client:
            try:
                containers = docker_client.containers.list(all=True)
                for c in containers:
                    # е®№еҷЁеҗҚж јеј? arbore-{service_name}
                    if c.name.startswith("arbore-"):
                        service_name = c.name[len("arbore-"):]
                        container_dict[service_name] = c
                        # жҸҗеҸ–зҠ¶жҖҒдҝЎжҒ?
                        try:
                            health_info = c.attrs.get("State", {}).get("Health", {})
                            health = health_info.get("Status", "unknown")
                            
                            # еҰӮжһңеҒҘеә·зҠ¶жҖҒжҳҜstartingпјҢжЈҖжҹҘжҳҜеҗҰи¶…иҝҮstart_period
                            if health == "starting":
                                started_at = health_info.get("Start", "")
                                if started_at:
                                    try:
                                        from datetime import datetime
                                        start_time = datetime.fromisoformat(started_at.replace('Z', '+00:00'))
                                        elapsed = (datetime.now(start_time.tzinfo) - start_time).total_seconds()
                                        # еҰӮжһңи¶…иҝҮ60з§’иҝҳеңЁstartingпјҢеҸҜиғҪжҳҜеҒҘеә·жЈҖжҹҘжңүй—®йўҳпјҢж”№дёәunknown
                                        if elapsed > 60:
                                            health = "unknown"
                                    except:
                                        pass
                        except:
                            health = "unknown"
                        
                        container_status_dict[service_name] = {
                            'status': c.status,
                            'container_id': c.id[:12],
                            'health': health,
                            'attrs': c.attrs
                        }
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"жҹҘиҜўе®№еҷЁзҠ¶жҖҒеӨұиҙ? {e}")
        else:
            # Fallback: дҪҝз”Ёdockerе‘Ҫд»ӨжҹҘиҜў
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ['docker', 'ps', '-a', '--format', '{{.Names}}\t{{.Status}}\t{{.ID}}'],
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True,
                    timeout=10
                )
                if result.returncode == 0:
                    for line in result.stdout.strip().split('\n'):
                        if not line.strip():
                            continue
                        parts = line.split('\t')
                        if len(parts) >= 3:
                            container_name = parts[0]
                            status_str = parts[1]
                            container_id = parts[2][:12]
                            
                            if container_name.startswith("arbore-"):
                                service_name = container_name[len("arbore-"):]
                                # и§ЈжһҗзҠ¶жҖ?
                                if 'Up' in status_str:
                                    status = 'running'
                                elif 'Exited' in status_str:
                                    status = 'exited'
                                else:
                                    status = status_str.lower()
                                
                                container_status_dict[service_name] = {
                                    'status': status,
                                    'container_id': container_id,
                                    'health': 'unknown',  # docker psж— жі•иҺ·еҸ–еҒҘеә·зҠ¶жҖ?
                                    'attrs': None
                                }
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"дҪҝз”Ёdockerе‘Ҫд»ӨжҹҘиҜўе®№еҷЁзҠ¶жҖҒеӨұиҙ? {e}")
        
        # дёәжҜҸдёӘжңҚеҠЎж·»еҠ е®№еҷЁзҠ¶жҖҒдҝЎжҒ?
        for service in services:
            service_name = service['name']
            container_name = f"arbore-{service_name}"
            container_info = container_status_dict.get(service_name)
            
            if container_info:
                # е®№еҷЁеӯҳеңЁпјҢиҺ·еҸ–зҠ¶жҖ?
                service['status'] = container_info['status']
                service['container_id'] = container_info['container_id']
                service['health'] = container_info['health']
                
                # иҺ·еҸ–з«ҜеҸЈжҳ е°„пјҲеҰӮжһңжңүattrsпј?
                if container_info.get('attrs'):
                    try:
                        port_bindings = container_info['attrs'].get("NetworkSettings", {}).get("Ports", {})
                        ports = []
                        for container_port, host_ports in port_bindings.items():
                            if host_ports:
                                for hp in host_ports:
                                    ports.append(f"{hp['HostPort']}:{container_port.split('/')[0]}")
                        service['ports_display'] = ports
                    except:
                        service['ports_display'] = []
                else:
                    service['ports_display'] = []
            else:
                # е®№еҷЁдёҚеӯҳең?
                service['status'] = "not_found"
                service['health'] = "unknown"
                service['container_id'] = None
                service['ports_display'] = []
        
        return {"services": services}
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"иҺ·еҸ–иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎеҲ—иЎЁеӨұиҙ? {str(e)}")

@app.post("/api/v1/custom-services/validate")
async def validate_custom_service(
    name: str = Form(...),
    port: int = Form(...),
    endpoint: str = Form(None)  # е·ІеәҹејғпјҢдҝқз•ҷд»ҘдҝқжҢҒеҗ‘еҗҺе…је®?
):
    """йӘҢиҜҒиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎеҸӮж•°пјҲеңЁдёҠдј ж–Үд»¶д№ӢеүҚи°ғз”ЁпјүгҖӮйңҖи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжңүж•Ҳж–№еҸҜж·»еҠ жңҚеҠЎгҖ?""
    try:
        _license_valid_or_403()
    except HTTPException:
        raise

    try:
        # йӘҢиҜҒз«ҜеҸЈиҢғеӣҙпј?000-7999пј?
        if not (7000 <= port <= 7999):
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎз«ҜеҸЈеҝ…йЎ»еңЁ7000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ?)
        
        # йӘҢиҜҒжңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°ж јејҸ
        if not re.match(r'^[a-z0-9-]+$', name):
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°еҸӘиғҪеҢ…еҗ«е°ҸеҶҷеӯ—жҜҚгҖҒж•°еӯ—е’Ңиҝһеӯ—з¬?)
        
        # йӘҢиҜҒе”ҜдёҖжҖ§пјҲеҸӘжЈҖжҹҘз«ҜеҸЈпјҢдёҚеҶҚйңҖиҰҒз«ҜзӮ№пјү
        existing_services = parse_docker_compose_custom_services()
        
        # жЈҖжҹҘжңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°жҳҜеҗҰе·ІеӯҳеңЁ
        for service in existing_services:
            if service['name'] == name:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§° '{name}' е·Іеӯҳең?)
        
        # жЈҖжҹҘз«ҜеҸЈжҳҜеҗҰе·Іиў«дҪҝз”?
        for service in existing_services:
            if service['port'] == port:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"з«ҜеҸЈ {port} е·Іиў«жңҚеҠЎ '{service['name']}' дҪҝз”Ё")
        
        return {
            "valid": True,
            "message": "йӘҢиҜҒйҖҡиҝҮ"
        }
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"йӘҢиҜҒеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")

@app.post("/api/v1/custom-services/upload")
async def upload_custom_service(
    file: UploadFile = File(...),
    name: str = Form(...),
    port: int = Form(...),
    container_port: int = Form(None),  # е®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҸҜйҖүпјҢеҰӮжһңдёҚжҢҮе®ҡеҲҷдҪҝз”Ёportпј?
    endpoint: str = Form(None),  # е·ІеәҹејғпјҢдҝқз•ҷд»ҘдҝқжҢҒеҗ‘еҗҺе…је®№пјҢзҺ°еңЁйҖҡиҝҮз«ҜеҸЈзӣҙжҺҘи®ҝй—®
    description: str = Form(...),
    icon: str = Form("Box"),
    env_vars: str = Form(None, description="зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸJSONй…ҚзҪ®пјҢж јеј? {\"KEY1\":\"value1\",\"KEY2\":\"value2\"}"),
    volumes: str = Form(None, description="еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪJSONй…ҚзҪ®пјҢж јеј? [\"host_path:container_path\", \"host_path2:container_path2:ro\"]"),
    memory_limit_mb: int = Form(None),
    memory_reservation_mb: int = Form(None)
):
    """дёҠдј Dockerй•ңеғҸtarж–Үд»¶е№¶йғЁзҪІжңҚеҠЎгҖӮйңҖи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжңүж•Ҳж–№еҸҜж·»еҠ жңҚеҠЎгҖ?""
    try:
        _license_valid_or_403()
    except HTTPException:
        raise

    try:
        # ========== з¬¬дёҖжӯҘпјҡеҝ«йҖҹйӘҢиҜҒпјҲеңЁж–Үд»¶дёҠдј д№ӢеүҚпјҢйҒҝе…ҚжөӘиҙ№ж—¶й—ҙе’Ңиө„жәҗпјү==========
        # йӘҢиҜҒз«ҜеҸЈиҢғеӣҙпј?000-7999пј?
        if not (7000 <= port <= 7999):
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎз«ҜеҸЈеҝ…йЎ»еңЁ7000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ?)
        
        # йӘҢиҜҒжңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°ж јејҸ
        if not re.match(r'^[a-z0-9-]+$', name):
            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°еҸӘиғҪеҢ…еҗ«е°ҸеҶҷеӯ—жҜҚгҖҒж•°еӯ—е’Ңиҝһеӯ—з¬?)
        
        # еҝ«йҖҹйӘҢиҜҒе”ҜдёҖжҖ§пјҡжңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°гҖҒз«ҜеҸЈеҝ…йЎ»е”ҜдёҖпјҲеңЁж–Үд»¶ж“ҚдҪңд№ӢеүҚпј?
        # жіЁж„ҸпјҡиҝҷйҮҢе…ҲиҝӣиЎҢйӘҢиҜҒпјҢеҰӮжһңеӨұиҙҘеҸҜд»Ҙз«ӢеҚіиҝ”еӣһпјҢйҒҝе…ҚдёҠдј еӨ§ж–Үд»?
        existing_services = parse_docker_compose_custom_services()
        
        # жЈҖжҹҘжңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°жҳҜеҗҰе·ІеӯҳеңЁ
        for service in existing_services:
            if service['name'] == name:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§° '{name}' е·Іеӯҳең?)
        
        # жЈҖжҹҘз«ҜеҸЈжҳҜеҗҰе·Іиў«дҪҝз”?
        for service in existing_services:
            if service['port'] == port:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"з«ҜеҸЈ {port} е·Іиў«жңҚеҠЎ '{service['name']}' дҪҝз”Ё")
        
        # ========== з¬¬дәҢжӯҘпјҡйӘҢиҜҒйҖҡиҝҮеҗҺпјҢжүҚејҖе§Ӣж–Үд»¶ж“ҚдҪңпјҲжӯӨж—¶ж–Үд»¶жүҚејҖе§ӢзңҹжӯЈдёҠдј пјү==========
        
        # ========== з¬¬дәҢжӯҘпјҡйӘҢиҜҒйҖҡиҝҮеҗҺпјҢжүҚејҖе§Ӣж–Үд»¶ж“ҚдҪ?==========
        project_root = get_project_root()
        temp_dir = os.path.join(project_root, "temp", "custom-services")
        os.makedirs(temp_dir, exist_ok=True)
        
        # дҝқеӯҳдёҠдј зҡ„ж–Үд»?
        tar_path = os.path.join(temp_dir, f"{name}.tar")
        with open(tar_path, "wb") as f:
            shutil.copyfileobj(file.file, f)
        
        # еҠ иҪҪDockerй•ңеғҸ
        try:
            if not os.path.exists(tar_path):
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"дёҠдј зҡ„ж–Үд»¶дёҚеӯҳеңЁ: {tar_path}")

            image_name = f"{name}:latest"

            # дјҳе…ҲдҪҝз”Ё Python docker е®ўжҲ·з«ҜеҠ иҪҪпјҲйҒҝе…Қ Docker daemon и·Ҝеҫ„и®ҝй—®й—®йўҳпј?
            if docker_client:
                print(f"Using Python docker client to load image from: {tar_path}")
                try:
                    with open(tar_path, 'rb') as f:
                        loaded_images = docker_client.images.load(f.read())
                    if loaded_images and loaded_images[0].tags:
                        image_name = loaded_images[0].tags[0]
                    print(f"Successfully loaded image via Python client: {image_name}")
                except Exception as e:
                    raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Failed to load Docker image: {str(e)}")
            else:
                # Fallback: дҪҝз”Ё docker CLI subprocessпјҲйңҖиҰ?docker е‘Ҫд»Өең?PATH дёӯпјү
                abs_tar_path = os.path.abspath(tar_path)
                print(f"Using subprocess docker load: {abs_tar_path}")
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ['docker', 'load', '-i', abs_tar_path],
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True,
                    timeout=300,
                    cwd=project_root,
                )
                print(f"Docker load returncode: {result.returncode}, stdout: {result.stdout}, stderr: {result.stderr}")
                if result.returncode != 0:
                    error_msg = result.stderr or result.stdout or "Unknown error"
                    raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Failed to load Docker image: {error_msg}")
                image_match = re.search(r'Loaded image: (.+)', result.stdout)
                if image_match:
                    image_name = image_match.group(1).strip()
                print(f"Successfully loaded image via subprocess: {image_name}")

        except HTTPException:
            raise
        except Exception as e:
            import traceback
            print(f"Docker load exception: {str(e)}\n{traceback.format_exc()}")
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"еҠ иҪҪDockerй•ңеғҸеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")
        finally:
            # жё…зҗҶдёҙж—¶ж–Үд»¶
            if os.path.exists(tar_path):
                try:
                    os.remove(tar_path)
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"Warning: Failed to remove temp file: {e}")
        
        # еӨ„зҗҶзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®
        env_config = {}
        print(f"ж”¶еҲ°зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸеҸӮж•°: env_vars={env_vars}, type={type(env_vars)}")
        if env_vars and env_vars.strip():  # жЈҖжҹҘйқһз©әдё”йқһз©әзҷҪеӯ—з¬ҰдёІ
            try:
                env_config = json.loads(env_vars)
                print(f"и§ЈжһҗеҗҺзҡ„зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸ: {env_config}")
            except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
                print(f"зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸJSONи§ЈжһҗеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®ж јејҸй”ҷиҜҜ: {str(e)}")
        else:
            print("зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸеҸӮж•°дёәз©әжҲ–з©әзҷҪпјҢи·іиҝҮеӨ„зҗҶ")
        
        # еҲӣе»әй…ҚзҪ®зӣ®еҪ•е’?envж–Үд»¶пјҲеҰӮжһңжңүзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸпј?
        config_dir = None
        if env_config:
            project_root = get_project_root()
            config_dir = os.path.join(project_root, "config", name)
            os.makedirs(config_dir, exist_ok=True)
            print(f"еҲӣе»әй…ҚзҪ®зӣ®еҪ•: {config_dir}")
            
            env_file_path = os.path.join(config_dir, ".env")
            with open(env_file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                for key, value in env_config.items():
                    f.write(f"{key}={value}\n")
            # и®ҫзҪ®ж–Үд»¶жқғйҷҗдё?00пјҲд»…жүҖжңүиҖ…еҸҜиҜ»еҶҷпј?
            os.chmod(env_file_path, 0o600)
            print(f"е·ІеҲӣе»әзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸж–Үд»? {env_file_path}")
        else:
            print(f"жңӘй…ҚзҪ®зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸпјҢи·іиҝҮ.envж–Үд»¶еҲӣе»ә")
        
        # еӨ„зҗҶеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ?
        volumes_list = []
        print(f"ж”¶еҲ°еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪеҸӮж•? volumes={volumes}, type={type(volumes)}")
        if volumes and volumes.strip():  # жЈҖжҹҘйқһз©әдё”йқһз©әзҷҪеӯ—з¬ҰдёІ
            try:
                volumes_list = json.loads(volumes)
                if not isinstance(volumes_list, list):
                    raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®еҝ…йЎ»жҳҜж•°з»„ж јејҸ")
                # йӘҢиҜҒжҜҸдёӘжҢӮиҪҪйЎ№зҡ„ж јејҸ
                for volume in volumes_list:
                    if not isinstance(volume, str):
                        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪйЎ№еҝ…йЎ»жҳҜеӯ—з¬ҰдёІж јејҸ: {volume}")
                    # еҹәжң¬ж јејҸйӘҢиҜҒпјҡеә”иҜҘеҢ…еҗ«еҶ’еҸ·еҲҶйҡ”з¬Ұ
                    if ':' not in volume:
                        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪж јејҸй”ҷиҜҜпјҢеә”дҪҝз”?'host_path:container_path' ж јејҸ: {volume}")
                print(f"и§ЈжһҗеҗҺзҡ„еҚ·жҢӮиҪ? {volumes_list}")
            except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
                print(f"еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪJSONи§ЈжһҗеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®ж јејҸй”ҷиҜ? {str(e)}")
        else:
            print("еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪеҸӮж•°дёәз©әжҲ–з©әзҷҪпјҢи·іиҝҮеӨ„зҗ?)
        
        # ж·»еҠ еҲ°docker-compose.ymlпјҲbrowserless ж—?/health и·Ҝз”ұпјҢеҒҘеә·жЈҖжҹҘз”Ё /пј?
        health_check_path = "/" if name == "browserless" else "/health"
        try:
            add_service_to_docker_compose(name, port, image_name, config_dir, volumes_list, container_port, health_check_path, memory_limit_mb=memory_limit_mb, memory_reservation_mb=memory_reservation_mb)
        except HTTPException:
            raise
        except Exception as e:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"ж·»еҠ еҲ°docker-compose.ymlеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")
        
        # дҝқеӯҳжңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®пјҲжҸҸиҝ°гҖҒеӣҫж Үпјү
        try:
            save_custom_service_metadata(name, description, icon)
            print(f"е·ІдҝқеӯҳжңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®: {name}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"иӯҰе‘Ҡ: дҝқеӯҳжңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®еӨұиҙ? {e}")
        
        # еҗҜеҠЁж–°жңҚеҠ?
        startup_warning = None
        try:
            result = subprocess.run(
                _docker_compose_cmd() + ["up", "-d", name],
                cwd=project_root,
                timeout=120,
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
            )
            if result.returncode != 0:
                startup_warning = f"жңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ®е·ІеҶҷе…?docker-compose.ymlпјҢдҪҶиҮӘеҠЁеҗҜеҠЁеӨұиҙҘ: {result.stderr or result.stdout}"
                print(f"Service startup failed: returncode={result.returncode}, stderr={result.stderr}")
            else:
                print(f"Service {name} started successfully")
        except Exception as e:
            startup_warning = f"жңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ®е·ІеҶҷе…?docker-compose.ymlпјҢдҪҶиҮӘеҠЁеҗҜеҠЁејӮеёё: {str(e)}"
            print(f"Service startup exception: {str(e)}")

        response = {
            "success": True,
            "message": f"жңҚеҠЎ {name} йғЁзҪІжҲҗеҠҹпјҢи®ҝй—®ең°еқҖ: http://жңҚеҠЎеҷЁIP:{port}",
            "service": {
                "name": name,
                "port": port,
                "endpoint": endpoint or f"/{name}",
                "description": description,
                "image_name": image_name
            }
        }
        if startup_warning:
            response["warning"] = startup_warning
        return response
        
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        import traceback
        error_trace = traceback.format_exc()
        print(f"йғЁзҪІжңҚеҠЎејӮеёё: {str(e)}")
        print(f"е®Ңж•ҙй”ҷиҜҜе Ҷж Ҳ: {error_trace}")
        error_detail = f"йғЁзҪІжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}"
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=error_detail)

@app.delete("/api/v1/custom-services/{service_name}")
async def delete_custom_service(service_name: str):
    """еҲ йҷӨиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠ?""
    try:
        # иҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎдҝЎжҒҜпјҲд»Һdocker-compose.ymlпј?
        services = parse_docker_compose_custom_services()
        service_info = None
        for s in services:
            if s['name'] == service_name:
                service_info = s
                break
        
        if not service_info:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"жңҚеҠЎ {service_name} дёҚеӯҳең?)
        
        # еҒңжӯўе№¶еҲ йҷӨе®№еҷ?
        try:
            print(f"жӯЈеңЁеҒңжӯўе№¶еҲ йҷӨе®№еҷ? arbore-{service_name}")
            if docker_client:
                container_name = f"arbore-{service_name}"
                try:
                    container = docker_client.containers.get(container_name)
                    container.stop(timeout=30)
                    container.remove()
                    print(f"е®№еҷЁ {container_name} е·ІеҲ йҷ?)
                except docker.errors.NotFound:
                    print(f"е®№еҷЁ {container_name} дёҚеӯҳеңЁпјҢи·іиҝҮ")
            else:
                # дҪҝз”Ёdocker-composeе‘Ҫд»Ө
                result1 = subprocess.run(
                    _docker_compose_cmd() + ["stop", service_name],
                    cwd=get_project_root(),
                    timeout=60,
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True
                )
                if result1.returncode != 0:
                    print(f"еҒңжӯўе®№еҷЁиӯҰе‘Ҡ: {result1.stderr}")
                
                result2 = subprocess.run(
                    _docker_compose_cmd() + ["rm", "-f", service_name],
                    cwd=get_project_root(),
                    timeout=60,
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True
                )
                if result2.returncode != 0:
                    print(f"еҲ йҷӨе®№еҷЁиӯҰе‘Ҡ: {result2.stderr}")
                else:
                    print(f"е®№еҷЁ {service_name} е·ІеҲ йҷ?)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"иӯҰе‘Ҡ: еҲ йҷӨе®№еҷЁеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")
            import traceback
            print(traceback.format_exc())
        
        # д»Һdocker-compose.ymlдёӯеҲ йҷ?
        try:
            print(f"жӯЈеңЁд»Һdocker-compose.ymlеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ®: {service_name}")
            remove_service_from_docker_compose(service_name)
            print(f"е·Ід»Һdocker-compose.ymlеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ®")
        except HTTPException:
            # HTTPExceptionйңҖиҰҒеҗ‘дёҠжҠӣеҮ?
            raise
        except Exception as e:
            # е…¶д»–ејӮеёёд№ҹиҰҒжҠӣеҮәпјҢдёҚиғҪйқҷй»ҳеҗһжҺ?
            print(f"й”ҷиҜҜ: д»Һdocker-compose.ymlеҲ йҷӨеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")
            import traceback
            print(traceback.format_exc())
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"д»Һdocker-compose.ymlеҲ йҷӨеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")
        
        # жё…зҗҶй…ҚзҪ®зӣ®еҪ•пјҲеҰӮжһңеӯҳеңЁпјү
        try:
            project_root = get_project_root()
            config_dir = os.path.join(project_root, "config", service_name)
            if os.path.exists(config_dir):
                shutil.rmtree(config_dir)
                print(f"е·Іжё…зҗҶй…ҚзҪ®зӣ®еҪ? {config_dir}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"иӯҰе‘Ҡ: жё…зҗҶй…ҚзҪ®зӣ®еҪ•еӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")
        
        # еҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ?
        try:
            delete_custom_service_metadata(service_name)
            print(f"е·ІеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®: {service_name}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"иӯҰе‘Ҡ: еҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®еӨұиҙ? {e}")
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "message": f"жңҚеҠЎ {service_name} е·ІеҲ йҷ?
        }
        
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"еҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")

@app.put("/api/v1/custom-services/{service_name}")
async def update_custom_service(service_name: str, update: CustomServiceUpdate):
    """жӣҙж–°иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ?""
    try:
        # иҺ·еҸ–зҺ°жңүжңҚеҠЎдҝЎжҒҜпјҲд»Һdocker-compose.ymlпј?
        services = parse_docker_compose_custom_services()
        service_info = None
        for s in services:
            if s['name'] == service_name:
                service_info = s
                break
        
        if not service_info:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"жңҚеҠЎ {service_name} дёҚеӯҳең?)
        
        # жӣҙж–°жңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®пјҲеҰӮжһңжӣҙж–°дәҶжҸҸиҝ°жҲ–еӣҫж Үпј?
        if update.description is not None or update.icon is not None:
            try:
                new_description = update.description or service_info.get('description', f"{service_name}жңҚеҠЎ")
                new_icon = update.icon or service_info.get('icon', 'Box')
                save_custom_service_metadata(service_name, new_description, new_icon)
                print(f"е·Іжӣҙж–°жңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®: {service_name}")
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"иӯҰе‘Ҡ: жӣҙж–°жңҚеҠЎе…ғж•°жҚ®еӨұиҙ? {e}")
        
        # еӨ„зҗҶзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸжӣҙж–°
        if update.env_vars is not None:
            project_root = get_project_root()
            config_dir = os.path.join(project_root, "config", service_name)
            os.makedirs(config_dir, exist_ok=True)
            
            try:
                env_config = json.loads(update.env_vars) if update.env_vars else {}
            except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®ж јејҸй”ҷиҜҜ: {str(e)}")
            
            env_file_path = os.path.join(config_dir, ".env")
            with open(env_file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                for key, value in env_config.items():
                    f.write(f"{key}={value}\n")
            os.chmod(env_file_path, 0o600)
            print(f"е·Іжӣҙж–°зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ? {env_file_path}")
        
        # еӨ„зҗҶеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪжӣҙж–?
        volumes_list = None
        if update.volumes is not None:
            try:
                if update.volumes.strip():
                    volumes_list = json.loads(update.volumes)
                    if not isinstance(volumes_list, list):
                        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®еҝ…йЎ»жҳҜж•°з»„ж јејҸ")
                    # йӘҢиҜҒжҜҸдёӘжҢӮиҪҪйЎ№зҡ„ж јејҸ
                    for volume in volumes_list:
                        if not isinstance(volume, str):
                            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪйЎ№еҝ…йЎ»жҳҜеӯ—з¬ҰдёІж јејҸ: {volume}")
                        if ':' not in volume:
                            raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪж јејҸй”ҷиҜҜпјҢеә”дҪҝз”?'host_path:container_path' ж јејҸ: {volume}")
                else:
                    volumes_list = []
                print(f"е·Іжӣҙж–°еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®: {volumes_list}")
            except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®ж јејҸй”ҷиҜ? {str(e)}")
        
        # еҰӮжһңжӣҙж–°дәҶз«ҜеҸЈгҖҒеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪгҖҒеҶ…еӯҳжҲ–зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸпјҢйңҖиҰҒжӣҙж–°docker-composeй…ҚзҪ®
        if update.port or volumes_list is not None or update.env_vars is not None or update.memory_limit_mb is not None or update.memory_reservation_mb is not None:
            project_root = get_project_root()
            docker_compose_path = os.path.join(project_root, "docker-compose.yml")
            # еңЁеҲ йҷӨеүҚе…ҲиҜ»еҸ–еҪ“еү?compose дёӯзҡ„ image_name е’?volumesпјҲд»…еҪ“жңӘеңЁжң¬ж¬ЎжҸҗдәӨдёӯжҸҗдҫӣж—¶йңҖиҰҒдҝқз•ҷпјү
            content_before_remove = ""
            if os.path.exists(docker_compose_path):
                with open(docker_compose_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    content_before_remove = f.read()
            
            image_name = f"{service_name}:latest"
            image_match = re.search(rf'{service_name}:\s*\n\s+image:\s*([^\n]+)', content_before_remove)
            if image_match:
                image_name = image_match.group(1).strip()
            
            # иӢҘжң¬ж¬ЎжңӘжҸҗдәӨеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪпјҢеҲҷд»ҺеҪ“еүҚ compose дёӯиҜ»еҸ?
            if volumes_list is None and content_before_remove:
                service_pattern = rf'{re.escape(service_name)}\s*:.*?(?=\n  [a-z]|\n\n|\Z)'
                service_match = re.search(service_pattern, content_before_remove, re.DOTALL)
                if service_match:
                    service_config = service_match.group(0)
                    volumes_pattern = r'volumes:\s*\n((?:\s+- .+\n?)+)'
                    volumes_match = re.search(volumes_pattern, service_config)
                    if volumes_match:
                        volumes_block = volumes_match.group(1)
                        volume_items = re.findall(r'-\s*(.+)', volumes_block)
                        volumes_list = [item.strip() for item in volume_items]
                    else:
                        volumes_list = []
                else:
                    volumes_list = []
            elif volumes_list is None:
                volumes_list = []
            
            # еҲ йҷӨж—§й…ҚзҪ?
            remove_service_from_docker_compose(service_name)
            
            # дҪҝз”Ёж–°й…ҚзҪ®ж·»еҠ?
            new_port = update.port or service_info['port']
            new_description = update.description or service_info['description']
            
            # йӘҢиҜҒз«ҜеҸЈиҢғеӣҙ
            if not (7000 <= new_port <= 7999):
                raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="з«ҜеҸЈеҝ…йЎ»ең?000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ?)
            
            # йӘҢиҜҒе”ҜдёҖжҖ§пјҲжҺ’йҷӨеҪ“еүҚжңҚеҠЎпј?
            existing_services = parse_docker_compose_custom_services()
            for service in existing_services:
                if service['name'] == service_name:
                    continue  # жҺ’йҷӨеҪ“еүҚжңҚеҠЎ
                
                # жЈҖжҹҘз«ҜеҸЈжҳҜеҗҰеҶІзӘ?
                if service['port'] == new_port:
                    raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"з«ҜеҸЈ {new_port} е·Іиў«жңҚеҠЎ '{service['name']}' дҪҝз”Ё")
            
            new_icon = update.icon or service_info.get('icon', 'Box')
            
            # иҺ·еҸ–й…ҚзҪ®зӣ®еҪ•пјҲз”ЁдәҺenv_fileпј?
            config_dir = os.path.join(project_root, "config", service_name)
            # еҰӮжһңжӣҙж–°дәҶзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸпјҢзЎ®дҝқconfig_dirеӯҳеңЁ
            if update.env_vars is not None:
                os.makedirs(config_dir, exist_ok=True)
            config_dir = config_dir if os.path.exists(os.path.join(config_dir, ".env")) else None
            
            # иҺ·еҸ–е®№еҷЁз«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҰӮжһңжӣҙж–°дәҶcontainer_portпјҢдҪҝз”Ёж–°еҖјпјӣеҗҰеҲҷй»ҳи®ӨдҪҝз”Ёе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈпјү
            new_container_port = update.container_port
            if new_container_port is None:
                # еҰӮжһңжңӘжҢҮе®ҡе®№еҷЁз«ҜеҸЈпјҢй»ҳи®ӨдҪҝз”Ёе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈпјҲдҝқжҢҒз«ҜеҸЈдёҖиҮҙпјү
                new_container_port = new_port
            # еҶ…еӯҳйҷҗеҲ¶пјҡдјҳе…Ҳз”Ёжң¬ж¬ЎжҸҗдәӨеҖјпјҢеҗҰеҲҷдҝқз•ҷеҺҹй…ҚзҪ®пјҲservice_info дёӯеҸҜиғҪж— жӯӨй”®еҲҷдј  Noneпј?
            new_memory_limit_mb = update.memory_limit_mb if update.memory_limit_mb is not None else service_info.get("memory_limit_mb")
            new_memory_reservation_mb = update.memory_reservation_mb if update.memory_reservation_mb is not None else service_info.get("memory_reservation_mb")
            health_check_path = "/" if service_name == "browserless" else "/health"
            add_service_to_docker_compose(service_name, new_port, image_name, config_dir, volumes_list, new_container_port, health_check_path, memory_limit_mb=new_memory_limit_mb, memory_reservation_mb=new_memory_reservation_mb)
        
        # еҰӮжһңеҸӘжӣҙж–°дәҶзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸпјҲжІЎжңүжӣҙж–°з«ҜеҸ?еҚ·жҢӮиҪ?еҶ…еӯҳпјүпјҢйңҖиҰҒйҮҚеҗҜе®№еҷЁд»ҘеҠ иҪҪж–°зҡ„зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸ
        # жіЁж„ҸпјҡеҰӮжһңжӣҙж–°дәҶз«ҜеҸЈ/еҚ·жҢӮиҪ?еҶ…еӯҳпјҢдёҠйқўзҡ„д»Јз Ғе·Із»ҸдјҡйҮҚж–°з”ҹжҲ?docker-compose е№¶йҮҚе»әе®№еҷ?
        if update.env_vars is not None and not (update.port or update.endpoint or (volumes_list is not None) or update.memory_limit_mb is not None or update.memory_reservation_mb is not None):
            try:
                container_name = f"arbore-{service_name}"
                print(f"зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸе·Іжӣҙж–°пјҢйҮҚеҗҜе®№еҷЁд»ҘеҠ иҪҪж–°й…ҚзҪ®: {container_name}")
                if docker_client:
                    try:
                        container = docker_client.containers.get(container_name)
                        container.restart(timeout=30)
                        print(f"е®№еҷЁ {container_name} е·ІйҮҚеҗ?)
                    except Exception as e:
                        print(f"дҪҝз”ЁDockerе®ўжҲ·з«ҜйҮҚеҗҜеӨұиҙҘпјҢе°қиҜ•дҪҝз”Ёdocker compose: {str(e)}")
                        subprocess.run(
                            _docker_compose_cmd() + ["restart", service_name],
                            cwd=get_project_root(),
                            timeout=60
                        )
                else:
                    subprocess.run(
                        _docker_compose_cmd() + ["restart", service_name],
                        cwd=get_project_root(),
                        timeout=60
                    )
                print(f"е®№еҷЁ {container_name} е·ІйҮҚеҗҜпјҢж–°зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸе·Із”ҹж•Ҳ")
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"иӯҰе‘Ҡ: йҮҚеҗҜе®№еҷЁеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")
                # дёҚжҠӣеҮәејӮеёёпјҢеӣ дёәзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸж–Үд»¶е·Іжӣҙж–°пјҢз”ЁжҲ·еҸҜд»ҘжүӢеҠЁйҮҚеҗҜ
        
        return {
            "success": True,
            "message": f"жңҚеҠЎ {service_name} е·Іжӣҙж–?
        }
        
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"жӣҙж–°жңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")

@app.post("/api/v1/custom-services/{service_name}/restart")
async def restart_custom_service(service_name: str):
    """йҮҚеҗҜиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎе®№еҷЁпјҲйҮҚж–°еҲӣе»әд»ҘеҠ иҪҪжңҖж–°зҡ„env_fileй…ҚзҪ®пј?""
    try:
        container_name = f"arbore-{service_name}"
        project_root = get_project_root()
        
        print(f"жӯЈеңЁйҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎ: {service_name} (йҮҚж–°еҲӣе»әе®№еҷЁд»ҘеҠ иҪҪжңҖж–°й…ҚзҪ?")
        
        # дҪҝз”Ё docker compose up -d йҮҚж–°еҲӣе»әе®№еҷЁпјҲдјҡеҠ иҪҪжңҖж–°зҡ„env_fileпј?
        # иҝҷжҜ” restart жӣҙеҘҪпјҢеӣ дё?restart дёҚдјҡйҮҚж–°еҠ иҪҪ env_file
        result = subprocess.run(
            _docker_compose_cmd() + ["up", "-d", "--force-recreate", service_name],
            cwd=project_root,
            timeout=120,
            capture_output=True,
            text=True
        )
        
        if result.returncode == 0:
            print(f"жңҚеҠЎ {service_name} е·ІйҮҚж–°еҲӣе»әе№¶еҗҜеҠЁ")
            return {
                "success": True,
                "message": f"жңҚеҠЎ {service_name} е·ІйҮҚеҗҜпјҲе·ІйҮҚж–°еҲӣе»әе®№еҷЁпјҢж–°зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸе·Із”ҹж•Ҳпј?
            }
        else:
            error_msg = result.stderr or result.stdout or "жңӘзҹҘй”ҷиҜҜ"
            print(f"йҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: {error_msg}")
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"йҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: {error_msg}")
        
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"йҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")

@app.get("/api/v1/custom-services/{service_name}/env")
async def get_service_env_vars(service_name: str):
    """иҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎзҡ„зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ?""
    try:
        project_root = get_project_root()
        config_dir = os.path.join(project_root, "config", service_name)
        env_file_path = os.path.join(config_dir, ".env")
        
        env_vars = {}
        if os.path.exists(env_file_path):
            with open(env_file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                for line in f:
                    line = line.strip()
                    if line and not line.startswith('#') and '=' in line:
                        key, value = line.split('=', 1)
                        env_vars[key.strip()] = value.strip()
        
        # еҚідҪҝж–Үд»¶дёҚеӯҳеңЁд№ҹиҝ”еӣһз©әеҜ№иұЎпјҢиҖҢдёҚжҳ?04
        return {"env_vars": env_vars}
    except Exception as e:
        # иҝ”еӣһз©әеҜ№иұЎиҖҢдёҚжҳҜй”ҷиҜҜпјҢеӣ дёә.envж–Үд»¶еҸҜиғҪдёҚеӯҳең?
        print(f"иҜ»еҸ–зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸеӨұиҙҘпјҲеҸҜиғҪж–Үд»¶дёҚеӯҳеңЁпј? {str(e)}")
        return {"env_vars": {}}

@app.get("/api/v1/custom-services/{service_name}/volumes")
async def get_service_volumes(service_name: str):
    """иҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎзҡ„еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®"""
    try:
        project_root = get_project_root()
        docker_compose_path = os.path.join(project_root, "docker-compose.yml")
        
        volumes_list = []
        if os.path.exists(docker_compose_path):
            with open(docker_compose_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                content = f.read()
            
            # жҹҘжүҫжңҚеҠЎй…ҚзҪ®дёӯзҡ„ volumes йғЁеҲҶ
            # еҢ№й…ҚжңҚеҠЎе®ҡд№үеқ?
            service_pattern = rf'{re.escape(service_name)}\s*:.*?(?=\n  [a-z]|\n\n|\Z)'
            service_match = re.search(service_pattern, content, re.DOTALL)
            
            if service_match:
                service_config = service_match.group(0)
                # жҹҘжүҫ volumes: йғЁеҲҶ
                volumes_pattern = r'volumes:\s*\n((?:\s+- .+\n?)+)'
                volumes_match = re.search(volumes_pattern, service_config)
                
                if volumes_match:
                    volumes_block = volumes_match.group(1)
                    # жҸҗеҸ–жҜҸдёӘжҢӮиҪҪйЎ?
                    volume_items = re.findall(r'-\s*(.+)', volumes_block)
                    volumes_list = [item.strip() for item in volume_items]
        
        # еҚідҪҝжІЎжңүй…ҚзҪ®д№ҹиҝ”еӣһз©әж•°з»„пјҢиҖҢдёҚжҳ?04
        return {"volumes": volumes_list}
    except Exception as e:
        # иҝ”еӣһз©әж•°з»„иҖҢдёҚжҳҜй”ҷиҜҜпјҢеӣ дёәvolumesеҸҜиғҪдёҚеӯҳең?
        print(f"иҜ»еҸ–еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪеӨұиҙҘпјҲеҸҜиғҪй…ҚзҪ®дёҚеӯҳеңЁпјү: {str(e)}")
        return {"volumes": []}

@app.get("/api/v1/custom-services/available-port")
async def get_available_port_api():
    """иҺ·еҸ–дёӢдёҖдёӘеҸҜз”Ёз«ҜеҸ?""
    try:
        port = get_available_port()
        return {"port": port}
    except HTTPException:
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"иҺ·еҸ–еҸҜз”Ёз«ҜеҸЈеӨұиҙҘ: {str(e)}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8002)

<template>

<script setup>
import { ref, onMounted, provide } from 'vue'
import axios from 'axios'
import ServicesView from './components/ServicesView.vue'
import ResourcesView from './components/ResourcesView.vue'
import LogsView from './components/LogsView.vue'
import SystemConfigView from './components/SystemConfigView.vue'
import LicenseView from './components/LicenseView.vue'
import CustomServicesView from './components/CustomServicesView.vue'

// еҪ“еүҚжҝҖжҙ»зҡ„ж ҮзӯҫйЎөж ҮиҜҶпјҲCurrent active tab nameпј?
const activeTab = ref('services')
// еҗҺз«Ҝ API зүҲжң¬еҸ·пјҲdisplayed API version textпј?
const apiVersion = ref('v1.1.0')
// жһ„е»әж—¶й—ҙпјҢз”ЁдәҺиҫ…еҠ©жҺ’жҹҘйғЁзҪІзүҲжң¬пјҲbuild timestamp for diagnosticsпј?
const buildTime = ref('')

provide('setActiveTab', (name) => {
  activeTab.value = name
})

const handleTabClick = (tab) => {
  // еҪ“еүҚд»…з”ЁдәҺи°ғиҜ•ж—Ҙеҝ—пјҢеҰӮйңҖеҹӢзӮ№жҲ–иЎҢдёәеҲҶжһҗпјҢеҸҜд»ҘеңЁжӯӨеӨ„з»ҹдёҖжү©еұ•гҖ?
  console.log('Tab clicked:', tab.name)
}

// иҺ·еҸ– API зүҲжң¬дҝЎжҒҜе№¶еұ•зӨәеңЁеӨҙйғЁ
// Fetch API version info and expose it in the header badge.
onMounted(async () => {
  try {
    const response = await axios.get('/api/v1/version')
    if (response.data.version) {
      apiVersion.value = `v${response.data.version}`
    }
    if (response.data.build_time) {
      buildTime.value = response.data.build_time
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to fetch version:', error)
  }
})
</script>

        </el-form-item>

        <el-form-item label="жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°" prop="name">
          <el-input
            v-model="serviceForm.name"
            placeholder="дҫӢеҰӮ: my-api-service"
            :disabled="!!editingService"
            @blur="handleNameBlur"
          />
          <div class="form-tip">еҸӘиғҪеҢ…еҗ«е°ҸеҶҷеӯ—жҜҚгҖҒж•°еӯ—е’Ңиҝһеӯ—з¬?/div>
        </el-form-item>

        <el-form-item label="жҸҸиҝ°дҝЎжҒҜ" prop="description">
          <el-input
            v-model="serviceForm.description"
            type="textarea"
            :rows="2"
            placeholder="иҜ·иҫ“е…ҘжңҚеҠЎжҸҸиҝ?
          />
        </el-form-item>

        <el-form-item label="е®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸ? prop="port">
          <el-input-number
            v-model="serviceForm.port"
            :min="7000"
            :max="7999"
            :step="1"
            style="width: 100%"
          />
          <div class="form-tip">з«ҜеҸЈиҢғеӣҙпј?000-7999пјҢиҝҷжҳҜеҜ№еӨ–и®ҝй—®зҡ„з«ҜеҸЈпјҲж јејҸпјҡhttp://жңҚеҠЎеҷЁIP:з«ҜеҸЈпј?/div>
        </el-form-item>

        <el-form-item label="е®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸ? prop="container_port">
          <el-input-number
            v-model="serviceForm.container_port"
            :min="1"
            :max="65535"
            :step="1"
            style="width: 100%"
          />
          <div class="form-tip">е®№еҷЁеҶ…жңҚеҠЎе®һйҷ…зӣ‘еҗ¬зҡ„з«ҜеҸЈпјҢй»ҳи®ӨдёҺе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈдёҖиҮҙгҖӮеҰӮжһңжңҚеҠЎзЎ¬зј–з ҒдәҶз«ҜеҸЈпјҲеҰ?000пјүпјҢеҸҜд»Ҙдҝ®ж”№дёәе®һйҷ…з«ҜеҸЈпјҢзі»з»ҹдјҡиҮӘеҠЁжҳ е°„еҲ°е®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸ?/div>
        </el-form-item>

        <el-form-item label="еҶ…еӯҳйҷҗеҲ¶ (MB)" prop="memory_limit_mb">
          <el-input-number
            v-model="serviceForm.memory_limit_mb"
            :min="0"
            :max="65536"
            :step="256"
            style="width: 100%"
            placeholder="дёҚеЎ«еҲҷдёҚйҷҗеҲ¶"
            controls-position="right"
          />
          <div class="form-tip">е®№еҷЁжңҖеӨ§еҸҜз”ЁеҶ…еӯҳпјҲMBпјүпјҢеҰ?4096 иЎЁзӨә 4GBгҖӮдҝ®ж”№еҗҺйңҖйҮҚеҗҜе®№еҷЁз”ҹж•Ҳ</div>
        </el-form-item>
        <el-form-item label="еҶ…еӯҳйў„з•ҷ (MB)" prop="memory_reservation_mb">
          <el-input-number
            v-model="serviceForm.memory_reservation_mb"
            :min="0"
            :max="65536"
            :step="256"
            style="width: 100%"
            placeholder="еҸҜйҖ?
            controls-position="right"
          />
          <div class="form-tip">е®№еҷЁдҝқиҜҒеҸҜз”ЁеҶ…еӯҳпјҲMBпјүпјҢеҸҜйҖүгҖӮдҝ®ж”№еҗҺйңҖйҮҚеҗҜе®№еҷЁз”ҹж•Ҳ</div>
        </el-form-item>

        <el-form-item
          v-if="!editingService"
          label="Dockerй•ңеғҸ"
          prop="file"
        >
          <div class="file-upload-wrapper">
            <input
              id="file-input-tar"
              type="file"
              accept=".tar"
              style="display: none;"
              @change="handleFileInputChange"
            />
            <label for="file-input-tar" class="file-input-label">
              <el-button type="primary" style="pointer-events: none;">
                <Upload style="margin-right: 4px;" />
                йҖүжӢ©tarж–Үд»¶
              </el-button>
            </label>
            <div v-if="serviceForm.file" class="file-name">
              {{ serviceForm.file.name }}
            </div>
            <div class="form-tip">
              иҜ·дёҠдј е·Іжү“еҢ…зҡ„Dockerй•ңеғҸtarж–Үд»¶
            </div>
          </div>
        </el-form-item>

        <!-- зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ® -->
        <el-form-item
          label="зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸ"
        >
          <el-tabs v-model="envTabType" class="env-vars-tabs">
            <el-tab-pane label="иЎЁеҚ•жЁЎејҸ" name="form">
              <div class="env-vars-form">
                <div
                  v-for="(item, index) in envVars"
                  :key="index"
                  class="env-var-item"
                >
                  <el-input
                    v-model="item.key"
                    placeholder="еҸҳйҮҸеҗ?
                    style="width: 200px; margin-right: 8px;"
                  />
                  <el-input
                    v-model="item.value"
                    placeholder="еҸҳйҮҸеҖ?
                    type="password"
                    show-password
                    style="flex: 1; margin-right: 8px;"
                  />
                  <el-button
                    type="danger"
                    link
                    @click="removeEnvVar(index)"
                  >
                    еҲ йҷӨ
                  </el-button>
                </div>
                <el-button
                  type="primary"
                  link
                  @click="addEnvVar"
                  style="margin-top: 8px;"
                >
                  + ж·»еҠ еҸҳйҮҸ
                </el-button>
              </div>
            </el-tab-pane>
            <el-tab-pane label="JSONжЁЎејҸ" name="json">
              <el-input
                v-model="envVarsJson"
                type="textarea"
                :rows="8"
                placeholder='{"AUTH_ENABLED": "true", "SM4_KEY": "your_key"}'
                class="env-vars-json-input"
              />
              <div class="form-tip">
                иҜ·иҫ“е…ҘJSONж јејҸзҡ„зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®пјҢдҫӢеҰӮ: {"KEY1": "value1", "KEY2": "value2"}
              </div>
            </el-tab-pane>
          </el-tabs>
        </el-form-item>

        <!-- еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ?-->
        <el-form-item
          label="еҚ·жҢӮиҪ?
        >
          <el-tabs v-model="volumesTabType" class="env-vars-tabs">
            <el-tab-pane label="иЎЁеҚ•жЁЎејҸ" name="form">
              <div class="env-vars-form">
                <div
                  v-for="(item, index) in volumesList"
                  :key="index"
                  class="env-var-item"
                >
                  <el-input
                    v-model="item.hostPath"
                    placeholder="е®ҝдё»жңәи·Ҝеҫ„пјҲеҰ? /path/to/huggingface/modelsпј?
                    style="flex: 1; margin-right: 8px;"
                  />
                  <el-input
                    v-model="item.containerPath"
                    placeholder="е®№еҷЁеҶ…и·Ҝеҫ„пјҲеҰ? /modelsпј?
                    style="flex: 1; margin-right: 8px;"
                  />
                  <el-checkbox
                    v-model="item.readOnly"
                    style="margin-right: 8px;"
                  >
                    еҸӘиҜ»
                  </el-checkbox>
                  <el-button
                    type="danger"
                    link
                    @click="removeVolume(index)"
                  >
                    еҲ йҷӨ
                  </el-button>
                </div>
                <el-button
                  type="primary"
                  link
                  @click="addVolume"
                  style="margin-top: 8px;"
                >
                  + ж·»еҠ жҢӮиҪҪ
                </el-button>
              </div>
            </el-tab-pane>
            <el-tab-pane label="JSONжЁЎејҸ" name="json">
              <el-input
                v-model="volumesJson"
                type="textarea"
                :rows="6"
                placeholder='["/path/to/huggingface/models:/models", "/path/to/data:/data:ro"]'
                class="env-vars-json-input"
              />
              <div class="form-tip">
                иҜ·иҫ“е…ҘJSONж•°з»„ж јејҸзҡ„еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®пјҢдҫӢеҰ? ["/host/path:/container/path", "/host/path2:/container/path2:ro"]
                <br>
                ж јејҸиҜҙжҳҺпјҡжҜҸдёӘжҢӮиҪҪйЎ№дёәеӯ—з¬ҰдёІпјҢж јејҸдёә "е®ҝдё»жңәи·Ҝеҫ?е®№еҷЁеҶ…и·Ҝеҫ? жҲ?"е®ҝдё»жңәи·Ҝеҫ?е®№еҷЁеҶ…и·Ҝеҫ?ro"пјҲroиЎЁзӨәеҸӘиҜ»пј?
              </div>
            </el-tab-pane>
          </el-tabs>
        </el-form-item>

        <el-form-item v-if="!editingService">
          <el-alert
            type="info"
            :closable="false"
            show-icon
          >
            <template #default>
              <span class="alert-text">иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎеҶ…йғЁз«ҜеҸЈиҢғеӣҙпјҡ7000-7999пјҢйҖҡиҝҮnginxи·Ҝеҫ„еҢәеҲҶдёҚеҗҢжңҚеҠЎпјҢnginxз»ҹдёҖеҜ№еӨ–жҸҗдҫӣи®ҝй—®</span>
            </template>
          </el-alert>
        </el-form-item>
      </el-form>

      <template #footer>
        <div class="dialog-footer">
          <el-button @click="showAddDialog = false">еҸ–ж¶Ҳ</el-button>
          <el-button
            type="primary"
            @click="submitService"
            :loading="submitting"
          >
            {{ editingService ? 'жӣҙж–°' : 'йғЁзҪІ' }}
          </el-button>
        </div>
      </template>
    </el-dialog>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
// иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎз®ЎзҗҶйҖ»иҫ‘пјҲCustom services management logicпј?
// дё»иҰҒиҒҢиҙЈпј?
// 1) йҖҡиҝҮ /admin-api/api/v1/custom-services зі»еҲ—жҺҘеҸЈпјҢе®ҢжҲҗжңҚеҠЎзҡ„еўһеҲ ж”№жҹҘпј?
// 2) еңЁиЎЁеҚ•дёӯж”¶йӣҶй•ңеғҸгҖҒз«ҜеҸЈгҖҒзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸгҖҒеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪзӯүдёҺе®№еҷЁзј–жҺ’зӣҙжҺҘзӣёе…ізҡ„дҝЎжҒҜпјӣ
// 3) йӣҶжҲҗи®ёеҸҜиҜҒж ЎйӘҢйҖ»иҫ‘пјҢзЎ®дҝқд»…еңЁе·ІжіЁеҶҢжҺҲжқғзҡ„зҺҜеўғдёӯејҖеҗҜиҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎеҠҹиғҪгҖ?
import { ref, reactive, computed, onMounted, nextTick, watch, inject } from 'vue'
import axios from 'axios'
import { ElMessage, ElMessageBox } from 'element-plus'

const setActiveTab = inject('setActiveTab', null)
import * as ElementPlusIconsVue from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
import { Search, Plus, Refresh, Upload } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'

const services = ref([])
const loading = ref(false)
const submitting = ref(false)
const showAddDialog = ref(false)
const showIconSelector = ref(false)
const iconSearchText = ref('')
const editingService = ref(null)
const serviceFormRef = ref(null)
// дёҚеҶҚйңҖиҰ?fileInputRefпјҢдҪҝз”ЁеҺҹз”?label + input ж–№ејҸ

// зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®
const envTabType = ref('form')
const envVars = ref([])
const envVarsJson = ref('')

// еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ?
const volumesTabType = ref('form')
const volumesList = ref([])
const volumesJson = ref('')

// жңҚеҠЎиҜҰжғ…
const showDetailsDialog = ref(false)
const selectedService = ref(null)
const serviceLogs = ref('')
const logsLoading = ref(false)
const logTail = ref(100)

const serviceForm = reactive({
  name: '',
  description: '',
  port: 7000,  // е®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈпјҢй»ҳи®Ө7000пјҢеҸҜең?000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ…йҖүжӢ©
  container_port: 7000,  // е®№еҷЁеҶ…з«ҜеҸЈпјҢй»ҳи®ӨзӯүдәҺе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸ?
  memory_limit_mb: null,  // еҶ…еӯҳйҷҗеҲ¶пјҲMBпјүпјҢеҸҜйҖ?
  memory_reservation_mb: null,  // еҶ…еӯҳйў„з•ҷпјҲMBпјүпјҢеҸҜйҖ?
  icon: 'Box',  // й»ҳи®Өеӣҫж Ү
  file: null
})

// и®°еҪ•дёҠдёҖж¬Ўзҡ„portеҖјпјҢз”ЁдәҺеҲӨж–ӯжҳҜеҗҰйңҖиҰҒиҮӘеҠЁеҗҢжӯҘcontainer_port
let previousPort = 7000

// зӣ‘еҗ¬portеҸҳеҢ–пјҢеҰӮжһңcontainer_portзӯүдәҺж—§зҡ„portеҖјпјҢеҲҷиҮӘеҠЁеҗҢжӯ?
watch(() => serviceForm.port, (newPort, oldPort) => {
  // еҰӮжһңcontainer_portзӯүдәҺж—§зҡ„portеҖјпјҢиҜҙжҳҺз”ЁжҲ·иҝҳжІЎжңүжүӢеҠЁдҝ®ж”№иҝҮпјҢиҮӘеҠЁеҗҢжӯ?
  if (serviceForm.container_port === oldPort || serviceForm.container_port === previousPort) {
    serviceForm.container_port = newPort
  }
  previousPort = newPort
})

// ж·»еҠ зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸ
const addEnvVar = () => {
  envVars.value.push({ key: '', value: '' })
}

// еҲ йҷӨзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸ
const removeEnvVar = (index) => {
  envVars.value.splice(index, 1)
}

// ж·»еҠ еҚ·жҢӮиҪ?
const addVolume = () => {
  volumesList.value.push({ hostPath: '', containerPath: '', readOnly: false })
}

// еҲ йҷӨеҚ·жҢӮиҪ?
const removeVolume = (index) => {
  volumesList.value.splice(index, 1)
}

// е°ҶзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸиҪ¬жҚўдёәJSON
const getEnvVarsJson = () => {
  if (envTabType.value === 'json') {
    // JSONжЁЎејҸпјҡзӣҙжҺҘиҝ”еӣһJSONеӯ—з¬Ұдё?
    if (!envVarsJson.value.trim()) {
      return null
    }
    try {
      // йӘҢиҜҒJSONж јејҸ
      JSON.parse(envVarsJson.value)
      return envVarsJson.value
    } catch (e) {
      throw new Error('зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸJSONж јејҸй”ҷиҜҜ')
    }
  } else {
    // иЎЁеҚ•жЁЎејҸпјҡиҪ¬жҚўдёәJSON
    const envObj = {}
    envVars.value.forEach(item => {
      if (item.key && item.value) {
        envObj[item.key] = item.value
      }
    })
    if (Object.keys(envObj).length === 0) {
      return null
    }
    return JSON.stringify(envObj)
  }
}

// е°ҶеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪиҪ¬жҚўдёәJSON
const getVolumesJson = () => {
  if (volumesTabType.value === 'json') {
    // JSONжЁЎејҸпјҡзӣҙжҺҘиҝ”еӣһJSONеӯ—з¬Ұдё?
    if (!volumesJson.value.trim()) {
      return null
    }
    try {
      // йӘҢиҜҒJSONж јејҸ
      const parsed = JSON.parse(volumesJson.value)
      if (!Array.isArray(parsed)) {
        throw new Error('еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®еҝ…йЎ»жҳҜж•°з»„ж јејҸ')
      }
      return volumesJson.value
    } catch (e) {
      throw new Error('еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪJSONж јејҸй”ҷиҜҜ: ' + e.message)
    }
  } else {
    // иЎЁеҚ•жЁЎејҸпјҡиҪ¬жҚўдёәJSONж•°з»„
    const volumesArray = []
    volumesList.value.forEach(item => {
      if (item.hostPath && item.containerPath) {
        let volumeStr = `${item.hostPath}:${item.containerPath}`
        if (item.readOnly) {
          volumeStr += ':ro'
        }
        volumesArray.push(volumeStr)
      }
    })
    if (volumesArray.length === 0) {
      return null
    }
    return JSON.stringify(volumesArray)
  }
}

// иҺ·еҸ–жүҖжңүеҸҜз”Ёзҡ„еӣҫж ҮпјҲд»ҺElementPlusIconsVueдёӯжҸҗеҸ–пјү
const getAllAvailableIcons = () => {
  const iconNames = Object.keys(ElementPlusIconsVue)
  // иҝҮж»ӨжҺүдёҖдәӣдёҚеёёз”Ёзҡ„еӣҫж ҮпјҢдҝқз•ҷеёёз”Ёе’Ңжңүз”Ёзҡ„
  const excludeIcons = ['ArrowLeft', 'ArrowRight', 'ArrowUp', 'ArrowDown', 'Close', 'Check', 'Loading']
  return iconNames
    .filter(name => !excludeIcons.includes(name))
    .map(name => ({
      name,
      component: ElementPlusIconsVue[name],
      label: name.replace(/([A-Z])/g, ' $1').trim()
    }))
    .sort((a, b) => a.label.localeCompare(b.label))
}

const availableIcons = getAllAvailableIcons()

// и®Ўз®—иҝҮж»ӨеҗҺзҡ„еӣҫж ҮеҲ—иЎЁ
const filteredIcons = computed(() => {
  if (!iconSearchText.value) {
    return availableIcons
  }
  const query = iconSearchText.value.toLowerCase()
  return availableIcons.filter(icon => 
    icon.label.toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
    icon.name.toLowerCase().includes(query)
  )
})

// иҺ·еҸ–еӣҫж Үз»„д»¶
const getIconComponent = (iconName) => {
  return ElementPlusIconsVue[iconName] || ElementPlusIconsVue.Box
}

// иҺ·еҸ–еӣҫж Үж Үзӯҫ
const getIconLabel = (iconName) => {
  const icon = availableIcons.find(i => i.name === iconName)
  return icon ? icon.label : 'Box'
}

// йҖүжӢ©еӣҫж Ү
const selectIcon = (iconName) => {
  serviceForm.icon = iconName
  showIconSelector.value = false
  iconSearchText.value = ''
}

// жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°еӨұз„Ұж—¶пјҢеҰӮжһңз«ҜзӮ№дёәз©әпјҢиҮӘеҠЁеЎ«е…?
// жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°еӨұз„Ұж—¶зҡ„еӨ„зҗҶпјҲдёҚеҶҚйңҖиҰҒиҮӘеҠЁеЎ«е……endpointпј?
const handleNameBlur = () => {
  // endpointе·Із§»йҷӨпјҢзҺ°еңЁйҖҡиҝҮз«ҜеҸЈзӣҙжҺҘи®ҝй—®
}

const formRules = {
  name: [
    { required: true, message: 'иҜ·иҫ“е…ҘжңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§?, trigger: 'blur' },
    {
      pattern: /^[a-z0-9-]+$/,
      message: 'жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°еҸӘиғҪеҢ…еҗ«е°ҸеҶҷеӯ—жҜҚгҖҒж•°еӯ—е’Ңиҝһеӯ—з¬?,
      trigger: 'blur'
    }
  ],
  description: [
    { required: true, message: 'иҜ·иҫ“е…ҘжңҚеҠЎжҸҸиҝ?, trigger: 'blur' }
  ],
  port: [
    { required: true, message: 'иҜ·иҫ“е…Ҙз«ҜеҸЈеҸ·', trigger: 'blur' },
    {
      type: 'number',
      min: 7000,
      max: 7999,
      message: 'з«ҜеҸЈеҝ…йЎ»ең?000-7999иҢғеӣҙеҶ?,
      trigger: 'blur'
    }
  ],
  file: [
    {
      validator: (rule, value, callback) => {
        if (!editingService.value && !serviceForm.file) {
          callback(new Error('иҜ·йҖүжӢ©Dockerй•ңеғҸtarж–Үд»¶'))
        } else {
          callback()
        }
      },
      trigger: 'change'
    }
  ]
}

const getServerIP = () => {
  return window.location.hostname
}

const getServiceUrl = (service) => {
  // зӣҙжҺҘдҪҝз”Ёз«ҜеҸЈи®ҝй—®пјҢдёҚеҶҚдҪҝз”Ёendpoint
  return `http://${getServerIP()}:${service.port}`
}

// иҺ·еҸ–зҠ¶жҖҒзұ»еһӢпјҲз”ЁдәҺel-tagзҡ„typeеұһжҖ§пјү
const getStatusType = (status) => {
  if (!status) return 'info'
  const statusLower = status.toLowerCase()
  if (statusLower === 'running') return 'success'
  if (statusLower === 'stopped' || statusLower === 'exited') return 'danger'
  if (statusLower === 'restarting') return 'warning'
  if (statusLower === 'not_found') return 'info'
  return 'info'
}

// иҺ·еҸ–зҠ¶жҖҒж–Үжң¬пјҲдёӯж–ҮжҳҫзӨәпј?
const getStatusText = (status) => {
  if (!status) return 'жңӘзҹҘ'
  const statusLower = status.toLowerCase()
  const statusMap = {
    'running': 'иҝҗиЎҢдё?,
    'stopped': 'е·ІеҒңжӯ?,
    'exited': 'е·ІйҖҖеҮ?,
    'restarting': 'йҮҚеҗҜдё?,
    'paused': 'е·ІжҡӮеҒ?,
    'not_found': 'жңӘжүҫеҲ?,
    'created': 'е·ІеҲӣе»?,
    'removing': 'еҲ йҷӨдё?
  }
  return statusMap[statusLower] || status
}

// иҺ·еҸ–еҒҘеә·зҠ¶жҖҒж–Үжң¬пјҲдёӯж–ҮжҳҫзӨәпј?
const getHealthText = (health, containerStatus) => {
  if (!health) return 'жңӘзҹҘ'
  const healthLower = health.toLowerCase()
  const statusLower = containerStatus ? containerStatus.toLowerCase() : ''
  
  // еҰӮжһңе®№еҷЁе·Із»ҸиҝҗиЎҢпјҢеҒҘеә·жЈҖжҹҘиҝҳеңЁstartingпјҢжҳҫзӨәдёә"еҒҘеә·жЈҖжҹҘдёӯ"
  if (healthLower === 'starting' && statusLower === 'running') {
    return 'еҒҘеә·жЈҖжҹҘдёӯ'
  }
  
  const healthMap = {
    'healthy': 'еҒҘеә·',
    'unhealthy': 'дёҚеҒҘеә?,
    'starting': 'еҗҜеҠЁдё?,
    'none': 'ж— жЈҖжҹ?
  }
  return healthMap[healthLower] || health
}

const refreshServices = async () => {
  loading.value = true
  try {
    console.log('Fetching custom services from /admin-api/api/v1/custom-services')
    const response = await axios.get('/admin-api/api/v1/custom-services')
    console.log('API response:', response.data)
    services.value = response.data.services || []
    console.log('Services loaded:', services.value.length, 'services')
    if (services.value.length === 0) {
      console.warn('No services returned from API')
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to fetch services:', error)
    console.error('Error response:', error.response)
    ElMessage.error('иҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎеҲ—иЎЁеӨұиҙҘ: ' + (error.response?.data?.detail || error.message))
  } finally {
    loading.value = false
  }
}

// дёҚеҶҚйңҖиҰ?triggerFileSelect еҮҪж•°пјҢдҪҝз”ЁеҺҹз”?label + input ж–№ејҸ

const handleFileInputChange = (event) => {
  // еҺҹз”ҹinputзҡ„changeдәӢд»¶
  const file = event.target.files?.[0]
  if (file) {
    serviceForm.file = file
    console.log('File selected:', file.name)
  }
}

// зӮ№еҮ»гҖҢж·»еҠ жңҚеҠЎгҖҚж—¶е…Ҳж ЎйӘҢи®ёеҸҜиҜҒпјҢжңӘжіЁеҶҢеҲҷи·іиҪ¬еҲ°и®ёеҸҜиҜҒйЎө
async function onAddServiceClick() {
  try {
    const res = await axios.get('/admin-api/api/v1/license')
    if (res.data.valid === true && res.data.registered === true) {
      showAddDialog.value = true
      return
    }
    ElMessage.warning('иҜ·е…Ҳе®ҢжҲҗи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжіЁеҶҢеҗҺеҶҚж·»еҠ иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎ')
    if (typeof setActiveTab === 'function') {
      setActiveTab('license')
    }
  } catch (err) {
    ElMessage.error('йӘҢиҜҒжіЁеҶҢзҠ¶жҖҒеӨұиҙ? ' + (err.response?.data?.detail?.message || err.message))
    if (typeof setActiveTab === 'function') {
      setActiveTab('license')
    }
  }
}


const submitService = async () => {
  if (!serviceFormRef.value) return

  // endpointйӘҢиҜҒе·Із§»йҷӨпјҢзҺ°еңЁйҖҡиҝҮз«ҜеҸЈзӣҙжҺҘи®ҝй—®

  await serviceFormRef.value.validate(async (valid) => {
    if (!valid) return

    submitting.value = true
    try {
      if (editingService.value) {
        // жӣҙж–°жңҚеҠЎ
        const updateData = {
          port: serviceForm.port,
          description: serviceForm.description,
          icon: serviceForm.icon
        }
        // еҰӮжһңе®№еҷЁз«ҜеҸЈдёҺе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈдёҚеҗҢпјҢжүҚж·»еҠ еҲ°жӣҙж–°ж•°жҚ?
        if (serviceForm.container_port && serviceForm.container_port !== serviceForm.port) {
          updateData.container_port = serviceForm.container_port
        }
        // еҶ…еӯҳйҷҗеҲ¶пјҲеҗ« null иЎЁзӨәеҸ–ж¶ҲйҷҗеҲ¶пјүпјҢдҝ®ж”№еҗҺйңҖйҮҚеҗҜз”ҹж•Ҳ
        if (serviceForm.memory_limit_mb !== undefined) {
          updateData.memory_limit_mb = serviceForm.memory_limit_mb
        }
        if (serviceForm.memory_reservation_mb !== undefined) {
          updateData.memory_reservation_mb = serviceForm.memory_reservation_mb
        }
        
        // ж·»еҠ зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®пјҲеҰӮжһңй…ҚзҪ®дәҶпј?
        try {
          const envVarsJsonStr = getEnvVarsJson()
          if (envVarsJsonStr) {
            updateData.env_vars = envVarsJsonStr
          }
        } catch (error) {
          ElMessage.error(error.message || 'зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®й”ҷиҜҜ')
          submitting.value = false
          return
        }
        
        // ж·»еҠ еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®пјҲеҰӮжһңй…ҚзҪ®дәҶпјү
        try {
          const volumesJsonStr = getVolumesJson()
          if (volumesJsonStr) {
            updateData.volumes = volumesJsonStr
          }
        } catch (error) {
          ElMessage.error(error.message || 'еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®й”ҷиҜ?)
          submitting.value = false
          return
        }
        
        await axios.put(
          `/admin-api/api/v1/custom-services/${editingService.value.name}`,
          updateData
        )
        ElMessage.success('жңҚеҠЎжӣҙж–°жҲҗеҠҹ')
      } else {
        // ж·»еҠ жңҚеҠЎ
        if (!serviceForm.file) {
          ElMessage.error('иҜ·йҖүжӢ©Dockerй•ңеғҸtarж–Үд»¶')
          submitting.value = false
          return
        }

        // з¬¬дёҖжӯҘпјҡе…ҲйӘҢиҜҒеҸӮж•°пјҲдёҚж¶үеҸҠж–Үд»¶дёҠдј пјҢеҝ«йҖҹиҝ”еӣһпјү
        try {
          const validateFormData = new FormData()
          validateFormData.append('name', serviceForm.name)
          validateFormData.append('port', serviceForm.port)
          // еҰӮжһңе®№еҷЁз«ҜеҸЈдёҺе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈдёҚеҗҢпјҢжүҚж·»еҠ еҲ°йӘҢиҜҒж•°жҚ?
          if (serviceForm.container_port && serviceForm.container_port !== serviceForm.port) {
            validateFormData.append('container_port', serviceForm.container_port)
          }
          // endpointеҸӮж•°е·Із§»йҷӨпјҢзҺ°еңЁйҖҡиҝҮз«ҜеҸЈзӣҙжҺҘи®ҝй—®
          
          await axios.post('/admin-api/api/v1/custom-services/validate', validateFormData, {
            headers: {
              'Content-Type': 'multipart/form-data'
            },
            timeout: 10000 // 10з§’и¶…ж—¶пјҲйӘҢиҜҒеә”иҜҘеҫҲеҝ«пј?
          })
        } catch (error) {
          // йӘҢиҜҒеӨұиҙҘпјҢз«ӢеҚіиҝ”еӣһпјҢдёҚиҝӣиЎҢж–Үд»¶дёҠдј?
          let errorMessage = 'йӘҢиҜҒеӨұиҙҘ'
          if (error.response?.data?.detail) {
            errorMessage = error.response.data.detail
          } else if (error.response) {
            errorMessage = `жңҚеҠЎеҷЁй”ҷиҜ? ${error.response.status} ${error.response.statusText}`
          }
          ElMessage.error('йғЁзҪІжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: ' + errorMessage)
          submitting.value = false
          return
        }

        // з¬¬дәҢжӯҘпјҡйӘҢиҜҒйҖҡиҝҮеҗҺпјҢеҶҚдёҠдј ж–Үд»?
        const formData = new FormData()
        formData.append('file', serviceForm.file)
        formData.append('name', serviceForm.name)
        formData.append('port', serviceForm.port)
        // еҰӮжһңе®№еҷЁз«ҜеҸЈдёҺе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸЈдёҚеҗҢпјҢжүҚж·»еҠ еҲ°иЎЁеҚ•ж•°жҚ?
        if (serviceForm.container_port && serviceForm.container_port !== serviceForm.port) {
          formData.append('container_port', serviceForm.container_port)
        }
        // endpointеҸӮж•°е·Із§»йҷӨпјҢзҺ°еңЁйҖҡиҝҮз«ҜеҸЈзӣҙжҺҘи®ҝй—®
        formData.append('description', serviceForm.description)
        formData.append('icon', serviceForm.icon)
        if (serviceForm.memory_limit_mb != null && serviceForm.memory_limit_mb !== '') {
          formData.append('memory_limit_mb', serviceForm.memory_limit_mb)
        }
        if (serviceForm.memory_reservation_mb != null && serviceForm.memory_reservation_mb !== '') {
          formData.append('memory_reservation_mb', serviceForm.memory_reservation_mb)
        }
        
        // ж·»еҠ зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®
        try {
          const envVarsJsonStr = getEnvVarsJson()
          console.log('еҮҶеӨҮеҸ‘йҖҒзҡ„зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸ:', envVarsJsonStr)
          if (envVarsJsonStr && envVarsJsonStr.trim()) {
            formData.append('env_vars', envVarsJsonStr)
            console.log('е·Іж·»еҠ зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸеҲ°FormData')
          } else {
            console.log('зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸдёәз©әпјҢи·іиҝ?)
          }
        } catch (error) {
          ElMessage.error(error.message || 'зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®й”ҷиҜҜ')
          submitting.value = false
          return
        }
        
        // ж·»еҠ еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ?
        try {
          const volumesJsonStr = getVolumesJson()
          console.log('еҮҶеӨҮеҸ‘йҖҒзҡ„еҚ·жҢӮиҪ?', volumesJsonStr)
          if (volumesJsonStr && volumesJsonStr.trim()) {
            formData.append('volumes', volumesJsonStr)
            console.log('е·Іж·»еҠ еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪеҲ°FormData')
          } else {
            console.log('еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪдёәз©әпјҢи·іиҝҮ')
          }
        } catch (error) {
          ElMessage.error(error.message || 'еҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ®й”ҷиҜ?)
          submitting.value = false
          return
        }

        await axios.post('/admin-api/api/v1/custom-services/upload', formData, {
          headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'multipart/form-data'
          },
          timeout: 7200000 // 2е°Ҹж—¶и¶…ж—¶пјҲеӨ§ tar дёҠдј пј?
        })

        ElMessage.success('жңҚеҠЎйғЁзҪІжҲҗеҠҹ')
      }

      showAddDialog.value = false
      resetForm()
      await refreshServices()
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('жңҚеҠЎж“ҚдҪңеӨұиҙҘ:', error)
      let errorMessage = 'жңӘзҹҘй”ҷиҜҜ'
      
      if (error.response) {
        // жңҚеҠЎеҷЁиҝ”еӣһдәҶй”ҷиҜҜе“Қеә”
        const detail = error.response.data?.detail || error.response.data?.message
        if (detail) {
          errorMessage = detail
        } else {
          errorMessage = `жңҚеҠЎеҷЁй”ҷиҜ? ${error.response.status} ${error.response.statusText}`
        }
      } else if (error.request) {
        // иҜ·жұӮе·ІеҸ‘еҮәдҪҶжІЎжңүж”¶еҲ°е“Қеә”
        errorMessage = 'ж— жі•иҝһжҺҘеҲ°жңҚеҠЎеҷЁпјҢиҜ·жЈҖжҹҘеҗҺз«ҜжңҚеҠЎжҳҜеҗҰиҝҗиЎ?
      } else {
        // е…¶д»–й”ҷиҜҜ
        errorMessage = error.message || 'жңӘзҹҘй”ҷиҜҜ'
      }
      
      ElMessage.error(
        (editingService.value ? 'жӣҙж–°' : 'йғЁзҪІ') +
        'жңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: ' + errorMessage
      )
    } finally {
      submitting.value = false
    }
  })
}

const editService = async (service) => {
  editingService.value = service
  serviceForm.name = service.name
  serviceForm.description = service.description
  serviceForm.port = service.port
  // endpointе·Із§»йҷӨпјҢзҺ°еңЁйҖҡиҝҮз«ҜеҸЈзӣҙжҺҘи®ҝй—®
  // д»ҺжңҚеҠЎдҝЎжҒҜдёӯиҜ»еҸ–е®№еҷЁз«ҜеҸЈпјҢеҰӮжһңжІЎжңүеҲҷдҪҝз”Ёе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸ?
  serviceForm.container_port = service.container_port || service.port
  previousPort = service.port  // жӣҙж–°previousPortпјҢйҒҝе…Қwatchи§ҰеҸ‘
  serviceForm.memory_limit_mb = service.memory_limit_mb ?? null
  serviceForm.memory_reservation_mb = service.memory_reservation_mb ?? null
  serviceForm.icon = service.icon || 'Box'
  serviceForm.file = null
  
  // еҠ иҪҪзҺ°жңүзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸй…ҚзҪ®
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(`/admin-api/api/v1/custom-services/${service.name}/env`)
    const envVarsObj = response.data.env_vars || {}
    
    if (Object.keys(envVarsObj).length > 0) {
      // иҪ¬жҚўдёәиЎЁеҚ•ж јеј?
      envVars.value = Object.keys(envVarsObj).map(key => ({
        key: key,
        value: envVarsObj[key]
      }))
      // иҪ¬жҚўдёәJSONж јејҸ
      envVarsJson.value = JSON.stringify(envVarsObj, null, 2)
      envTabType.value = 'json' // й»ҳи®ӨжҳҫзӨәJSONжЁЎејҸ
    } else {
      // еҰӮжһңжІЎжңүзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸпјҢжё…з©әпјҲдҪҶдёҚжҳҫзӨәй”ҷиҜҜпјҢеӣ дёәеҸҜиғҪзЎ®е®һжІЎжңүй…ҚзҪ®пјү
      envVars.value = []
      envVarsJson.value = ''
      console.log('иҜҘжңҚеҠЎжңӘй…ҚзҪ®зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸ')
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('еҠ иҪҪзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸеӨұиҙҘ:', error)
    // еҰӮжһңAPIи°ғз”ЁеӨұиҙҘпј?04зӯүпјүпјҢиҜҙжҳҺеҸҜиғҪжІЎжң?envж–Үд»¶пјҢиҝҷжҳҜжӯЈеёёзҡ„
    if (error.response?.status === 404) {
      // 404иЎЁзӨәжІЎжңүй…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶пјҢиҝҷжҳҜжӯЈеёёзҡ„пјҢжё…з©әеҚіеҸ?
      envVars.value = []
      envVarsJson.value = ''
    } else {
      // е…¶д»–й”ҷиҜҜжүҚжҸҗзӨ?
      console.warn('еҠ иҪҪзҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸж—¶еҮәй”?', error.message)
      envVars.value = []
      envVarsJson.value = ''
    }
  }
  
  // еҠ иҪҪзҺ°жңүеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪй…ҚзҪ?
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(`/admin-api/api/v1/custom-services/${service.name}/volumes`)
    const volumesArray = response.data.volumes || []
    
    if (volumesArray.length > 0) {
      // иҪ¬жҚўдёәиЎЁеҚ•ж јеј?
      volumesList.value = volumesArray.map(volume => {
        const parts = volume.split(':')
        const hostPath = parts[0] || ''
        const containerPath = parts[1] || ''
        const readOnly = parts[2] === 'ro'
        return { hostPath, containerPath, readOnly }
      })
      // иҪ¬жҚўдёәJSONж јејҸ
      volumesJson.value = JSON.stringify(volumesArray, null, 2)
      volumesTabType.value = 'json' // й»ҳи®ӨжҳҫзӨәJSONжЁЎејҸ
    } else {
      // еҰӮжһңжІЎжңүеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪпјҢжё…з©ә
      volumesList.value = []
      volumesJson.value = ''
      console.log('иҜҘжңҚеҠЎжңӘй…ҚзҪ®еҚ·жҢӮиҪ?)
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('еҠ иҪҪеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪеӨұиҙ?', error)
    // еҰӮжһңAPIи°ғз”ЁеӨұиҙҘпј?04зӯүпјүпјҢиҜҙжҳҺеҸҜиғҪжІЎжңүй…ҚзҪ®пјҢиҝҷжҳҜжӯЈеёёзҡ?
    if (error.response?.status === 404) {
      volumesList.value = []
      volumesJson.value = ''
    } else {
      console.warn('еҠ иҪҪеҚ·жҢӮиҪҪж—¶еҮәй”ҷ:', error.message)
      volumesList.value = []
      volumesJson.value = ''
    }
  }
  
  showAddDialog.value = true
}

const showServiceDetails = async (service) => {
  selectedService.value = service
  showDetailsDialog.value = true
  await loadServiceLogs()
}

const handleDetailsDialogClose = () => {
  selectedService.value = null
  serviceLogs.value = ''
  logTail.value = 100
}

const loadServiceLogs = async () => {
  if (!selectedService.value) return
  
  logsLoading.value = true
  try {
    // иҮӘе®ҡд№үжңҚеҠЎзҡ„е®№еҷЁеҗҚжҳҜ arbore-{service_name}
    const containerName = `arbore-${selectedService.value.name}`
    const response = await axios.get(`/admin-api/api/v1/services/${containerName}/logs`, {
      params: {
        tail: logTail.value
      }
    })
    
    // е°Ҷж—Ҙеҝ—ж•°з»„жӢјжҺҘжҲҗеӯ—з¬Ұдё?
    serviceLogs.value = response.data.logs?.join('\n') || 'жҡӮж— ж—Ҙеҝ—'
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('еҠ иҪҪж—Ҙеҝ—еӨұиҙҘ:', error)
    const errorMsg = error.response?.data?.detail || error.message || 'жңӘзҹҘй”ҷиҜҜ'
    serviceLogs.value = `еҠ иҪҪж—Ҙеҝ—еӨұиҙҘ: ${errorMsg}`
    ElMessage.error('еҠ иҪҪж—Ҙеҝ—еӨұиҙҘ: ' + errorMsg)
  } finally {
    logsLoading.value = false
  }
}

const restartService = async (service) => {
  try {
    await ElMessageBox.confirm(
      `зЎ®е®ҡиҰҒйҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠ?"${service.name}" еҗ—пјҹ\n\nжӯӨж“ҚдҪңе°ҶйҮҚж–°еҲӣе»әе№¶еҗҜеҠЁе®№еҷЁпјҢд»ҘеҠ иҪҪжңҖж–°зҡ„зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸе’Ңй…ҚзҪ®гҖӮ`,
      'зЎ®и®ӨйҮҚеҗҜе®№еҷЁ',
      {
        confirmButtonText: 'зЎ®е®ҡйҮҚеҗҜ',
        cancelButtonText: 'еҸ–ж¶Ҳ',
        type: 'warning'
      }
    )

    console.log(`жӯЈеңЁйҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎ: ${service.name}`)
    const response = await axios.post(`/admin-api/api/v1/custom-services/${service.name}/restart`)
    console.log('йҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎе“Қеә”:', response.data)
    
    ElMessage.success('жңҚеҠЎйҮҚеҗҜжҲҗеҠҹ')
    await refreshServices()
    // еҰӮжһңиҜҰжғ…еҜ№иҜқжЎҶжү“ејҖпјҢеҲ·ж–°ж—Ҙеҝ?
    if (showDetailsDialog.value && selectedService.value?.name === service.name) {
      await loadServiceLogs()
    }
  } catch (error) {
    if (error !== 'cancel') {
      console.error('йҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ:', error)
      const errorMsg = error.response?.data?.detail || error.message || 'жңӘзҹҘй”ҷиҜҜ'
      ElMessage.error('йҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: ' + errorMsg)
    }
  }
}

const deleteService = async (service) => {
  try {
    await ElMessageBox.confirm(
      `зЎ®е®ҡиҰҒеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠ?"${service.name}" еҗ—пјҹжӯӨж“ҚдҪңе°ҶеҒңжӯўе№¶еҲ йҷӨе®№еҷЁпјҢе№¶д»Һй…ҚзҪ®дёӯз§»йҷӨгҖӮ`,
      'зЎ®и®ӨеҲ йҷӨ',
      {
        confirmButtonText: 'зЎ®е®ҡ',
        cancelButtonText: 'еҸ–ж¶Ҳ',
        type: 'warning'
      }
    )

    console.log(`жӯЈеңЁеҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎ: ${service.name}`)
    const response = await axios.delete(`/admin-api/api/v1/custom-services/${service.name}`)
    console.log('еҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎе“Қеә”:', response.data)
    
    if (response.data.warnings && response.data.warnings.length > 0) {
      ElMessage.warning(`жңҚеҠЎе·ІеҲ йҷӨпјҢдҪҶжңүиӯҰе‘Ҡ: ${response.data.warnings.join('; ')}`)
    } else {
      ElMessage.success('жңҚеҠЎеҲ йҷӨжҲҗеҠҹ')
    }
    await refreshServices()
  } catch (error) {
    if (error !== 'cancel') {
      console.error('еҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ:', error)
      const errorMsg = error.response?.data?.detail || error.message || 'жңӘзҹҘй”ҷиҜҜ'
      ElMessage.error('еҲ йҷӨжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: ' + errorMsg)
    }
  }
}

const resetForm = () => {
  editingService.value = null
  serviceForm.name = ''
  serviceForm.description = ''
  serviceForm.port = 7000  // й»ҳи®Ө7000
  serviceForm.container_port = 7000  // й»ҳи®ӨзӯүдәҺе®ҝдё»жңәз«ҜеҸ?
  serviceForm.memory_limit_mb = null
  serviceForm.memory_reservation_mb = null
  previousPort = 7000  // йҮҚзҪ®previousPort
  // endpointе·Із§»йҷӨпјҢзҺ°еңЁйҖҡиҝҮз«ҜеҸЈзӣҙжҺҘи®ҝй—®
  serviceForm.icon = 'Box'  // йҮҚзҪ®дёәй»ҳи®Өеӣҫж ?
  serviceForm.file = null
  // йҮҚзҪ®зҺҜеўғеҸҳйҮҸ
  envVars.value = []
  envVarsJson.value = ''
  envTabType.value = 'form'
  // йҮҚзҪ®еҚ·жҢӮиҪ?
  volumesList.value = []
  volumesJson.value = ''
  volumesTabType.value = 'form'
  // жё…з©әж–Үд»¶иҫ“е…ҘпјҲдҪҝз”ЁеҺҹз”ҹж–№ејҸпјү
  const fileInput = document.getElementById('file-input-tar')
  if (fileInput) {
    fileInput.value = ''
  }
  if (serviceFormRef.value) {
    serviceFormRef.value.resetFields()
  }
}

// зӣ‘еҗ¬еҜ№иҜқжЎҶе…ій—ӯпјҢйҮҚзҪ®иЎЁеҚ•
const handleDialogClose = () => {
  resetForm()
}

onMounted(() => {
  refreshServices()
})
</script>

    и®ёеҸҜиҜҒз®ЎзҗҶи§Ҷеӣ?/ License Management View

    жң¬з»„д»¶з”ЁдәҺеұ•зӨәе®ҝдё»жңәзЎ¬д»¶жҢҮзә№гҖҒеҪ“еүҚи®ёеҸҜиҜҒзҠ¶жҖҒпјҢе№¶жҸҗдҫӣдёҖдёӘз®ҖжҙҒзҡ„жіЁеҶҢиЎЁеҚ•пј?

    English description:
    This view is responsible for visualizing license status and guiding
    customers through the registration process.  It shows the host hardware
    fingerprint (derived from the machineвҖ‘id of the physical host) and
    offers a small form where the company identifier and validation code
