<script setup>
// и®ёеҸҜиҜҒз®ЎзҗҶйҖ»иҫ‘пјҲLicense management logicпј?
// - fetchLicense:  д»ҺеҗҺз«ҜжӢүеҸ–еҪ“еүҚи®ёеҸҜиҜҒдёҺе®ҝдё»жңәжҢҮзә№дҝЎжҒҜпј?
// - copyFingerprint: ж–№дҫҝз”ЁжҲ·дёҖй”®еӨҚеҲ¶зЎ¬д»¶жҢҮзә№е№¶еҸ‘йҖҒз»ҷе®ўжңҚжҲ–й”Җе”®пјӣ
// - submitRegister: жҸҗдәӨиЎЁеҚ•еҲ°еҗҺз«ҜиҝӣиЎҢи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжіЁеҶҢпјҢе№¶еҲ·ж–°еұ•зӨәзҠ¶жҖҒгҖ?
import { ref, reactive, onMounted } from 'vue'
import axios from 'axios'
import { ElMessage } from 'element-plus'

const license = ref({
  registered: false,
  valid: false,
  errorCode: null,
  hostFingerprint: '',
  companyId: '',
  companyName: '',
  versionInfo: '',
})
const loading = ref(false)
const submitting = ref(false)
const formRef = ref(null)

const form = reactive({
  companyId: '',
  validationCode: '',
  companyName: '',
})

const formRules = {
  companyId: [{ required: true, message: 'иҜ·иҫ“е…ҘдјҒдёҡID', trigger: 'blur' }],
  validationCode: [{ required: true, message: 'иҜ·иҫ“е…Ҙж ЎйӘҢз Ғ', trigger: 'blur' }],
  companyName: [{ required: true, message: 'иҜ·иҫ“е…ҘдјҒдёҡеҗҚз§?, trigger: 'blur' }],
}

const apiBase = '/admin-api'
const licenseApiUrl = () => `${apiBase}/api/v1/license`
const fingerprintApiUrl = () => `${apiBase}/api/v1/license/hardware-fingerprint`
const registerApiUrl = () => `${apiBase}/api/v1/license/register`

async function fetchLicense() {
  loading.value = true
  try {
    const res = await axios.get(licenseApiUrl())
    license.value = {
      registered: !!res.data.registered,
      valid: !!res.data.valid,
      errorCode: res.data.errorCode || null,
      hostFingerprint: res.data.hostFingerprint || '',
      companyId: res.data.companyId || '',
      companyName: res.data.companyName || '',
      versionInfo: res.data.versionInfo || '',
    }
  } catch (err) {
    license.value.registered = false
    license.value.hostFingerprint = 'иҺ·еҸ–еӨұиҙҘ'
    ElMessage.error('иҺ·еҸ–и®ёеҸҜиҜҒдҝЎжҒҜеӨұиҙ? ' + (err.response?.data?.detail?.message || err.message))
  } finally {
    loading.value = false
  }
}

function copyFingerprint() {
  const text = license.value.hostFingerprint
  if (!text || text === 'еҠ иҪҪдё?..' || text === 'иҺ·еҸ–еӨұиҙҘ') {
    ElMessage.warning('ж— еҸҜеӨҚеҲ¶зҡ„дё»жңәж ҮиҜ?)
    return
  }
  if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(
      () => ElMessage.success('е·ІеӨҚеҲ¶еҲ°еүӘиҙҙжқ?),
      () => fallbackCopy(text)
    )
  } else {
    fallbackCopy(text)
  }
}

function fallbackCopy(text) {
  const ta = document.createElement('textarea')
  ta.value = text
  ta.style.position = 'fixed'
  ta.style.opacity = '0'
  document.body.appendChild(ta)
  ta.select()
  try {
    document.execCommand('copy')
    ElMessage.success('е·ІеӨҚеҲ¶еҲ°еүӘиҙҙжқ?)
  } catch (e) {
    ElMessage.error('еӨҚеҲ¶еӨұиҙҘ')
  }
  document.body.removeChild(ta)
}

async function submitRegister() {
  if (!formRef.value) return
  await formRef.value.validate(async (valid) => {
    if (!valid) return
    submitting.value = true
    try {
      const fd = new FormData()
      fd.append('companyId', form.companyId)
      fd.append('validationCode', form.validationCode)
      fd.append('companyName', form.companyName)
      await axios.post(registerApiUrl(), fd, {
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'multipart/form-data' },
      })
      ElMessage.success('и®ёеҸҜиҜҒжіЁеҶҢжҲҗеҠ?)
      form.companyId = ''
      form.validationCode = ''
      form.companyName = ''
      await fetchLicense()
    } catch (err) {
      const detail = err.response?.data?.detail
      const msg = (detail && (detail.message || detail)) || err.message
      ElMessage.error('жіЁеҶҢеӨұиҙҘ: ' + msg)
    } finally {
      submitting.value = false
    }
  })
}

onMounted(() => {
  fetchLicense()
})
</script>

  <!--
    ж—Ҙеҝ—жҹҘзңӢи§Ҷеӣҫ / Logs View

    дёӯж–ҮиҜҙжҳҺпј?    жң¬з»„д»¶дёәиҝҗз»ҙдәәе‘ҳжҸҗдҫӣз»ҹдёҖзҡ„ж—Ҙеҝ—е…ҘеҸЈпјҢеҸҜд»ҘеңЁжөҸи§ҲеҷЁдёӯзӣҙжҺҘжҹҘзң?Web Admin
    жҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°иҮӘиә«ж—Ҙеҝ—д»ҘеҸҠеҗ„дёӘдёҡеҠЎжңҚеҠЎзҡ„е®№еҷЁж—Ҙеҝ—пјҢд»ҺиҖҢеңЁдёҚзҷ»еҪ•жңҚеҠЎеҷЁзҡ„жғ…еҶөдёӢ

    This view lets operators inspect logs produced by the webвҖ‘admin backend
    service itself as well as logs from individual business services
    (Docker containers).  It is intentionally simple but powerful enough
    for firstвҖ‘line troubleshooting without SSH access.
  -->
  <div class="logs-view">
    <!-- жҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°жңҚеҠЎпјҲWeb Admin APIпјүиҮӘиә«ж—Ҙеҝ?-->
    <el-card class="log-section-card" shadow="never">
      <template #header>
        <span>жҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°жңҚеҠЎж—Ҙеҝ—пјҲWeb Admin APIпј?/span>

      <p class="section-desc">жҹҘзңӢжң¬з®ЎзҗҶжҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°еҗҺз«Ҝзҡ„иҝҗиЎҢж—Ҙеҝ—пјҢдҫҝдәҺжҺ’жҹҘй—®йўҳгҖ?/p>
      <el-button type="primary" @click="loadAdminLogs" :loading="loadingAdmin">
        еҠ иҪҪжҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°ж—Ҙеҝ?      </el-button>
    </el-card>

    <el-form :inline="true" class="logs-form">
      <el-form-item label="йҖүжӢ©жңҚеҠЎ">
        <el-select
          v-model="selectedService"

          style="width: 200px;"
          :loading="loadingServices"
          filterable
        >
          <el-option
            v-for="service in serviceList"
            :key="service"

            :value="service"

<script setup>
// ж—Ҙеҝ—жҹҘзңӢйҖ»иҫ‘пјҲLog viewing logicпј?// - fetchServiceList: дёҺжңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖҒйЎөеӨҚз”ЁеҗҺз«Ҝж•°жҚ®пјҢеҠЁжҖҒиҺ·еҫ—жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°еҲ—иЎЁпјӣ
// - loadAdminLogs: еҠ иҪҪжҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°еҗҺз«ҜиҮӘиә«зҡ„ж—Ҙеҝ—ж–Үд»¶пјҢж–№дҫҝжҺ’жҹ?API й—®йўҳпј?// - loadLogs:      жҢүз…§з”ЁжҲ·йҖүжӢ©зҡ„жңҚеҠЎеҗҚиҺ·еҸ–еҜ№еә”е®№еҷЁзҡ„жңҖж–°ж—Ҙеҝ—зүҮж®өгҖ?import { ref, computed, onMounted } from 'vue'
import axios from 'axios'
import { ElMessage } from 'element-plus'

const selectedService = ref('arbore-flow')
const tail = ref(100)
const logs = ref([])
const loading = ref(false)
const loadingAdmin = ref(false)
const serviceList = ref([])
const loadingServices = ref(false)
const logSource = ref('') // 'admin' | 'service'
const logSourceLabel = computed(() =>
  logSource.value === 'admin' ? 'жҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°жңҚеҠЎж—Ҙеҝ? : (logSource.value === 'service' && selectedService.value ? `${selectedService.value} ж—Ҙеҝ—` : 'ж—Ҙеҝ—')
)

// д»ҺеҗҺз«?/api/v1/services жӢүеҸ–жңҚеҠЎеҲ—иЎЁпјҢдёҺгҖҢжңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖҒгҖҚдёҖиҮҙпјҢйҒҝе…ҚзЎ¬зј–з ҒйҒ—жјҸпјҲеҰ?quickchartпј?const fetchServiceList = async () => {
  loadingServices.value = true
  try {
    const res = await axios.get('/api/v1/services')
    const list = (res.data?.services || []).map(s => s.name).filter(Boolean)
    if (list.length) {
      serviceList.value = list
      if (!list.includes(selectedService.value)) {
        selectedService.value = list[0]
      }
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('иҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎеҲ—иЎЁеӨұиҙҘ:', e)
    serviceList.value = []
  } finally {
    loadingServices.value = false
  }
}

onMounted(() => {
  fetchServiceList()
})

const loadAdminLogs = async () => {
  loadingAdmin.value = true
  try {
    const response = await axios.get('/api/v1/system/admin-logs', {
      params: { tail: 200 }
    })
    logs.value = Array.isArray(response.data?.logs) ? response.data.logs : []
    logSource.value = 'admin'
    ElMessage.success('жҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°ж—Ҙеҝ—еҠ иҪҪжҲҗеҠ?)
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('еҠ иҪҪжҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°ж—Ҙеҝ—еӨұиҙ? ' + error.message)
    logs.value = []
  } finally {
    loadingAdmin.value = false
  }
}

const loadLogs = async () => {
  if (!selectedService.value) {
    ElMessage.warning('иҜ·е…ҲйҖүжӢ©жңҚеҠЎ')
    return
  }
  
  loading.value = true
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(`/api/v1/services/${selectedService.value}/logs`, {
      params: { tail: tail.value }
    })
    logs.value = Array.isArray(response.data?.logs) ? response.data.logs : []
    logSource.value = 'service'
    ElMessage.success('ж—Ҙеҝ—еҠ иҪҪжҲҗеҠҹ')
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('еҠ иҪҪж—Ҙеҝ—еӨұиҙҘ: ' + error.message)
    logs.value = []
  } finally {
    loading.value = false
  }
}
</script>

<template>
  <!--
    зі»з»ҹиө„жәҗзӣ‘жҺ§и§Ҷеӣҫ / System Resources View

    дёӯж–ҮиҜҙжҳҺпј?
    жң¬з»„д»¶йҖҡиҝҮи°ғз”ЁеҗҺз«Ҝ /api/v1/system/resources жҺҘеҸЈпјҢе®ҡжңҹиҺ·еҸ?CPUгҖҒеҶ…еӯҳгҖ?
    зЈҒзӣҳзӯүе…ій”®иө„жәҗзҡ„дҪҝз”Ёжғ…еҶөпјҢе№¶д»ҘиҝӣеәҰжқЎзҡ„ж–№ејҸиҝӣиЎҢеҸҜи§ҶеҢ–еұ•зӨәгҖӮиҜҘйЎөйқўдё»иҰҒ
    йқўеҗ‘иҝҗз»ҙдәәе‘ҳпјҢз”ЁдәҺеҝ«йҖҹеҲӨж–ӯеҪ“еүҚе®ҝдё»жңәжҳҜеҗҰеӯҳеңЁиө„жәҗз“¶йўҲгҖ?

    English description:
    This component periodically polls the `/api/v1/system/resources` endpoint
    to retrieve CPU, memory and disk utilization metrics of the host machine.
    The data is rendered as progress bars so that operators can quickly spot
    abnormal resource consumption patterns (for example memory exhaustion or
    disk almost full).
  -->
  <div class="resources-view">
    <el-row :gutter="20">
      <el-col :span="24">
        <el-card shadow="hover" class="resource-card">
          <template #header>
            <span>CPUдҪҝз”ЁзҺ?/span>
          </template>
          <div class="resource-item">
            <el-progress 
              :percentage="resources.cpu.percent" 
              :color="getColor(resources.cpu.percent)"
              :stroke-width="20"
            />
            <p style="margin-top: 10px;">
              ж ёеҝғж•? {{ resources.cpu.count }}
            </p>
          </div>
        </el-card>
      </el-col>
      
      <el-col :span="24">
        <el-card shadow="hover" class="resource-card">
          <template #header>
            <span>еҶ…еӯҳдҪҝз”Ё</span>
          </template>
          <div class="resource-item">
            <el-progress 
              :percentage="resources.memory.percent" 
              :color="getColor(resources.memory.percent)"
              :stroke-width="20"
            />
            <p style="margin-top: 10px;">
              е·Із”Ё: {{ formatBytes(resources.memory.used) }} / 
              {{ formatBytes(resources.memory.total) }}
            </p>
          </div>
        </el-card>
      </el-col>
      
      <el-col :span="24">
        <el-card shadow="hover" class="resource-card">
          <template #header>
            <span>зЈҒзӣҳдҪҝз”Ё</span>
          </template>
          <div class="resource-item">
            <el-progress 
              :percentage="resources.disk.percent" 
              :color="getColor(resources.disk.percent)"
              :stroke-width="20"
            />
            <p style="margin-top: 10px;">
              е·Із”Ё: {{ formatBytes(resources.disk.used) }} / 
              {{ formatBytes(resources.disk.total) }}
            </p>
          </div>
        </el-card>
      </el-col>
    </el-row>
    
    <el-button 
      type="primary" 
      @click="refreshResources" 
      :loading="loading"
      style="margin-top: 20px;"
    >
      еҲ·ж–°иө„жәҗ
    </el-button>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
// иө„жәҗзӣ‘жҺ§йҖ»иҫ‘пјҲResource monitoring logicпј?
// иҒҢиҙЈиҜҙжҳҺпј?
// 1) е®ҡжңҹд»ҺеҗҺз«ҜжӢүеҸ–жңҖж–°иө„жәҗдҪҝз”Ёжғ…еҶөпјӣ
// 2) е°ҶеҺҹе§Ӣеӯ—иҠӮж•°иҪ¬жҚўдёәдәәзұ»еҸҜиҜ»зҡ„еҚ•дҪҚеӯ—з¬ҰдёІпјӣ
// 3) ж №жҚ®еҚ з”ЁзҷҫеҲҶжҜ”иҝ”еӣһеҜ№еә”зҡ„йўңиүІпјҢеҪўжҲҗзӣҙи§Ӯзҡ„йЈҺйҷ©ж„ҹзҹҘгҖ?
import { ref, onMounted } from 'vue'
import axios from 'axios'
import { ElMessage } from 'element-plus'

const resources = ref({
  cpu: { percent: 0, count: 0 },
  memory: { total: 0, used: 0, percent: 0 },
  disk: { total: 0, used: 0, percent: 0 }
})
const loading = ref(false)

// ж №жҚ®еҚ жҜ”иҝ”еӣһиҝӣеәҰжқЎйўңиүІпјҲз»?/ ж©?/ зәўпјү
// Map percentage to progress-bar color (green / orange / red).
const getColor = (percent) => {
  if (percent < 50) return '#10b981'  // Arboreе“ҒзүҢз»ҝиүІ
  if (percent < 80) return '#f59e0b'  // ж©ҷиүІиӯҰе‘Ҡ
  return '#ef4444'  // зәўиүІеҚұйҷ©
}

const formatBytes = (bytes) => {
  if (bytes === 0) return '0 B'
  const k = 1024
  const sizes = ['B', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB', 'TB']
  const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k))
  return Math.round(bytes / Math.pow(k, i) * 100) / 100 + ' ' + sizes[i]
}

const refreshResources = async () => {
  loading.value = true
  try {
    const response = await axios.get('/api/v1/system/resources')
    resources.value = response.data
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('иҺ·еҸ–зі»з»ҹиө„жәҗеӨұиҙҘ: ' + error.message)
  } finally {
    loading.value = false
  }
}

onMounted(() => {
  refreshResources()
  // жҜ?0з§’иҮӘеҠЁеҲ·ж–?
  setInterval(refreshResources, 10000)
})
</script>

<style scoped>
.resources-view {
  padding: 20px 0;
}

.resources-view :deep(.el-card) {
  background: rgba(30, 41, 59, 0.5);
  border: 1px solid rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.1);
  border-radius: 8px;
}

.resources-view :deep(.el-card__header) {
  background: rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.5);
  border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.1);
  color: #f1f5f9;
}

.resources-view :deep(.el-card__body) {
  background: rgba(30, 41, 59, 0.3);
  color: #f1f5f9;
}

.resource-card {
  margin-bottom: 20px;
}

.resource-item {
  padding: 10px 0;
}

.resource-item p {
  color: #94a3b8;
  margin-top: 10px;
}
</style>

<template>
  <!--
    жңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖҒи§Ҷеӣ?/ Services View

    дёӯж–ҮиҜҙжҳҺпј?
    жң¬з»„д»¶иҙҹиҙЈйӣҶдёӯеұ•зӨ?Arbore AI Host е№іеҸ°дёӯеҗ„дёӘж ёеҝғжңҚеҠЎпјҲDocker е®№еҷЁжҲ?systemd
    жңҚеҠЎпјүзҡ„иҝҗиЎҢзҠ¶жҖҒгҖҒеҒҘеә·жЈҖжҹҘз»“жһңд»ҘеҸҠеёёз”Ёж“ҚдҪңе…ҘеҸЈгҖӮйЎөйқўдёҠзҡ„жҜҸдёҖдёӘеҚЎзүҮйғҪеҜ№еә”
    дёҖдёӘйҖ»иҫ‘жңҚеҠЎе®һдҫӢпјҢж”ҜжҢҒдёҖй”®еҗҜеҠЁгҖҒеҒңжӯўгҖҒйҮҚеҗҜд»ҘеҸҠи·іиҪ¬еҲ° Web жҺ§еҲ¶еҸ°зӯүеҠЁдҪңгҖ?

    English description:
    This view aggregates the runtime state of all core services that make up
    the Arbore AI Host platform.  Each card represents either a Docker
    container based service or a systemd unit and exposes shortcuts to open
    its web UI (if any), as well as start/stop/restart controls.

    и®ҫи®Ўе…іжіЁзӮ?/ Design considerations:
    - жё…жҷ°зҡ„зҠ¶жҖҒж ҮиҜҶпјҡеҗҢж—¶еұ•зӨәеҺҹе§ӢзҠ¶жҖҒеӯ—ж®өе’Ңзҝ»иҜ‘еҗҺзҡ„дёӯж–Үж–ҮжЎҲпјҢйҒҝе…ҚиҜҜи§ЈгҖ?
    - и®ёеҸҜиҜҒиҒ”еҠЁпјҡеҪ“и®ёеҸҜиҜҒж— ж•Ҳж—¶пјҢзҰҒжӯўж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠЎзҡ„еҗҜеҒңж“ҚдҪңпјҢе№¶еңЁйЎ¶йғЁз»ҷеҮәжҸҗзӨәгҖ?
    - еҸҜжү©еұ•й…ҚзҪ®пјҡжңҚеҠЎзҡ„еұ•зӨәеҗҚз§°дёҺи®ҝй—® URL жҠҪзҰ»еҲ?serviceConfig дёӯпјҢж–№дҫҝеҗҺз»ӯ
      еўһеҮҸжңҚеҠЎжҲ–жӣҙжҚўз«ҜеҸЈж—¶еҸӘдҝ®ж”№й…ҚзҪ®иҖҢж— йңҖи°ғж•ҙжЁЎжқҝз»“жһ„гҖ?
  -->
  <div class="services-view">
    <el-alert
      v-if="!licenseValid && licenseErrorCode"
      type="warning"
      :closable="false"
      show-icon
      class="license-alert"
    >
      <template #title>
        жңӘжіЁеҶҢжҲ–и®ёеҸҜиҜҒж— ж•ҲпјҢж ҮеҮҶжңҚеҠЎж— жі•еҗҜеҠЁ/йҮҚеҗҜгҖӮиҜ·еүҚеҫҖгҖҢи®ёеҸҜиҜҒгҖҚйЎөе®ҢжҲҗжіЁеҶҢгҖ?
      </template>
    </el-alert>
    <el-row :gutter="20">
      <el-col :span="8" v-for="service in services" :key="service.name">
        <el-card class="service-card" shadow="hover">
          <template #header>
            <div class="card-header">
              <span class="service-name">{{ getServiceDisplayName(service.name) }}</span>
              <el-tag :type="getStatusType(service.status)" size="small">
                {{ getStatusText(service.status) }}
              </el-tag>
            </div>
          </template>
          
          <div class="service-info">
            <p><strong>зҠ¶жҖ?</strong> {{ service.status }}</p>
            <p v-if="service.health !== 'unknown'">
              <strong>еҒҘеә·:</strong> 
              <el-tag :type="service.health === 'healthy' ? 'success' : 'warning'" size="small">
                {{ service.health }}
              </el-tag>
            </p>
            <p v-if="service.ports.length > 0">
              <strong>з«ҜеҸЈ:</strong> {{ service.ports.join(', ') }}
            </p>
            <p v-if="service.type === 'systemd'">
              <strong>зұ»еһӢ:</strong> <el-tag size="small">Systemd</el-tag>
            </p>
            
            <div class="service-actions" style="margin-top: 10px;">
              <el-button 
                type="primary" 
                size="small" 
                @click="openService(service)"
                :disabled="service.status !== 'running'"
                style="margin-right: 5px;"
              >
                и®ҝй—®жңҚеҠЎ
              </el-button>
              
              <el-button 
                v-if="service.status !== 'running' && (service.type === 'systemd' || service.name.startsWith('service-'))"
                type="success" 
                size="small" 
                @click="startService(service)"
                :loading="service.loading"
                :disabled="!licenseValid"
                style="margin-right: 5px;"
              >
                еҗҜеҠЁ
              </el-button>
              
              <el-button 
                v-if="service.status === 'running' && (service.type === 'systemd' || service.name.startsWith('service-'))"
                type="warning" 
                size="small" 
                @click="stopService(service)"
                :loading="service.loading"
                style="margin-right: 5px;"
              >
                еҒңжӯў
              </el-button>
              
              <el-button 
                v-if="service.status === 'running' && (service.type === 'systemd' || service.name.startsWith('service-'))"
                type="info" 
                size="small" 
                @click="restartService(service)"
                :loading="service.loading"
                :disabled="!licenseValid"
              >
                йҮҚеҗҜ
              </el-button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </el-card>
      </el-col>
    </el-row>
    
    <el-button 
      type="primary" 
      @click="refreshServices" 
      :loading="loading"
      style="margin-top: 20px;"
    >
      еҲ·ж–°зҠ¶жҖ?
    </el-button>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
// жңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖҒи§ҶеӣҫйҖ»иҫ‘еұӮпјҲscript йғЁеҲҶпј?
// Script section for the Services View component.
// иҝҷйҮҢдё»иҰҒе®ҢжҲҗдёүзұ»е·ҘдҪңпј?
// 1) дёҺеҗҺз«?/api/v1/services API дәӨдә’пјҢиҺ·еҸ–еҪ“еүҚжңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖҒеҸҠи®ёеҸҜиҜҒж ЎйӘҢз»“жһңпјӣ
// 2) ж №жҚ®зҠ¶жҖҒдҝЎжҒҜжҺЁеҜјеҮәж ҮзӯҫйўңиүІгҖҒж–ҮжЎҲзӯүеұ•зӨәз»ҶиҠӮпј?
// 3) е°ҒиЈ…еҜ№еҚ•дёӘжңҚеҠЎзҡ„еҗҜеҠЁ / еҒңжӯў / йҮҚеҗҜзӯүж“ҚдҪңпјҢз»ҹдёҖеӨ„зҗҶй”ҷиҜҜжҸҗзӨәгҖ?

import { ref, onMounted } from 'vue'
import axios from 'axios'
import { ElMessage } from 'element-plus'

const services = ref([])
const loading = ref(false)
const licenseValid = ref(true)
const licenseErrorCode = ref(null)

// иҺ·еҸ–еҪ“еүҚжңҚеҠЎеҷ?IPпјҲд»ҺжөҸи§ҲеҷЁи®ҝй—®ең°еқҖдёӯжҺЁеҜјпјү
// Get current server IP from window.location, so that the sameеүҚз«Ҝ
// йЎөйқўеҸҜд»ҘеңЁдёҚеҗҢйғЁзҪІзҺҜеўғдёӢиҮӘеҠЁйҖӮй…ҚеҗҺз«Ҝдё»жңәең°еқҖгҖ?
const getServerIP = () => {
  return window.location.hostname
}

// жңҚеҠЎеұ•зӨәй…ҚзҪ®пјҲService display configurationпј?
// key дёәеҗҺз«Ҝиҝ”еӣһзҡ„жңҚеҠЎеҗҚз§°пјҢvalue дёӯеҢ…еҗ«дёӯж–Үеұ•зӨәеҗҚе’ҢеҸҜйҖүзҡ„ Web и®ҝй—®ең°еқҖгҖ?
// жӯӨеӨ„ж•…ж„ҸдҝқжҢҒдёәдёҖдёӘйӣҶдёӯй…ҚзҪ®еқ—пјҢж–№дҫҝеңЁиҪҜд»¶и‘—дҪңжқғж–ҮжЎЈдёӯиҜҙжҳҺеҗ„дёӘеӯҗзі»з»ҹдҪңз”ЁгҖ?
const serviceConfig = {
  'arbore-flow': { name: 'е·ҘдҪңжөҒжңҚеҠ?, url: () => `http://${getServerIP()}:5678` },
  'arbore-func': { name: 'еә”з”ЁжңҚеҠЎ', url: () => `http://${getServerIP()}:13000` },
  'arbore-postgres-nocobase': { name: 'PostgreSQL (еә”з”Ёж•°жҚ®еә?', url: null },
  'arbore-postgres-vector': { name: 'PostgreSQL (еҗ‘йҮҸж•°жҚ®еә?', url: null },
  'arbore-ollama': { name: 'AIжЁЎеһӢжңҚеҠЎ', url: () => `http://${getServerIP()}:11434` },
  'arbore-ollama-webui': { name: 'AIжЁЎеһӢз•Ңйқў', url: () => `http://${getServerIP()}:3000` },
  'arbore-quickchart': { name: 'еӣҫиЎЁз”ҹжҲҗжңҚеҠЎ', url: () => `http://${getServerIP()}/quickchart` },
  // service-router е·Із§»йҷӨпјҢжүҖжңүжңҚеҠЎйҖҡиҝҮ nginx зӣҙжҺҘеҸҚеҗ‘д»ЈзҗҶ
  // 'service-router': { name: 'жңҚеҠЎи·Ҝз”ұ (PDF/OCR)', url: () => `http://${getServerIP()}:2026` },
  'service-pdf-to-png': { name: 'PDFиҪ¬PNGжңҚеҠЎ', url: null },
  'service-paddle-ocr': { name: 'PaddleOCRжңҚеҠЎ', url: null },
  'service-tesseract-ocr': { name: 'Tesseract OCRжңҚеҠЎ', url: null }
}

const getServiceDisplayName = (name) => {
  return serviceConfig[name]?.name || name
}

const getStatusType = (status) => {
  const statusMap = {
    'running': 'success',
    'stopped': 'danger',
    'exited': 'danger',
    'restarting': 'warning',
    'not_found': 'info',
    'unknown': 'info'
  }
  return statusMap[status] || 'info'
}

const getStatusText = (status) => {
  const statusMap = {
    'running': 'иҝҗиЎҢдё?,
    'stopped': 'е·ІеҒңжӯ?,
    'exited': 'е·ІеҒңжӯ?,
    'restarting': 'йҮҚеҗҜдё?,
    'not_found': 'жңӘжүҫеҲ?,
    'unknown': 'жңӘзҹҘ'
  }
  return statusMap[status] || status
}

const openService = (service) => {
  const config = serviceConfig[service.name]
  if (config && config.url) {
    // еҰӮжһңurlжҳҜеҮҪж•°пјҢи°ғз”Ёе®ғиҺ·еҸ–URL
    const url = typeof config.url === 'function' ? config.url() : config.url
    try {
      window.open(url, '_blank', 'noopener,noreferrer')
    } catch (error) {
      ElMessage.error('ж— жі•жү“ејҖжңҚеҠЎең°еқҖ: ' + error.message)
      // еҰӮжһңеј№зӘ—иў«йҳ»жӯўпјҢе°қиҜ•зӣҙжҺҘи·іиҪ¬
      window.location.href = url
    }
  } else {
    ElMessage.info('иҜҘжңҚеҠЎжІЎжңүWebи®ҝй—®ең°еқҖ')
  }
}

const refreshServices = async () => {
  loading.value = true
  try {
    const response = await axios.get('/api/v1/services')
    services.value = (response.data.services || []).map(service => ({
      ...service,
      loading: false
    }))
    licenseValid.value = response.data.licenseValid !== false
    licenseErrorCode.value = response.data.licenseErrorCode || null
    ElMessage.success('жңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖҒе·Іжӣҙж–°')
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('иҺ·еҸ–жңҚеҠЎзҠ¶жҖҒеӨұиҙ? ' + error.message)
  } finally {
    loading.value = false
  }
}

const startService = async (service) => {
  if (!licenseValid.value) {
    ElMessage.warning('иҜ·е…Ҳе®ҢжҲҗи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжіЁеҶ?)
    return
  }
  service.loading = true
  try {
    const response = await axios.post(`/api/v1/services/${service.name}/start`)
    ElMessage.success(response.data.message || 'жңҚеҠЎеҗҜеҠЁжҲҗеҠҹ')
    await refreshServices()
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('еҗҜеҠЁжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: ' + (error.response?.data?.detail || error.message))
  } finally {
    service.loading = false
  }
}

const stopService = async (service) => {
  service.loading = true
  try {
    const response = await axios.post(`/api/v1/services/${service.name}/stop`)
    ElMessage.success(response.data.message || 'жңҚеҠЎеҒңжӯўжҲҗеҠҹ')
    await refreshServices()
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('еҒңжӯўжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: ' + (error.response?.data?.detail || error.message))
  } finally {
    service.loading = false
  }
}

const restartService = async (service) => {
  if (!licenseValid.value) {
    ElMessage.warning('иҜ·е…Ҳе®ҢжҲҗи®ёеҸҜиҜҒжіЁеҶ?)
    return
  }
  service.loading = true
  try {
    const response = await axios.post(`/api/v1/services/${service.name}/restart`)
    ElMessage.success(response.data.message || 'жңҚеҠЎйҮҚеҗҜжҲҗеҠҹ')
    await refreshServices()
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('йҮҚеҗҜжңҚеҠЎеӨұиҙҘ: ' + (error.response?.data?.detail || error.message))
  } finally {
    service.loading = false
  }
}

onMounted(() => {
  refreshServices()
  // жҜ?0з§’иҮӘеҠЁеҲ·ж–?
  setInterval(refreshServices, 30000)
})
</script>

<style scoped>
.services-view {
  padding: 20px 0;
}

.service-card {
  margin-bottom: 20px;
  height: 100%;
  background: rgba(30, 41, 59, 0.5);
  border: 1px solid rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.1);
  border-radius: 8px;
}

.service-card :deep(.el-card__header) {
  background: rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.5);
  border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.1);
  color: #f1f5f9;
}

.service-card :deep(.el-card__body) {
  background: rgba(30, 41, 59, 0.3);
  color: #f1f5f9;
}

.card-header {
  display: flex;
  justify-content: space-between;
  align-items: center;
}

.service-name {
  font-weight: 600;
  font-size: 16px;
  color: #f1f5f9;
}

.service-info p {
  margin: 8px 0;
  font-size: 14px;
  color: #94a3b8;
}

.service-info p strong {
  color: #f1f5f9;
}

.license-alert {
  margin-bottom: 20px;
  background: rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.1);
  border: 1px solid rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.3);
}
</style>

<template>
  <!--
    зі»з»ҹй…ҚзҪ®и§Ҷеӣҫ / System Configuration View

    дёӯж–ҮиҜҙжҳҺпј?
    жң¬йЎөйқўз”ЁдәҺеұ•зӨәе’Ңдҝ®ж”№дёҺжңҚеҠЎеҷЁ IP зӣёе…ізҡ„й…ҚзҪ®гҖӮеҫҲеӨҡдёӢжёёжңҚеҠЎпјҲеҰ?NginxгҖ?
    дёҡеҠЎ API зӯүпјүеңЁз”ҹжҲҗи®ҝй—®ең°еқҖжҲ–еӣһи°?URL ж—¶пјҢйғҪдҫқиө–дәҺз»ҹдёҖзҡ?SERVER_IP
    и®ҫзҪ®пјҢеӣ жӯӨйңҖиҰҒжҸҗдҫӣдёҖдёӘз®ҖеҚ•гҖҒе®үе…Ёдё”еҸҜи§ҶеҢ–зҡ„дҝ®ж”№е…ҘеҸЈгҖ?

    English description:
    This view exposes a small but important configuration surface: the
    canonical server IP address.  Multiple downstream components rely on
    this value when constructing public URLs or callback endpoints, so the
    UI guides operators through refreshing, validating and persisting the
    correct IP into configuration files.
  -->
  <div class="system-config-view">
    <el-card class="config-card" shadow="hover">
      <template #header>
        <div class="card-header">
          <span class="card-title">жңҚеҠЎеҷЁIPең°еқҖй…ҚзҪ®</span>
        </div>
      </template>
      
      <div class="ip-info-section">
        <el-descriptions :column="1" border>
          <el-descriptions-item label="еҪ“еүҚжңҚеҠЎеҷЁIP">
            <el-tag type="info" size="large">{{ ipInfo.current_ip || 'жЈҖжөӢдёӯ...' }}</el-tag>
            <el-button 
              type="text" 
              size="small" 
              @click="refreshIpInfo"
              :loading="loading"
              style="margin-left: 10px;"
            >
              <el-icon><Refresh /></el-icon>
              еҲ·ж–°
            </el-button>
          </el-descriptions-item>
          
          <el-descriptions-item label="й…ҚзҪ®зҡ„IPең°еқҖ">
            <el-tag 
              :type="ipInfo.needs_update ? 'warning' : 'success'" 
              size="large"
            >
              {{ ipInfo.configured_ip || 'жңӘй…ҚзҪ? }}
            </el-tag>
          </el-descriptions-item>
          
          <el-descriptions-item label="зҠ¶жҖ?>
            <el-alert
              v-if="ipInfo.needs_update"
              type="warning"
              :closable="false"
              show-icon
            >
              <template #title>
                <strong>IPең°еқҖдёҚеҢ№й…?/strong>
                <p style="margin: 5px 0 0 0; font-size: 12px;">
                  еҪ“еүҚжңҚеҠЎеҷЁIP ({{ ipInfo.current_ip }}) дёҺй…ҚзҪ®зҡ„IP ({{ ipInfo.configured_ip }}) дёҚдёҖиҮ?
                </p>
              </template>
            </el-alert>
            <el-alert
              v-else-if="ipInfo.configured_ip"
              type="success"
              :closable="false"
              show-icon
            >
              <template #title>
                <strong>IPең°еқҖй…ҚзҪ®жӯЈзЎ®</strong>
                <p style="margin: 5px 0 0 0; font-size: 12px;">
                  еҪ“еүҚжңҚеҠЎеҷЁIPдёҺй…ҚзҪ®зҡ„IPдёҖиҮ?
                </p>
              </template>
            </el-alert>
            <el-alert
              v-else
              type="info"
              :closable="false"
              show-icon
            >
              <template #title>
                <strong>йҰ–ж¬Ўй…ҚзҪ®</strong>
                <p style="margin: 5px 0 0 0; font-size: 12px;">
                  иҜ·зӮ№еҮ»дёӢж–№жҢүй’®е°ҶеҪ“еүҚIPең°еқҖдҝқеӯҳеҲ°й…ҚзҪ®дёӯ
                </p>
              </template>
            </el-alert>
          </el-descriptions-item>
        </el-descriptions>
      </div>
      
      <div class="action-section" style="margin-top: 30px;">
        <el-button 
          type="primary" 
          size="large"
          @click="updateIp"
          :loading="updating"
          :disabled="!ipInfo.needs_update && ipInfo.configured_ip !== ''"
        >
          <el-icon><Setting /></el-icon>
          {{ ipInfo.configured_ip ? 'жӣҙж–°IPй…ҚзҪ®' : 'дҝқеӯҳеҪ“еүҚIPй…ҚзҪ®' }}
        </el-button>
        
        <el-button 
          type="info" 
          size="large"
          @click="refreshIpInfo"
          :loading="loading"
          style="margin-left: 10px;"
        >
          <el-icon><Refresh /></el-icon>
          еҲ·ж–°дҝЎжҒҜ
        </el-button>
      </div>
      
      <!-- жӣҙж–°з»“жһңеұ•зӨә -->
      <el-card v-if="updateResult" class="result-card" style="margin-top: 20px;">
        <template #header>
          <div class="result-header">
            <el-icon :class="updateResult.success ? 'success-icon' : 'error-icon'">
              <component :is="updateResult.success ? 'CircleCheck' : 'CircleClose'" />
            </el-icon>
            <span>{{ updateResult.success ? 'жӣҙж–°жҲҗеҠҹ' : 'жӣҙж–°еӨұиҙҘ' }}</span>
          </div>
        </template>
        
        <div class="result-content">
          <p><strong>ж–°IPең°еқҖ:</strong> {{ updateResult.new_ip }}</p>
          <p v-if="updateResult.message"><strong>ж¶ҲжҒҜ:</strong> {{ updateResult.message }}</p>
          
          <div v-if="updateResult.restart_results && updateResult.restart_results.length > 0" style="margin-top: 15px;">
            <p><strong>жңҚеҠЎйҮҚеҗҜзҠ¶жҖ?</strong></p>
            <ul style="margin-left: 20px;">
              <li v-for="(result, index) in updateResult.restart_results" :key="index">
                {{ result.service }}: 
                <el-tag 
                  :type="result.status === 'restarted' ? 'success' : 'danger'" 
                  size="small"
                >
                  {{ result.status }}
                </el-tag>
                <span v-if="result.error" style="color: #f56c6c; margin-left: 10px;">
                  {{ result.error }}
                </span>
              </li>
            </ul>
          </div>
          
          <div v-if="updateResult.script_output" style="margin-top: 15px;">
            <p><strong>и„ҡжң¬иҫ“еҮә:</strong></p>
            <pre class="script-output">{{ updateResult.script_output }}</pre>
          </div>
        </div>
      </el-card>
    </el-card>
  </div>
</template>

<script setup>
// зі»з»ҹй…ҚзҪ®йҖ»иҫ‘пјҲSystem configuration logicпј?
// ж ёеҝғжөҒзЁӢпј?
// 1) refreshIpInfo: иҜ»еҸ–еҪ“еүҚжЈҖжөӢеҲ°зҡ„жңҚеҠЎеҷЁ IP дёҺе·Ідҝқеӯҳй…ҚзҪ®пј?
// 2) updateIp:      з”ЁжҲ·зЎ®и®ӨеҗҺпјҢе°ҶеҪ“еү?IP еҶҷе…Ҙй…ҚзҪ®е№¶йҮҚеҗҜзӣёе…іжңҚеҠЎпјӣ
// 3) йҖҡиҝҮ updateResult еҗ‘з”ЁжҲ·еҸҚйҰҲи„ҡжң¬жү§иЎҢз»“жһңд»ҘеҸҠеҗ„дёӘжңҚеҠЎзҡ„йҮҚеҗҜзҠ¶жҖҒгҖ?
import { ref, onMounted } from 'vue'
import axios from 'axios'
import { ElMessage, ElMessageBox } from 'element-plus'
import { Refresh, Setting, CircleCheck, CircleClose } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'

const ipInfo = ref({
  current_ip: '',
  configured_ip: '',
  needs_update: false
})

const loading = ref(false)
const updating = ref(false)
const updateResult = ref(null)

const refreshIpInfo = async () => {
  loading.value = true
  try {
    const response = await axios.get('/api/v1/system/config')
    ipInfo.value = {
      current_ip: response.data.current_ip || '',
      configured_ip: response.data.configured_ip || '',
      needs_update: response.data.needs_update || false
    }
  } catch (error) {
    ElMessage.error('иҺ·еҸ–IPдҝЎжҒҜеӨұиҙҘ: ' + (error.response?.data?.detail || error.message))
  } finally {
    loading.value = false
  }
}

const updateIp = async () => {
  try {
    await ElMessageBox.confirm(
      `зЎ®е®ҡиҰҒе°Ҷй…ҚзҪ®зҡ„IPең°еқҖжӣҙж–°дё?${ipInfo.value.current_ip} еҗ—пјҹ\n\nиҝҷе°Ҷпјҡ\n1. жӣҙж–°.envж–Үд»¶дёӯзҡ„SERVER_IP\n2. жӣҙж–°nginxгҖҒchat-serviceзӯүй…ҚзҪ®ж–Үд»¶\n3. йҮҚеҗҜзӣёе…іDockerжңҚеҠЎпјҲarbore-flowгҖҒarbore-nginxпјү`,
      'зЎ®и®Өжӣҙж–°IPй…ҚзҪ®',
      {
        confirmButtonText: 'зЎ®е®ҡ',
        cancelButtonText: 'еҸ–ж¶Ҳ',
        type: 'warning',
      }
    )
    
    updating.value = true
    updateResult.value = null
    
    try {
      const response = await axios.post('/api/v1/system/config/update-ip')
      updateResult.value = response.data
      
      if (response.data.success) {
        ElMessage.success(response.data.message || 'IPй…ҚзҪ®жӣҙж–°жҲҗеҠҹ')
        // еҲ·ж–°IPдҝЎжҒҜ
        await refreshIpInfo()
      } else {
        ElMessage.error('IPй…ҚзҪ®жӣҙж–°еӨұиҙҘ')
      }
    } catch (error) {
      const errorDetail = error.response?.data?.detail || error.message
      updateResult.value = {
        success: false,
        error: errorDetail
      }
      ElMessage.error('жӣҙж–°IPй…ҚзҪ®еӨұиҙҘ: ' + errorDetail)
    }
  } catch (error) {
    // з”ЁжҲ·еҸ–ж¶Ҳ
    if (error !== 'cancel') {
      ElMessage.error('ж“ҚдҪңеӨұиҙҘ: ' + error.message)
    }
  } finally {
    updating.value = false
  }
}

onMounted(() => {
  refreshIpInfo()
})
</script>

// Arbore Web Admin еүҚз«Ҝе…ҘеҸЈж–Үд»¶
// Arbore Web Admin Frontend Bootstrap Entry
//
// жң¬ж–Үд»¶иҙҹиҙЈеҲӣе»?Vue еә”з”Ёе®һдҫӢгҖҒжҢӮиҪҪе…ЁеұҖ UI з»„д»¶еә“д»ҘеҸҠз»ҹдёҖзҡ„е“ҒзүҢж ·ејҸдё»йўҳгҖ?
// иҝҷйҮҢзҡ„еҲқе§ӢеҢ–жөҒзЁӢзӣёеҜ№зЁіе®ҡпјҢеңЁеҗҺз»ӯзүҲжң¬жј”иҝӣдёӯдё»иҰҒд»ҘвҖңеҸҜй…ҚзҪ®вҖқгҖҒвҖңеҸҜжү©еұ•вҖқдёәзӣ®ж Үпј?
//   1) еҰӮжһңжңӘжқҘжңүеӨҡиҜӯиЁҖж”ҜжҢҒпјҢеҸҜеңЁиҝҷйҮҢжҢӮиҪ?i18n жҸ’д»¶пј?
//   2) еҰӮжһңйңҖиҰҒе…ЁеұҖзҠ¶жҖҒз®ЎзҗҶпјҢеҸҜеңЁиҝҷйҮҢеј•е…Ҙ Pinia жҲ?Vuexпј?
//   3) еҰӮжһңиҰҒжӢ“еұ•жӣҙеӨҡе…ЁеұҖжҢҮд»Ө / з»„д»¶пјҢеҗҢж ·е»әи®®еңЁжӯӨйӣҶдёӯжіЁеҶҢгҖ?
//
// This file is the single bootstrap point for the Vue application.  It wires
// up Element Plus (the UI library), global icon components and the dark themed
// Arbore brand stylesheet, then mounts the root `App` component into the DOM.
// The code is intentionally small but heavily documented so that maintainers
// can quickly understand where to plug new capabilities into the frontend.
// ============================================================================

import { createApp } from 'vue'
import ElementPlus from 'element-plus'
import 'element-plus/dist/index.css'
import 'element-plus/theme-chalk/dark/css-vars.css'
import './styles/arbore-theme.css'
import * as ElementPlusIconsVue from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
import App from './App.vue'

const app = createApp(App)

// жіЁеҶҢ Element Plus еӣҫж ҮпјҲRegister all Element Plus icons globallyпј?
// иҝҷж ·еңЁд»»ж„Ҹз»„д»¶дёӯйғҪеҸҜд»ҘйҖҡиҝҮ <IconName /> зҡ„ж–№ејҸзӣҙжҺҘдҪҝз”ЁпјҢж— йңҖйҮҚеӨҚеҜје…ҘгҖ?
for (const [key, component] of Object.entries(ElementPlusIconsVue)) {
  app.component(key, component)
}

// й…ҚзҪ® Element Plus дё»йўҳиүІпјҲArbore е“ҒзүҢиүІеҚ дҪҚпјү
// Configure Element Plus theme (placeholder for Arbore brand palette).
// зӣ®еүҚд»…з®ҖеҚ•еҗҜз”Ёз»„д»¶еә“пјҢеҗҺз»ӯеҰӮйңҖзІҫз»ҶеҢ–дё»йўҳе®ҡеҲ¶пјҢеҸҜд»ҘеңЁжӯӨеҜ№иұЎдёӯеўһеҠ?
// е…ЁеұҖе°әеҜёгҖҒеңҶи§’гҖҒдё»иүІзӯүеҸӮж•°гҖ?
app.use(ElementPlus, {
  // еҸҜд»ҘеңЁиҝҷйҮҢй…ҚзҪ®дё»йў?
})

app.mount('#app')
